# cs.CL [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Phase transition on a context-sensitive random language model with short range interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00947)
*Yuma Toji,Jun Takahashi,Vwani Roychowdhury,Hideyuki Miyahara*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究构建了一个具有短程相互作用（short-range interactions）的随机语言模型（random language model），发现即使仅参考长度不随句子长度变化的上下文，模型仍会发生相变（phase transition），表明语言模型的有限温度相变源于语言的内在本质而非长程相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究表明，具有长程相互作用（long-range interactions）的语言模型存在Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless相变，但统计力学中已知长程相互作用本身就能诱导相变。因此需要澄清语言模型中的相变是否源于真正语言特性而非长程相互作用效应。

Method: 构建了一个具有短程相互作用的随机语言模型，该模型属于乔姆斯基层次结构（Chomsky hierarchy）中的上下文敏感文法（context-sensitive grammars）类别，允许显式参考上下文。数值研究了其统计特性，特别关注仅参考长度不随句子长度变化的上下文的情况。

Result: 研究发现，即使模型仅参考长度恒定的上下文（不随句子长度变化），仍会发生相变。这一结果表明语言模型的有限温度相变确实由语言内在本质诱导，而非长程相互作用所致。

Conclusion: 语言模型中的有限温度相变源于语言的内在特性，而非长程相互作用效应。该发现为从统计力学角度理解语言模型提供了更坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: Since the random language model was proposed by E. DeGiuli [Phys. Rev. Lett. 122, 128301], language models have been investigated intensively from the viewpoint of statistical mechanics. Recently, the existence of a Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless transition was numerically demonstrated in models with long-range interactions between symbols. In statistical mechanics, it has long been known that long-range interactions can induce phase transitions. Therefore, it has remained unclear whether phase transitions observed in language models originate from genuinely linguistic properties that are absent in conventional spin models. In this study, we construct a random language model with short-range interactions and numerically investigate its statistical properties. Our model belongs to the class of context-sensitive grammars in the Chomsky hierarchy and allows explicit reference to contexts. We find that a phase transition occurs even when the model refers only to contexts whose length remains constant with respect to the sentence length. This result indicates that finite-temperature phase transitions in language models are genuinely induced by the intrinsic nature of language, rather than by long-range interactions.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.dis-nn'></div>

# cond-mat.dis-nn [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Soft vector spins with dimensional annealing for combinatorial optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01003)
*Marvin Syed,Richard Zhipeng Wang,Natalia G. Berloff*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于矢量自旋（vector spins）的软模型，通过多维矢量自由度增强伊辛模型（Ising model）基态搜索能力，并展示了三种维度退火方法在多种基准问题上的优越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，专为高效最小化伊辛能量（Ising energy）而设计的模拟硬件受到广泛关注。本研究旨在探索如何利用此类硬件中自然存在或人工创建的多维矢量自由度（vectorial degrees of freedom），以增强解决优化问题的能力。

Method: 引入了一种可在多种模拟硬件平台上实现的软矢量自旋（soft vector spins）模型，并提出了三种维度退火方法（dimensional annealing methods），这些方法利用矢量自由度扩大的相空间来最小化伊辛能量。

Result: 在不同基准问题上的模拟表明，所有测试的维度退火方法中，矢量自由度相比一维自由度在寻找伊辛模型基态方面均有改进。当维度 $d \gtrsim 3$ 时优势最为显著，但维度继续增加时收益递减。

Conclusion: 研究结果可为新型模拟优化硬件和算法提供启发，这些硬件和算法应明确纳入矢量自由度的优势，以提升组合优化问题的求解能力。

Abstract: Recently, purpose-built analog hardware that can efficiently minimize the Ising energy and thereby solve a variety of combinatorial optimization problems has been receiving widespread attention. In this work, we show how multidimensional, vectorial degrees of freedom, that are either naturally present or can be artificially created in such hardware, could strengthen the capability to find optimal solutions to optimization problems. In order to achieve this, we introduce a simple model of soft vector spins that should be implementable on a variety of analog hardware platforms as well as three different dimensional annealing methods which harness the enlarged phase space of the vectorial degrees of freedom to minimize the Ising energy. We perform simulations on different benchmark problems and show that for all dimensional annealing methods we tested, vectorial degrees of freedom improve upon one-dimensional degrees of freedom when it comes to finding the ground state of the Ising model. In particular, we find that this advantage becomes most pronounced for $d \gtrsim 3$ dimensional degrees of freedom, with diminishing returns as the dimension is increased further. Our results could inspire new analog optimization hardware and algorithms that explicitly incorporate the advantage of vectorial degrees of freedom.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.HE'></div>

# astro-ph.HE [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [A Novel Method to Construct Frequency-Domain Gravitational Waveform for Accelerating Sources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00253)
*Xinmiao Zhao,Han Yan,Xian Chen*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出频率域谱微分（FSD）方法，用于在引力波信号的整个并合-环落（inspiral-merger-ringdown）阶段更自洽地处理天体物理环境效应，相比传统的平稳相位近似（SPA）和后牛顿（PN）形式，FSD能更准确地模拟加速源的信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确模拟致密天体并合信号的并合-环落（IMR）阶段对于检验广义相对论至关重要。然而，天体物理环境会扭曲引力波（GW）信号，若忽略这些效应可能导致参数估计偏差甚至对引力的理解错误。传统基于平稳相位近似（SPA）和后牛顿（PN）形式的方法在最终并合-环落阶段与快速轨道演化和强引力场不一致。

Method: 本文引入频率域谱微分（frequency-domain spectral differentiation, FSD）方法，该方法将加速度引起的时间偏移映射到频域中的微分运算。这种映射不依赖于SPA或PN形式，因此可用于构建跨越整个IMR阶段的加速波形。

Result: FSD波形与传统SPA+PN波形比较显示，前者能更准确地匹配加速源的模拟信号，特别是在并合-环落阶段且包含高阶FSD修正时。费舍尔信息矩阵（Fisher information matrix）分析表明，FSD波形在测量有效加速度方面能达到比SPA+PN波形更高的精度。

Conclusion: FSD方法为双星引力波源最终并合-环落阶段的各种天体物理环境效应提供了更自洽的处理方式，克服了传统方法在强引力场和快速轨道演化情况下的局限性。

Abstract: Accurately modeling the inspiral-merger-ringdown (IMR) signal of coalescing compact objects is essential for the test of general relativity. However, it is known that astrophysical environments can distort gravitational-wave (GW) signal and, if ignored, may bias parameter estimation or even our understanding of gravity. Previous studies suggest that various astrophysical environmental effects can be modeled in a unified way by introducing an effective acceleration. However, such models are based on stationary phase approximation (SPA) and post-Newtonian (PN) formalism, which are inconsistent with the fast orbital evolution and strong gravity in the final merger-ringdown phase. To overcome this limit, we introduce frequency-domain spectral differentiation (FSD), which maps the time shift of the signal caused by acceleration into a differentiation in the frequency domain. The mapping does not rely on SPA or PN formalism, therefore can be used to construct the accelerated waveform across the entire IMR phases. We compare the FSD waveforms with the conventional SPA+PN ones, and find that the former more faithfully match the simulated signals of accelerating sources, especially in the merger-ringdown phase and when higher-order FSD corrections are included. A Fisher information matrix analysis suggests that FSD waveforms can achieve higher precision than SPA+PN waveforms in measuring effective acceleration. Therefore, the FSD method offers a more self-consistent treatment of various astrophysical environmental effects in the final merger-ringdown phase of binary GW sources.

</details>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Model for the curvature response of the CDF II drift chamber](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00318)
*Ashutosh Vijay Kotwal*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: CDF II实验利用漂移室测量带电粒子动量，本文提出轨迹曲率响应模型，参数约束来自宇宙射线数据和W玻色子质量测量信息，验证了校准程序的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为精确测量带电粒子动量，需要建立漂移室对带电粒子轨迹曲率的响应模型，以改进CDF II实验中动量测量的校准精度。

Method: 提出漂移室对带电粒子轨迹曲率的响应模型，利用宇宙射线数据和CDF在W玻色子质量测量中发布的信息对模型参数进行约束。

Result: 模型为高动量粒子精密磁径迹分析提供了框架，验证了CDF校准程序的鲁棒性，并讨论了漂移室动量测量校准的影响。

Conclusion: 该响应模型为高动量粒子精密磁径迹分析提供了有效框架，证明了CDF校准方法的稳健性，对类似实验的动量测量校准具有参考价值。

Abstract: The CDF II experiment at the Fermilab Tevatron used a drift chamber to measure the momenta of charged particles. We present a model for the response of the drift chamber to the curvature of a charged particle's trajectory. Constraints on the model parameters are obtained from cosmic-ray data and from information published by CDF in the context of the W boson mass measurement. Implications for the calibration of the drift chamber measurement of momentum are discussed. The robustness of the CDF calibration procedure is demonstrated. The model provides a framework for the analysis of precision magnetic trackers of high-momentum particles.

</details>


### [5] [Joint LHCb--Belle II Prospects to Constrain New Physics in $B\to D^{(*)}τν$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00735)
*Johannes Albrecht,Florian Bernlochner,Marco Colonna,Lorenz Gärtner,Abhijit Mathad,Biljana Mitreska,Markus Prim,Ilias Tsaklidis*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究提出了在有效场论框架下，通过联合分析LHCb和Belle II实验的$\bar{B}\to D^{(*)}τ\barν_τ$衰变数据，优化威尔逊系数（Wilson coefficients）提取的策略。采用事件级别重加权技术避免重复模拟，并通过同时拟合（simultaneous fit）减少模型偏差，提高对非标准模型效应的探测灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半轻子衰变$b\to cτ\barν_τ$是探测非标准模型效应的有力探针，但需要最大化数据灵敏度同时控制标准模型建模偏差。不同实验间的理论输入（如形状因子参数）存在相关性，需要一致处理以充分利用当前和未来的实验数据。

Method: 研究采用事件级别重加权（event-by-event reweighting）技术，将模拟样本映射到任意威尔逊系数组合，避免为每个有效场论假设重复大规模探测器模拟。通过同时拟合（simultaneous fit）多个$\bar{B}\to D^{(*)}τ\barν_τ$通道和数据集，共享威尔逊系数和共同的形状因子参数。

Result: 同时拟合相比独立拟合减少了模型诱导的偏差，提高了灵敏度。该方法为利用LHCb和Belle II即将到来的数据集，在$b\to cτ\barν_τ$跃迁中实现精确有效场论约束提供了稳健且可扩展的策略。

Conclusion: 通过联合分析LHCb和Belle II实验配置，共享威尔逊系数和共同形状因子参数的同时拟合方法，能够有效控制标准模型建模偏差，提高对非标准模型效应的探测能力，为未来高精度有效场论约束提供了可靠框架。

Abstract: Semileptonic $b\to cτ\barν_τ$ decays are powerful probes of non-Standard-Model effects within an effective-field-theory (EFT) framework, but fully exploiting them in current and future data demands combinations that maximise sensitivity while controlling biases from Standard-Model-based modelling and from theory inputs that are shared, and therefore correlated, across analyses in different experiments. We present a first sensitivity study of a combined extraction of Wilson coefficients in $\bar{B}\to D^{(*)}τ\barν_τ$ decays using LHCb- and Belle~II-like analysis configurations. Detector simulations for signal and backgrounds are typically generated under Standard Model assumptions; if non-SM contributions are present, this can bias the fitted Wilson coefficients. In addition, hadronic inputs such as form-factor parameters of signal and background components are common across analyses, requiring a consistent treatment of fully correlated effects in combinations. To avoid repeating large-scale detector simulation for each EFT hypothesis, we use event-by-event reweighting to map simulated samples to arbitrary combinations of Wilson coefficients. We then compare a simultaneous fit across multiple $\bar{B}\to D^{(*)}τ\barν_τ$ channels and datasets with a combination based on post-fit averages. Sharing Wilson coefficients and common form-factor parameters in the simultaneous fit reduces model-induced biases and improves sensitivity relative to independent fits, providing a robust and scalable strategy for precision EFT constraints in $b\to cτ\barν_τ$ transitions using forthcoming LHCb and Belle~II datasets.

</details>


### [6] [Potassium-40 geoneutrinos detection and the Earth's large-scale structures imaging by directional geoneutrino detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00808)
*Haozhe Sun,Zhe Wang,Shaomin Chen*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种利用切伦科夫液体闪烁体进行中微子方向性探测的地球中微子（geoneutrino）探测方法，旨在通过中微子-电子弹性散射探测地球内部放射性元素产生的电子（反）中微子，并研究其对地球内部化学组成和大尺度结构的探测潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地球中微子（geoneutrinos）作为地球内部放射性元素衰变产生的电子（反）中微子，是探测地球内部化学组成的独特探针。本研究旨在开发一种方向性地球中微子探测方法，以更好地理解地球内部结构。

Method: 采用切伦科夫液体闪烁体（Cherenkov liquid scintillator）进行中微子方向性探测，利用中微子-电子弹性散射（neutrino-electron elastic scattering）机制。通过优化太阳角切割（solar angle cut）抑制太阳中微子本底，并基于先前测量和模拟研究中微子方向重建分辨率。

Result: 研究发现，发现钾中微子（potassium neutrinos）的3σ灵敏度为2.8千吨-年（kiloton-years）。拒绝均匀地球中微子分布的3σ置信度所需曝光量为10.6千吨-年，表明该方法具有探测地球大尺度非均匀结构的能力。

Conclusion: 方向性地球中微子探测方法具有探测地球内部化学组成和大尺度结构的潜力，为地球物理学研究提供了新的观测手段，特别是对钾、铀、钍等放射性元素分布的探测能力。

Abstract: Geoneutrinos, the electron (anti)neutrinos generated in decays or decay chains of the radioactive elements within the Earth, primarily K-40, U-238, and Th-232, serve as a unique probe for the inner chemical composition of the Earth. A directional geoneutrino detection method with a Cherenkov liquid scintillator is investigated in this work. The neutrino-electron elastic scattering in the scintillator is employed to detect geoneutrinos. The direction reconstruction resolution for neutrinos is studied based on previous measurements and simulations. The intrinsic neutrino background from the Sun is suppressed with an optimized solar angle cut. The 3 sigma sensitivity to discover the potassium neutrinos is 2.8 kiloton-years. The potential to reach a non-uniform geoneutrino image with the Earth's large-scale structures is also studied. The required exposure is 10.6 kiloton-years to reject a uniform geoneutrino distribution by 3 sigma.

</details>


### [7] [Sensitivity study of $\bar{K}_1(1270)$ decay dynamics using four $D\to \bar{K}_1(1270)(\to \bar Kππ)e^+ν$ decay channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00859)
*Ying'ao Tang,Liang Sun,Panting Ge,Menghao Wang*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究利用半轻子D介子衰变对$\bar{K}_1(1270)$衰变模式的测量进行灵敏度分析，以BESIII实验为案例，提出了模型无关的$\bar{K}_1(1270)\to \bar Kππ$分支比测量方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过半轻子D介子衰变对$\bar{K}_1(1270)$的衰变模式进行灵敏度分析，特别关注BESIII实验环境下的测量可行性。

Method: 采用半轻子D介子衰变作为分析框架，同时对$\bar{K}_1(1270)$衰变到四个三体末态$K^-π^+π^-$、$K^-π^+π^0$、$K_S^0π^+π^-$和$K_S^0π^-π^0$进行联合分析，提出模型无关的测量方法。

Result: 研究展示了在BESIII实验环境下对$\bar{K}_1(1270)$衰变模式的联合分析方案，并提出了不依赖中间共振态详细知识的模型无关分支比测量方法。

Conclusion: 该研究为$\bar{K}_1(1270)\to \bar Kππ$衰变分支比的精确测量提供了一种模型无关的新方法，特别适用于BESIII实验环境，避免了传统方法中对中间共振态贡献的详细知识依赖。

Abstract: A sensitivity study for the measurement of $\bar{K}_1(1270)$ decay modes is performed using semileptonic $D$-meson decays. The BESIII experiment is taken as a case study, where a simultaneous analysis of $\bar{K}_1(1270)$ decays to the four thee-body final states $K^-π^+π^-$, $K^-π^+π^0$, $K_S^0π^+π^-$, and $K_S^0π^-π^0$ is presented and a model-independent determination of \mbox{$\mathcal{B}(\bar{K}_1(1270)\to \bar Kππ)$}, without requiring detailed knowledge of intermediate resonant contributions, is proposed.

</details>


### [8] [Site-specific ILC Detector Installation Plan](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00906)
*Karsten Buesser,Thomas Schoerner*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文讨论了ILC（International Linear Collider）探测器概念ILD和SiD的组装与安装规划，强调这些复杂程序需要细致的物流安排，并指出当前计划仍需根据具体场地条件进一步细化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ILC探测器概念ILD和SiD是极其复杂的装置，其在实验洞穴（experimental cavern）的组装与安装面临诸多挑战。这些程序需要周密的规划与物流安排，考虑众多约束条件和边界条件。

Method: 文档描述了ILD和SiD探测器安装过程中的约束条件与边界条件。特别地，ILD已经投入大量精力制定了详细的安装计划，这些计划将在文档中简要概述。

Result: 由于ILC尚未成为确定项目，且最终相互作用点（interaction point）尚未选定，所有安装计划目前均为初步方案。这些计划需要根据具体的场地特定（site-specific）和项目特定（project-specific）条件进一步细化。

Conclusion: ILC探测器安装规划仍处于初步阶段，需要根据项目最终确定后的具体条件进行详细设计。当前计划为后续工作提供了基础框架，但需保持灵活性以适应未来变化。

Abstract: Both ILC detector concepts, ILD and SiD, are very complex machines, the assembly and installation of which in the experimental cavern at the ILC interaction point will be complicated endeavours. These procedures require careful planning and logistics, taking into account numerous constraints and boundary conditions. Some of these are described in this document. Especially ILD has already invested significant effort into elaborate installation plans, which will be briefly described in this document. However, with the ILC not being a secured project and a final interaction point not chosen, all these plans have to be considered preliminary and need to be further detailed, taking into account the concrete site-specific and project-specific conditions.

</details>


### [9] [Blobel's Regularized Unfolding: Eigenmode Decomposition and Automatic Smoothing for Inverse Problems in Particle Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01069)
*Vincent Alexander Croft*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文系统阐述了基于三次B样条表示和特征模式滤波的正则化反卷积方法，该方法被称为Blobel正则化反卷积（BRU），通过样条系数参数化平滑函数表示真实分布，并采用基于统计精度的曲率惩罚特征模式分解进行正则化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在提供Blobel正则化反卷积（BRU）方法的自包含处理，该方法与传统的基于直方图的反卷积方法不同，通过平滑函数参数化表示真实分布，并实现正则化强度的自动确定。

Method: 该方法基于三次B样条（cubic B-spline）表示和特征模式滤波（eigenmode filtering），将真实分布表示为样条系数参数化的平滑函数，正则化通过曲率惩罚相对于统计精度的特征模式分解实现，正则化强度可从数据中自动确定。

Result: 文档描述了该方法的数学结构，提供了正则化强度自动确定机制，并与标准方法进行了详细比较，包括基于Tikhonov正则化的方法、Richardson-Lucy迭代和朴素矩阵反演。

Conclusion: Blobel正则化反卷积（BRU）方法提供了一种系统化的正则化反卷积框架，通过样条表示和特征模式分解实现了与传统直方图方法不同的反卷积策略，并具备正则化参数自动确定的能力。

Abstract: This document presents a self-contained treatment of regularized unfolding based on cubic B-spline representations and eigenmode filtering, following the original formulation by Blobel and direct translation of the original implementation in Fortran into a modern format. The method, which has been called by several names under its various historical representations, is named here as Blobel's Regularised Unfolding (BRU). This method differs from conventional histogram-based unfolding approaches in that the true distribution is represented as a smooth function parametrised by spline coefficients, and the regularization operates through an eigenmode decomposition of the curvature penalty relative to the statistical precision. This document describes the mathematical structure of the method, the mechanism by which the regularisation strength is determined automatically from the data, and provides a detailed comparison with standard methods including Tikhonov regularisation based methods, Richardson-Lucy iteration, and naive matrix inversion.

</details>

### [10] [Large deviations of the periodic Toda chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00635)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在为周期性Toda链在广义吉布斯系综统计下的动力学关联函数计算热力学极限铺平道路。通过建立谱测度的大偏差原理，为理解系统在广义吉布斯系综下的统计性质提供理论基础。

Method: 研究证明了周期性Toda链Lax矩阵谱测度的大偏差原理，该原理适用于动量约束为零和动量允许涨落两种情况。证明直接基于实现经典变量分离的变量表示的广义吉布斯配分函数。

Result: 建立了受广义吉布斯测度约束的周期性Toda链Lax矩阵谱测度的大偏差原理，其速率函数可视为系统自由能的推广。该原理在两种动量条件下均成立，并基于变量分离表示直接证明。

Conclusion: 该工作为计算广义吉布斯系综统计下Toda链动力学关联函数的热力学极限奠定了基础，通过建立谱测度的大偏差原理，为系统在广义吉布斯系综下的统计力学分析提供了关键工具。

Abstract: This work establishes a large deviation principle for the spectral measure of the Lax matrix associated to the periodic Toda chain of $N$ particles, subject to a generalised Gibbs measure. This large deviation principle is governed by a rate function which can be regarded as a generalisation of the free energy of the system. Such a large deviation principle is proven both for the model when the momentum is constrained to be zero and when it is allowed to fluctuate. Moreover, the large deviation principle is proven directly on the level of the representation of the generalised Gibbs partition function given in terms of the variables realising the classical separation of variables, \textit{i.e.} rectify the equations of motion. As such, this work paves the way towards the computation of the thermodynamic limit of dynamical correlation functions in the Toda chain subject to generalised Gibbs ensemble statistics.

### [11] [One-loop $p$-adic string theory and the Néron local height function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00970)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索p-adic弦理论中世界面作用量在几何结构不同描述之间的对应关系，特别是Bruhat-Tits树的商空间与其渐近边界Tate曲线之间的对偶性。

Method: 通过考虑$PGL(2,\mathbb{Q}_p)$的Bruhat-Tits树在亏格1Schottky群作用下的商空间，并在其渐近边界Tate曲线$\mathbb{Q}_p^\ast/q^\mathbb{Z}$上构造对偶描述。

Result: 证明了对偶作用量的两点函数与Tate曲线的Néron-Tate局部高度函数完全一致，建立了p-adic弦理论与算术几何之间的精确对应关系。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了p-adic弦世界面作用量的几何描述与算术几何中高度函数理论之间的深刻联系，为理解p-adic弦理论的数学结构提供了新视角。

Abstract: The $p$-adic string worldsheet action on the quotient of the Bruhat-Tits tree of $PGL(2,\mathbb{Q}_p)$ by a genus 1 Schottky group has a dual description on the asymptotic boundary, the Tate curve $\mathbb{Q}_p^\ast/q^\mathbb{Z}$. We show that the two point function of the dual action coincides with the Néron-Tate local height function of the Tate curve.

### [12] [Solutions of Calabi-Yau Differential Operators as Truncated p-adic Series and Efficient Computation of Zeta Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01191)
*Pyry Kuusela,Michael Lathwood,Miroslava Mosso Rojas,Michael Stepniczka*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 本文提出一种称为"p-adically truncated recurrence"的新方法，通过使用模p^A的p-adic数解递推关系，显著提高了Calabi-Yau三维流形局部zeta函数的计算效率，使计算范围从约1000个素数扩展到数万个素数，甚至可处理10^6到10^7量级的大素数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有变形方法（deformation method）在计算Calabi-Yau三维流形的局部zeta函数（local zeta functions）时，随着素数p增大，有理周期系数（rational period coefficients）快速增长导致计算效率急剧下降，通常仅能处理约1000个素数。

Method: 提出"p-adically truncated recurrence"方法，其解为模p^A的p-adic数，其中A∈ℕ。通过选择适当的p-adic精度A，保留所有对最终结果有贡献的p-adic数字，从而避免有理系数快速增长问题。

Result: 该方法显著提升了计算速度和内存使用效率，使在桌面计算机上计算数万个素数的局部zeta函数成为可能，甚至可处理10^6到10^7量级的大素数。已实现为Sage兼容的Python包PFLFunction。

Conclusion: p-adically truncated recurrence方法有效解决了原有变形方法在大素数下的效率瓶颈，将局部zeta函数的计算能力扩展了数个数量级，为相关数论和几何研究提供了更强大的计算工具。

Abstract: Recently, a version of the deformation method developed in arXiv:2104.07816 has been used to great effect to compute the local zeta functions of Calabi-Yau threefolds by computing their periods as series with rational coefficients and using this to find a matrix representing the Frobenius action on a $p$-adic cohomology. However, this method rapidly becomes inefficient as the prime $p$ grows, due to the rational period coefficients growing quickly. In this paper, we point out that this problem can be circumvented by a simple process that we call $p$-adically truncated recurrence. This is a recurrence relation whose solutions are $p$-adic numbers modulo $p^A$ for a given $A \in \mathbb{N}$ and thus grow only slowly as $p$ grows. We show that the $p$-adic accuracy $A$ can be chosen such that all $p$-adic digits which contribute to the final result are kept, and therefore we are able to obtain the correct result by using these solutions. The improvements to speed and memory usage allow for computing the local zeta functions for tens of thousands of primes on a desktop computer, and make computing local zeta functions possible even for primes of size $10^6$ to $10^7$. Previously such computations were practically possible for around 1000 first primes. We have implemented this method in a Sage-compatible Python package PFLFunction.

</details>

### [13] [Applications of renormalisation to orthonormal Strichartz estimates and the NLS system on the circle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00252)
*Sonae Hadama,Andrew Rout*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对圆环上的非线性薛定谔方程组（NLSS）引入密度重整化（renormalisation）程序，证明重整化密度比非重整化密度满足更好的正交Strichartz估计，并应用于确定三次重整化NLSS的临界Schatten指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于改进圆环上非线性薛定谔方程组（nonlinear Schrödinger equations, NLSS）密度相关的正交Strichartz估计。先前Nakamura (2020)考虑的非重整化密度存在估计限制，需要引入重整化程序以获得更好的估计结果。

Method: 方法核心是引入密度重整化（renormalisation）程序，特别针对圆环上的非线性薛定谔方程组。通过重整化处理密度，分析其满足的正交Strichartz估计（orthonormal Strichartz estimates）性质，并与非重整化情况进行比较。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）重整化密度比非重整化密度满足更好的正交Strichartz估计；2）确定了三次重整化NLSS的临界Schatten指数，该指数区分了全局适定性（global well-posedness）和不适定性（ill-posedness）；3）对于d≥2维环面𝕋^d，重整化密度带来的正交Strichartz估计改进是最小的。

Conclusion: 结论表明密度重整化程序能有效改进圆环上NLSS的正交Strichartz估计，但高维情况下改进有限。最优Strichartz估计指数范围作为猜想提出，为后续研究提供方向。

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce a renormalisation procedure for the density associated with the system of nonlinear Schrödinger equations (NLSS) on a circle. We show that this renormalised density satisfies better orthonormal Strichartz estimates than the non-renormalised density, which was considered in Nakamura (2020). We leave as a conjecture the optimal range of exponents for these Strichartz estimates. As an application, we determine the critical Schatten exponent below which the cubic renormalised NLSS on the circle is globally well-posed and above which it is ill-posed. Finally, we show that the improvement for orthonormal Strichartz estimates satisfied by the renormalised density on $\mathbb{T}^d$ for $d \geq 2$ is minimal.

</details>

### [14] [An All-Loop Amplituhedron in Two Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00083)
*Jonah Stalknecht*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文定义并研究了二维闵可夫斯基空间中的正几何$Δ^{(L)}$，作为环幅面体（loop amplituhedra）的自然推广。该几何对应无质量香蕉图（massless banana graphs）的正则形式，其红外发散结构呈现指数化现象，可重整为Fox-Wright函数，并在大环数极限下涌现世界线路径积分描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将环幅面体（loop amplituhedra）的概念推广到二维闵可夫斯基空间$\mathbb{R}^{1,1}$，为探索环振幅的几何结构提供一个简单且可处理的设定。这为在标准范围之外研究环幅面体提供了一个可控的玩具模型。

Method: 方法基于对偶动量空间中的光锥几何（lightcone geometries）框架，定义并研究正几何$Δ^{(L)}$。该几何也可等价地作为$\mathcal{N}=4$超杨-米尔斯理论中$L$-环幅面体的特定边界获得。利用二维设定的简单性，计算任意环阶的正则形式（canonical form）。

Result: 结果显示$Δ^{(L)}$的正则形式对应无质量香蕉图（massless banana graphs）。在维度正规化（dimensional regularization）下对所有环阶进行积分，发现完整的红外发散结构由单环结果的$L$次幂捕获，类似于红外指数化（IR exponentiation）现象。这些积分函数可重整为Fox-Wright函数的闭式非微扰结果。

Conclusion: 当$L\to\infty$时，该几何产生世界线（worldlines）上的路径积分，暗示在强耦合下会出现对偶描述。该构造为探索环振幅的几何提供了一个简单且可处理的设定，并为在标准范围之外研究环幅面体提供了可控的玩具模型。

Abstract: We define and study a positive geometry $Δ^{(L)}$ which serves as a natural generalization of loop amplituhedra to two-dimensional Minkowski space $\mathbb{R}^{1,1}$. The geometry is formulated in the framework of lightcone geometries in dual momentum space, and can equivalently be obtained as a specific boundary of the $L$-loop amplituhedron for $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang--Mills. The simplicity of the two-dimensional setting allows us to calculate the canonical form of $Δ^{(L)}$ at any loop order, which is shown to correspond to massless banana graphs. We integrate the canonical form at all loop orders in dimensional regularization, and find that the full IR divergence structure at $L$-loops is captured by the $L$th power of the one-loop result, a phenomenon analogous to IR exponentiation. Furthermore, these integrated functions can be resummed into a closed-form non-perturbative result given by a Fox--Wright function. In the limit where $L\to\infty$, the geometry gives rise to a path integral over worldlines, suggesting the emergence of a dual description at strong coupling. This construction provides a simple and tractable setting in which to explore the geometry of loop amplitudes, and offers a controlled toy model for investigating loop amplituhedra beyond their standard scope.

</details>


### [15] [Instanton condensation and a new phase of BPS black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00095)
*Jack Holden*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文分析了AdS₅×S⁵中BPS黑洞的1/16-BPS超共形指数，揭示了在小黑洞鞍点处微正则系综中的新不稳定性，这与矩阵模型描述中的瞬子凝聚相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析AdS₅×S⁵中具有相等电荷的BPS黑洞的1/16-BPS超共形指数（1/16-BPS superconformal index），旨在揭示微正则系综（microcanonical ensemble）中的新物理现象。

Method: 研究方法基于矩阵模型（matrix model）描述下的指数分析，通过瞬子凝聚（instanton condensation）现象来识别不稳定性，并将黑洞物理与场论对偶描述中的部分去禁闭相（partially deconfined phase）相联系。

Result: 研究结果发现，在半径接近但略小于"小黑洞"尺度的黑洞处存在新的不稳定性，这导致该区域出现新的主导相，并可能解决BPS相图中部分去禁闭相定位的困惑。

Conclusion: 该研究结论表明，瞬子在部分去禁闭中具有重要作用，为理解禁闭（confinement）、部分去禁闭以及全息映射下色自由度（colour degrees of freedom）的编码提供了新途径。

Abstract: We analyse the 1/16-BPS superconformal index for BPS black holes at equal charge in $AdS_5 \times S_5$, uncovering evidence for a new instability in the microcanonical ensemble along the small black hole saddle. This is indicated by instanton condensation in the matrix model description of the index. This instability occurs for black holes of radius close to, but below, the scale at which black holes become `small', and implies a new dominant phase in this region. We propose a connection to the partially deconfined phase in the field theory dual description. This would resolve recent confusion about the location of the partially deconfined phase in the BPS phase diagram and promises new avenues for understanding confinement, partial deconfinement, and the encoding of colour degrees of freedom under the holographic map. We also motivate the importance of instantons in partial deconfinement from a matrix model perspective.

### [16] [de Sitter extremal surfaces, time contours, complexifications and pseudo-entropies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00108)
*K. Narayan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了德西特时空（de Sitter）中无边界（no-boundary）极值曲面及其伪熵面积，重点分析了未来边界（future boundary）上不同子区域的几何特性，并探讨了通过解析延拓（analytic continuation）与反德西特时空（AdS）熵不等式的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在深入理解德西特时空（de Sitter）中极值曲面（extremal surfaces）的几何特性及其与伪熵（pseudo-entropy）的关系。研究基于先前工作，探索不同子区域（subregions）的极值曲面存在性及其在复时间平面（complex time plane）中的行为。

Method: 通过分析德西特时空（de Sitter）中无边界（no-boundary）极值曲面及其面积积分，研究采用复时间平面（complex time plane）中的时间轮廓（time contours）来定义极值曲面面积。特别以$dS_3$作为详细示例，并探讨了通过光射线（lightrays）将未来边界子区域映射到静态补丁（static patch）中恒定时间切片上的子区域。

Result: 对于大子区域（large subregions），存在具有透明几何解释的类时+欧几里得（timelike+Euclidean）极值曲面以及复（complex）极值曲面。对于小子区域（small subregions），情况类似于庞加莱$dS$，仅存在复极值曲面。研究发现多个具有不可区分面积的极值曲面，其时间轮廓可在复时间平面中相互变形而无阻碍，表明这些曲面在目的上是等价的。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，德西特时空（de Sitter）中复$dS$副本几何（replica geometries）之间存在等价性。这为德西特时空中多子区域和熵不等式（entropy inequalities）提供了图像，即通过解析延拓（analytic continuation）编码反德西特时空（AdS）的相应关系。

Abstract: We study no-boundary de Sitter extremal surfaces and their pseudo-entropy areas for generic subregions at the future boundary, building on previous work. For large subregions, timelike+Euclidean extremal surfaces exist with transparent geometric interpretations, as do complex ones. The situation for small subregions is analogous to Poincare $dS$ and only complex extremal surfaces exist. In general, the extremal surface area integrals are defined via time contours in the complex time plane. We find multiple extremal surfaces with indistinguishable areas whose time contours can be deformed into each other in the complex time plane without obstruction, which are equivalent for these purposes. This also suggests equivalences between complex $dS$ replica geometries. We discuss $dS_3$ as a simple example at length. This suggests a picture for multiple subregions and entropy inequalities in de Sitter, as encoding $AdS$ ones via analytic continuation. We also discuss mapping future boundary subregions and those on constant time slices in the static patch via lightrays.

</details>


### [17] [How to (Non-)Perturb a BPS Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00116)
*Alberto Castellano,Matteo Zatti*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文建立了平坦时空理论中BPS黑洞可观测量（observables）的非微扰修正（non-perturbative corrections）结构与近地平线几何中带电探针粒子（probe charged particles）性质之间的联系。通过分析AdS₂×S²背景中带电探针粒子的动力学，揭示了黑洞解（black hole solution）的物理由产生高阶导数修正（higher derivative corrections）的轻D膜态（light D-brane states）所控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解平坦时空理论中BPS黑洞可观测量非微扰修正的结构起源。具体而言，旨在探索这些修正与近地平线几何中带电探针粒子性质之间的深层联系，从而揭示黑洞物理背后的微观机制。

Method: 采用4维N=2超引力（4d N=2 supergravity）理论，包含无限塔的F项（infinite tower of F-terms），并在AdS₂×S²背景中引入带电探针膜（probe branes）。通过II型拓扑弦理论（Type II topological string theory）计算高阶算子（higher dimensional operators），并采用大体积有效的常数映射贡献（constant map contribution）进行近似。分析带电粒子的受力条件、经典轨迹及其产生的单圈有效作用量（1-loop effective action）。

Result: 简单的半经典分析（semiclassical analysis）能够定性地理解非微扰修正的结构。精确的路径积分评估（exact path integral assessment）重现了平坦时空理论的Gopakumar-Vafa积分（Gopakumar-Vafa integral），但现于黑洞吸引子几何（black hole attractor geometry）中计算。这表明完全反作用黑洞解（fully backreacted black hole solution）的物理由产生相关高阶导数修正的轻D膜态行为所控制。

Conclusion: 该研究明确展示了平坦时空BPS黑洞观测量的非微扰修正结构与近地平线几何中探针带电粒子性质之间的具体对应关系。通过将Gopakumar-Vafa积分置于黑洞吸引子几何中计算，揭示了黑洞物理如何由产生高阶导数修正的微观D膜态所主导，为理解黑洞微观结构提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We relate the structure of non-perturbative corrections to BPS black hole observables in flat-spacetime theories with certain properties of probe charged particles in the near-horizon geometry. Concretely, we consider 4d $\mathcal{N} = 2$ supergravity with an infinite tower of F-terms and probe branes in $\text{AdS}_2\times \mathbf{S}^2$ backgrounds threaded by constant electric-magnetic fields. The higher dimensional operators we pick are computed by Type II topological string theory, and we approximate them via the constant map contribution, which is valid at large volume and can be interpreted as arising from D0-branes integrated out in M-theory on a Calabi-Yau threefold times a circle. We analyze the resulting force conditions on massive particles carrying $(q_A, p^A)$ charges, their classical trajectories, and the 1-loop effective action they produce. A simple semiclassical analysis allows us to understand qualitatively the structure of the non-perturbative corrections. The exact path integral assessment then reproduces the Gopakumar--Vafa integral of the flat-spacetime theory, now evaluated in the black hole attractor geometry. Thus, we make explicit how the physics of the fully backreacted black hole solution is controlled by the behaviour of the light D-brane states which generate the relevant set of higher derivative corrections.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用后现代（postmodern）视角分析观测者角色，将定义"观测者规则"的尝试识别为元叙事（metanarrative）崩溃的表现。作者主张采用后后现代（post-postmodern）立场，接受观测者依赖与独立描述之间的不相容性。

Result: 分析表明观测者既提供又破坏微扰引力希尔伯特空间（perturbative gravitational Hilbert space），这种矛盾无法通过传统方式解决。作者提出应将这种模糊性视为量子引力基本自由度（fundamental degrees of freedom）的特征。

Abstract: Recent advances in semiclassical gravity, both in our understanding of the gravitational path integral and the algebraic structure of a gravitating subregion, rely on the presence of an observer to obtain a nontrivial Hilbert space for closed universe backgrounds. Here I examine this proposal from a postmodern lens, identifying attempts to define ``observer rules'' as manifestations of metanarrative breakdown: the observer both supplies and undermines the perturbative gravitational Hilbert space. Rather than resolving this tension, I advocate for a post-postmodern acceptance of the incompatibility between observer-dependent and observer-free descriptions of closed universes, treating the ambiguity as a feature of quantum gravity's fundamental degrees of freedom. To my knowledge, this is the first reference to post-postmodernism in concert with physics.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过变形正弦-戈登理论（sine-Gordon theory）在(d+1)维反德西特时空中寻找解，同时在标量场理论中构建多项式势的扭结解变形，并分析这些解在不同参数下的极限行为。

Abstract: We find infinitely many soliton-like solutions in a deformation of the sine-Gordon theory in $(d+1)$-dimensional $AdS_{d+1}$ (anti-de Sitter) spacetime for $d \geq 2$, as well as single solitonic solutions in $dS_{d+1}$ (de Sitter) and $\mathrm{H}{d+1}$ (Lobachevsky) spaces for $d \geq 1$ and in $AdS_2$. We also find a deformation of the kink solution in scalar field theory with a polynomial potential in $AdS_2$. The deformation of the sine-Gordon theory strikingly resembles the bosonic part of the flat-space supersymmetric sine-Gordon theory. In the infinite radius limit, single soliton solutions reduce to solitons in flat space. Meanwhile, the multisoliton solution of $AdS{d+1}$, $d\geq 2$ for certain values of the parameters reduces in the same limit to a single soliton solution boosted in the normal direction. However, there are also multisoliton solutions in $AdS_{d+1}$, $d \geq 2$ that do not have a flat space limit.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统计算机受限于处理速度和内存密度，而弯曲时空和奇异场似乎提供了加速计算的途径（如利用时间膨胀效应），这使得一些原本不可能的计算变得可行，但这与直觉相悖。

Method: 通过分析量子引力效应（包括沼泽地猜想）和弯曲时空量子场论，研究观察者和计算机在特定能量尺度下利用相对论效应加速计算的物理限制。

Result: 证明在自然单位下，能够承受能量尺度E的观察者和计算机，通过相对论效应最多只能以O(1)E每单位时间的e-折叠速率加速计算：(lnα)/τ≲E。同时将贝肯斯坦熵界理解为内存的类比界限。

Abstract: A computer, in order to perform a given computation, requires a certain amount of space (memory) and a certain amount of time (runtime). This leaves certain computations beyond reach due to technological limits on processing speed and memory density. Some computations, such as the halting problem, are not possible even in principle. However, curved spacetimes and exotic fields appear to provide avenues to accelerate computation, for instance by exploiting time dilation. Impossible computations seemingly become tractable, butting up against intuition. However, we show that such schemes are consistently thwarted by physical effects from quantum gravity (including swampland conjectures) and quantum field theory in curved space. More precisely, we show that an observer and a computer able to withstand energy scales up to order $E$ can, by using relativistic effects, accelerate computation at a rate of at most $\mathcal O(1)E$ e-folds per unit time in natural units: $(\lnα)/τ\lesssim E$. The Bekenstein bound for entropy can then be understood as the space (memory) analogue to (run)time: if a computer of length scale $D$, operating at energies up to order $E$, has access to $N$ different memory states, then $(\ln N)/D\lesssim E$.

Abstract: We study Matrix theory at strong coupling in a setting describing two static objects a fixed distance apart, using numerical techniques. This involves employing an operator algebra that represents an external observer measuring the relative positions and momenta of the two objects. We identify the location of the horizons of the objects from this entropic force and are led to a modification of the Schwarzschild spacetime inside the horizon. We find evidence that the inside of a black hole is instead to be described by AdS space. The conclusions constitute numerical validation of Verlinde's entropic gravity proposition and the fuzzball paradigm.

Method: 采用拉格朗日乘子法来获得激发解，避免了使用约束兼容参数化时出现的不连续性问题。这些解由整数p表征，其中激发解对应p≠0的情况。

Result: 分析显示全局电荷对参数的依赖呈现非标准行为（non-standard behaviors）。研究发现Skyrme-Chern-Simons项的存在不会显著改变能级模式（pattern of energy levels），p=0的解（基本解）总是具有最小能量。

Conclusion: 在2+1维Skyrme-Chern-Simons理论中，激发解需要使用拉格朗日乘子法获得，这些解具有非标准的全局电荷行为，但Skyrme-Chern-Simons项不会显著改变能级结构，基本解始终具有最小能量。

Abstract: We study excited solutions in a Skyrme--Chern-Simons theory in $2+1$ dimensions. In particular, we emphasize the necessity of using a Lagrange multiplier method to obtain excited solutions, due to the appearance of a discontinuity when using a constraint compliant parametrization. These solutions are characterized by an integer number $p$, excited solutions corresponding to $p\neq 0$. The dependence of the global charges on the parameters is analyzed, showing non-standard behaviors. We also find that the presence of the Skyrme--Chern-Simons term does not alter significantly the pattern of energy levels, so $p=0$ solutions (fundamental solutions) have always the minimal energy.

</details>

*Anastasia Volovich,Di Wu,Kai Yan*

TL;DR: 该研究探索了N=4超杨-米尔斯理论中N点能量关联子（energy correlators）在共线极限下的梅林空间表示，建立了关联子与星形积分（star integrals）之间的系统关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索N=4超杨-米尔斯理论中能量关联子在共线极限下的数学表示，特别是建立这些关联子与已知精确解的星形积分之间的系统联系。

Method: 采用梅林空间表示方法，将能量关联子表示为积分-微分算子作用于星形积分（即n维中的单圈n边形积分）。对于三点和四点关联子，分别建立了与特定积分的关系。

Result: 对于三点能量关联子，获得了梅林表示并将其与有质量盒子积分（massive box integral）关联，通过求解该关系验证了预期结果。对于四点关联子，获得了梅林表示并将其表示为特殊运动学下各种盒子和六边形积分的和。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种系统方法，将共线极限下的高点点能量关联子与已知精确解的星形积分联系起来，为理解这些关联子的数学结构提供了新途径。

Abstract: We explore the Mellin space representation for the collinear limit of $N$-point energy correlators in ${\cal N}=4$ super-Yang-Mills theory. We show that these correlators can be written as integro-differential operators acting on star integrals: one-loop $n$-gons in $n$ dimensions. For the three-point energy correlator, we obtain the Mellin representation, use it to relate the correlator to the massive box integral, and show how to solve this relation to match with the expected result. For the four-point energy correlator, we obtain the Mellin representation and use it to write the correlator to a sum of various box and hexagon integrals in special kinematics. Our results provide a systematic method to relate higher-point energy correlators in the collinear limit to star integrals, which are known exactly.

### [29] [Cosmological Wavefunctions as Amplitudes: Dual Shuffle Factorization and Uniqueness from New Hidden Zeros](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01133)
*Yang Li,Laurentiu Rodina*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文展示了宇宙学波函数系数与平坦空间散射振幅之间的深刻联系：通过变量映射，φ^n理论的波函数系数可转化为类似振幅的对象，这些对象具有新的图基隐藏零点结构，揭示了与幺正性对偶的因子化原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在揭示宇宙学波函数系数与平坦空间散射振幅之间的深层结构联系，探索φ^n理论中波函数系数的数学性质及其与已知振幅构造的关系。

Method: 通过将管变量（tube variables）映射到Mandelstam不变量，将每个波函数系数ψ_𝒢转化为与生成图G相关的类振幅对象𝒜_G；利用图基隐藏零点和因子化原理分析这些对象的结构性质。

Result: 发现了新的图基隐藏零点，扩展并统一了所有已知的宇宙学零点；揭示了与幺正性对偶的因子化原理，其中零点导致生成图的因子化G→G_L×G_R；证明了局域性与完整零点集唯一确定树级宇宙学波函数；建立了零点与BCFW位移下增强大z行为的对应关系。

Conclusion: 宇宙学为壳上方法提供了自然的研究框架，甚至揭示了平坦空间振幅中的新结构；零点结构与BCFW对应的扩展超越了平坦空间振幅，为环级唯一性提供了证据。

Abstract: We show that cosmological wavefunctions in $φ^n$ theories naturally generalize flat-space $\mathrm{Tr}(φ^3)$ scattering amplitudes: via a simple map from tube variables to Mandelstam invariants, each wavefunction coefficient $ψ_{\mathcal{G}}$ becomes an on-shell amplitude-like object $\mathcal{A}_G$ associated with a generating graph $G$. At tree level these objects coincide with the Cachazo-He-Yuan construction based on Cayley functions that generalizes Parke-Taylor factors. We uncover new graph-based hidden zeros that extend and unify all known cosmological zeros. Based on this zero structure, we uncover a factorization principle dual to unitarity. Instead of factorization across poles, $A\to A_L\times A_R$, a zero at $p_{a\in G_L}\!\cdot\! p_{b\in G_R}=0$ factorizes the generating graph, $G\to G_L\times G_R$, and is equivalent to the shuffle decomposition $\mathcal{A}_G=\mathcal{A}_{G_L}\unicode{x29E2}\mathcal{A}_{G_R}$. Near-zero factorization is a simple consequence of this new structure. Using dual factorization, we show that locality together with the full set of hidden zeros uniquely fixes tree-level cosmological wavefunctions without assuming unitarity. We show that these zeros are equivalent to special enhanced large-$z$ behavior under Britto-Cachazo-Feng-Witten (BCFW) shifts, extending the zeros--BCFW correspondence beyond flat-space amplitudes. We also find evidence for further extensions of the zero structure and loop-level uniqueness. Our results show that cosmology provides a natural arena for on-shell methods and even reveals new structure in flat-space amplitudes.

### [30] [Infinite Heat Order in 3+1 Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01184)
*Borut Bajc,Giulia Muco,Francesco Sannino,Sophie Wagner*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究证明在四维紫外完备量子场论中，自发对称破缺可以持续到任意高温。通过分析有限色数和味数的渐近自由模型，发现了标量热质量在高温下保持负值的具体理论实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探究在四维时空的紫外完备量子场论中，自发对称破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）是否能够持续到任意高温。这涉及对称性非恢复（symmetry non-restoration）现象在完全渐近自由（completely asymptotically free）模型中的可能性。

Method: 方法聚焦于具有规范群 $\mathrm{SU}(N_{c1})\times \mathrm{SU}(N_{c2})$ 的完全渐近自由模型，包含两个复标量场。研究扩展了先前Veneziano极限下的分析，推导了有限N的固定流方程（fixed-flow equations），计算了领头阶1/N修正，并对完整有限N系统进行了数值求解。

Result: 结果发现了具体的有限N基准理论，其中标量势有下界，规范部门渐近自由，且一个标量热质量（thermal mass）在任意高温下保持负值。这提供了四维紫外完备量子场论中无限热阶（infinite heat order）的明确微扰示例。

Conclusion: 结论表明在具有有限场内容的四维紫外完备量子场论中，存在明确的微扰理论实例，其中自发对称破缺可以持续到任意高温，实现了对称性非恢复现象。

Abstract: We investigate whether spontaneous symmetry breaking can persist up to arbitrarily high temperature in ultraviolet-complete quantum field theories in four spacetime dimensions. We focus on completely asymptotically free models with gauge group $\mathrm{SU}(N_{c1})\times \mathrm{SU}(N_{c2})$ and two complex scalar fields, each transforming in the fundamental representation of one gauge factor and singlet under the other. The scalar potential contains quartic self-interactions together with a negative portal coupling between the two sectors. In the Veneziano limit, this class of theories was previously shown to admit fixed-flow trajectories for which one scalar acquires a negative thermal mass at asymptotically large temperature, leading to symmetry non-restoration. Here we extend that analysis to finite numbers of colours and flavours. We derive the finite-$N$ fixed-flow equations, compute the leading $1/N$ corrections to the large-$N$ solutions, and solve the full finite-$N$ system numerically. We find explicit finite-$N$ benchmark theories for which the scalar potential remains bounded from below, the gauge sector is asymptotically free, and one scalar thermal mass stays negative at arbitrarily high temperature. This provides an explicit perturbative example of infinite heat order in a four-dimensional ultraviolet-complete quantum field theory with a finite field content.

### [31] [On Generalised Discrete Torsion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01225)
*Philip Boyle Smith,Yuji Tachikawa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了二维规范西格玛模型中广义离散挠率（generalised discrete torsion）的概念，将其从传统的$H^2(BG; U(1))$推广到$H^2_G(M; U(1))$，允许在轨道折叠$M/G$的不同奇点轨迹上分配不同的局部离散挠率相位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统离散挠率$H^2(BG; U(1))$对所有奇点轨迹分配相同的相位，本文旨在推广这一概念，允许在不同奇点轨迹上分配不同的局部离散挠率相位，从而更精细地描述轨道折叠理论。

Method: 通过引入广义离散挠率$H^2_G(M; U(1))$，实现了Gaberdiel和Kaste提出的在高亏格（higher genus）情况下手动插入局部离散挠率相位的方案，并将其应用于$T^6/\mathbb{Z}_2^2$和$T^7/\mathbb{Z}_2^3$轨道折叠共形场论（orbifold CFTs）的具体案例。

Result: 研究发现局部离散挠率相位可以彼此不同，但并非完全独立；在$T^7/\mathbb{Z}_2^3$案例中，轨道折叠共形场论仅实现了Joyce构造的$G_2$解消（resolutions）的9种可能贝蒂数（Betti numbers）中的3种。

Conclusion: 广义离散挠率为轨道折叠理论提供了更精细的相位分配方案，揭示了局部相位间的约束关系，并展示了在具体几何（Calabi-Yau和$G_2$）实现中的限制。

Abstract: For a 2d gauged sigma model with target space $M$ and discrete gauge group $G$, we consider a generalisation of Vafa's discrete torsion $H^2(BG; U(1))$ that assigns different local discrete torsion phases to different singular loci of the orbifold $M/G$. Our generalised discrete torsion lives in $H^2_G(M; U(1))$, and gives a consistent implementation of Gaberdiel and Kaste's prescription for inserting such local discrete torsion phases by hand at higher genus. We revisit the original application to $T^6/\mathbb{Z}_2^2$ and $T^7/\mathbb{Z}_2^3$ orbifold CFTs, and determine what smooth Calabi-Yau and $G_2$ geometries result from different choices of the generalised discrete torsion. We find that the local discrete torsion phases can be different from each other, but are not completely independent either; in the $T^7/\mathbb{Z}_2^3$ case for example, the orbifold CFTs only realise 3 out of the 9 possible Betti numbers of $G_2$ resolutions constructed by Joyce.

### [32] [Dielectric response and viscosity due to dipolar interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00262)
*David S. Dean,Haim Diamant*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究建立了强极性液体中粘度和介电响应之间的直接预测关系，揭示了偶极相互作用是水等强极性液体中粘性耗散的主要机制，并解释了为何许多液体的介电谱需要两个弛豫时间拟合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 介电响应和粘度是液体的两个基本性质，通常被分开处理。研究旨在揭示在强极性液体中，粘度可以直接从介电函数预测，重新审视源自德拜（Debye）的经典液体动力学思想。

Method: 采用热偶极场动力学与流体力学流动耦合的随机场理论，推导了可观测量对流动响应的广义久保（Kubo）关系。在此基础上，基于体力的关联函数而非通常的应力张量公式，推导了粘度算符的格林-久保（Green-Kubo）公式，进而得到了偶极相互作用对粘度的贡献。

Result: 在强极性液体如水中，源自热范德华（van der Waals）相互作用的粘性耗散是主要耗散机制，建立了介电弛豫与粘度之间的直接联系。理论预测即使只有一个微观弛豫机制存在，介电响应中也会出现第二个弛豫时间，这为许多液体需要两个弛豫时间来拟合其介电谱的普遍经验观察提供了自然解释。

Conclusion: 通过建立介电性质与粘度之间的预测性联系，该研究为识别电化学能量存储中有前景的溶剂提供了实用途径，并重新审视了源自德拜的经典液体动力学思想。

Abstract: The dielectric response and viscosity are two fundamental properties of liquids that are usually treated separately. Here we show that in highly polar liquids the viscosity can be predicted directly from the dielectric function. We employ a stochastic field theory for thermal dipole-field dynamics coupled to hydrodynamic flow, and derive a very general Kubo relation for the response of an observable to the flow. We then use this to derive a Green-Kubo formula for the viscosity operator in terms of the correlation function for the body force, rather than the usual stress tensor formulation, and from this we derive the contribution to the viscosity due to dipolar interactions. In strongly polar liquids like water we show that viscous dissipation arising from these thermal van der Waals interactions is the dominant dissipative mechanism, leading to a direct connection between dielectric relaxation and viscosity. The theory also predicts the emergence of a second relaxation time in the dielectric response even when only a single microscopic relaxation mechanism is present. This additional timescale contributes to the intrinsic Debye relaxation and provides a natural explanation for the widespread empirical observation that many liquids require two relaxation times to fit their dielectric spectra. By establishing a predictive link between dielectric properties and viscosity, our results revisit classical ideas of liquid dynamics originating with Debye and suggest a practical route for identifying promising solvents for electrochemical energy storage.

### [33] [Self-similar summation of virial expansions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00294)
*V. I. Yukalov,E. P. Yukalova*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于自相似近似理论（self-similar approximation theory）的新方法，用于对维里展开（virial expansion）进行求和，克服了传统Padé求和的局限性，如非唯一性、虚假极点等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 维里展开作为密度幂级数在低密度下有效，但在有限密度时通常发散。传统Padé求和存在多个缺陷：非唯一性导致大量可接受变体、常出现虚假非物理极点，且在应有物理极点时不一定能正确呈现。

Method: 提出基于自相似近似理论的新求和法，该方法正则且唯一确定，能够识别物理动机的极点。该方法仅依赖维里展开，无需拟合参数，在某些情况下可精确重构目标函数。

Result: 自相似近似（self-similar approximants）的精度不低于带拟合参数的最佳Padé近似或蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）。该方法已成功应用于硬盘流体（hard-disk fluids）、硬球流体（hard-sphere fluids）及幂律势（power-law potentials）系统的维里展开求和。

Conclusion: 自相似求和法为维里展开提供了一种正则、唯一且物理动机明确的替代方案，克服了传统Padé求和的局限性，并在多种系统中展示了其有效性。

Abstract: Virial expansions are the series in powers of density assumed to be small. However, the equations of state require to consider finite densities for which virial expansions, as a rule, diverge. In order to extrapolate a virial expansion to the values, where this expansion diverges, one uses summation methods. The most often used method is the Padé summation, which has several deficiencies. First of all, Padé approximants are not uniquely defined, suggesting a large table of admissible variants. Second, often there appear spurious unphysical poles. On the contrary, in those cases where the existence of a pole is physically motivated, Padé approximants do not necessarily exhibit it. A new approach for the summation of virial expansions is suggested, based on self-similar approximation theory. The method is regular and uniquely defined. It allows for the determination of physically motivated poles. The accuracy of self-similar approximants is not worse than that of the best Padé approximants with fitting parameters or of Monte Carlo simulations. The self-similar summation is based solely on virial expansions, involving no fitting parameters. In some cases, self-similar summation allows for reconstructing the sought functions exactly. The approach is illustrated by summing virial expansions for hard-disk fluids, hard-sphere fluids, and systems with power-law potentials.

</details>


### [34] [Unified Gauge-Geometry Symmetry for Equilibrium Statistical Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00354)
*Hai Pham-Van*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于对称性的平衡统计力学框架，将传统时空对称性与新发现的相空间规范平移不变性统一于单一李群结构，推导出广义Ward恒等式及交叉关系，为多体系统提供了统一的对称性组织基础。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于对称性的框架，运用Noether定理推导广义Ward恒等式（general Ward identities）及由对称生成元非对易性产生的交叉关系（cross-relations）。该方法将内部规范平移对称性纳入统一群结构，扩展了标准多体对称性。

Result: 所得李代数（Lie algebra）揭示了一系列精确恒等式，包含已知求和规则（sum rules）并暗示不同响应函数与关联函数间的交叉耦合关系。提出了Wigner-Eckart-Ward约化，将各向同性流体中的张量-超力关联子简化为两个标量径向谱，并构建了满足相应Ward约束的等变规范约束密度泛函理论（equivariant gauge-constrained DFT）框架。

Conclusion: 该框架为液体、混合物和界面现象提供了一致的组织基础，可能为多体系统中结构、力学和动力学之间的连接提供基于对称性的视角，实现了传统对称性与新发现规范不变性的统一整合。

Abstract: We present a symmetry-based framework for equilibrium statistical mechanics that formulates a single Lie group combining conventional spacetime symmetries with a recently identified phase-space gauge-shifting invariance [Muller et al., Phys. Rev. Lett. 133, 217101 (2024)]. Using Noether's theorem, we obtain a set of general Ward identities together with previously unexplored cross-relations arising from the noncommutation of different symmetry generators. The approach extends standard many-body symmetries, such as translations, rotations, Galilean boosts, dilations, and particle exchange, by incorporating an internal gauge-shift symmetry within a unified group structure. The resulting Lie algebra suggests a hierarchy of exact identities that encompass established sum rules and indicate possible cross-coupling relations between distinct response and correlation functions. We also identify a Wigner-Eckart-Ward reduction that simplifies tensor-hyperforce correlators to two scalar radial spectra in isotropic fluids, and we outline an equivariant gauge-constrained DFT formulation whose Euler-Lagrange equations are constructed to satisfy the corresponding Ward and cross-Ward constraints. This framework provides a consistent organizational basis for phenomena in liquids, mixtures, and interfaces, and may offer a symmetry-based perspective connecting structure, mechanics, and dynamics in many-body systems.

### [35] [Anomalous waiting-time distributions in postselection-free quantum many-body dynamics under continuous monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00358)
*Kazuki Yamamoto,Ryusuke Hamazaki*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究分析了连续监测量子多体系统中量子跳跃的等待时间分布（WTDs），发现半链子系统的WTD呈现异常尾部，与整个系统的泊松分布形成鲜明对比，揭示了测量强度对系统尺寸依赖性的定性变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索连续监测量子多体系统中量子跳跃的等待时间分布特性，特别是当无条件动力学导致平凡无限温度态时，子系统WTD的非平凡行为及其与系统尺寸和测量强度的关系。

Method: 通过分析超算符$\mathscr L_0$的谱特性来研究半链子系统的WTD，该超算符通过从完整Liouvillian中移除与半链子系统相关的跳跃项而定义。WTD仅从量子跳跃的时空记录$\{t_i,x_i\}$中提取，无需后选择即可实验获取。

Result: 研究发现半链子系统的WTD呈现异常尾部，显著偏离泊松分布。异常尾部的长时间行为由具有最大实部的特征值$λ_0$主导。测量强度导致$λ_0$的系统尺寸依赖性发生定性变化：弱测量时$λ_0$与系统尺寸成比例减小，强测量时$λ_0$与系统尺寸无关。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了理解监测量子动力学子系统中非平凡等待时间分布的谱框架，为评估多体效应对WTD的影响提供了新的诊断工具，揭示了异常半链WTD在热力学极限下的持续性。

Abstract: We investigate waiting-time distributions (WTDs) of quantum jumps in continuously monitored quantum many-body systems, whose unconditional dynamics lead to the trivial infinite-temperature state. We demonstrate that the WTD of a half-chain subsystem exhibits an anomalous tail, markedly deviating from the Poissonian distribution in stark contrast to that of the whole system. By analyzing the spectral properties of the superoperator $\mathscr L_0$, which is defined by removing the jump terms associated with the half-chain subsystem from the full Liouvillian, we find that the long-time behavior with the anomalous tail of the half-chain WTD is governed by the eigenvalue $λ_0\:(<0)$ with the largest real part. We further reveal a qualitative change in the system-size dependence of $λ_0$ as a function of the measurement strength: for sufficiently weak measurement, $λ_0$ decreases proportionally to the system size, while for strong measurement, $λ_0$ scales independently of the system size, signaling the persistence of the anomalous half-chain WTD in the thermodynamic limit. The WTD is extracted solely from the spacetime record of quantum jumps $\{t_i,x_i\}$ and can be experimentally accessed without postselection. Our work establishes a spectral framework for understanding nontrivial WTDs in subsystems of monitored quantum dynamics and provides a novel diagnostics to assess many-body effects on WTDs.

</details>


### [36] [Emergent Macroscopic Nonreciprocity from Identical Active Particles via Spontaneous Symmetry Breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00552)
*Wei-Chen Guo,Zuo Wang,Pei-Fang Wu,Li-Jun Lang,Bao-Quan Ai,Liang He*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了微观单物种非互易性（single-species nonreciprocity）在自发对称破缺（SSB）增强下可产生显著的宏观效应，包括诱导有效"双物种"非厄米结构、促进行波带形成，并驱动新颖的实空间凝聚现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用具有视野锥（vision cone）和外噪声（extrinsic noise）的单物种Vicsek模型，研究在有序相中微观非互易性的宏观表现。

Result: 自发对称破缺显著增强了微观单物种非互易性的宏观效应，诱导出具有"双物种"非厄米结构的有效描述。这种增强促进了行波带形成，并驱动了具有消失纵向宽度的"行波线"实空间凝聚现象。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了一种基本机制：自发对称破缺能够显著放大微观单物种非互易性在复杂系统中的宏观影响，导致新颖的集体行为和凝聚现象。

Abstract: Nonreciprocity is known to generate a wide range of exotic phenomena in multi-species many-body systems, where different species influence one another through couplings that violate Newton's third law. In contrast, in the absence of explicitly imposed macroscopic nonreciprocal processes, single-species nonreciprocity -- another distinct form of nonreciprocity -- typically plays only a limited role in shaping macroscopic physics. Here, using a single-species Vicsek model with a vision cone and extrinsic noise, we show that spontaneous symmetry breaking (SSB) can dramatically enhance the macroscopic consequences of microscopic single-species nonreciprocity. In the ordered phase, this enhancement gives rise to an emergent macroscopic nonreciprocity that induces the system of identical active particles to admit an effective description with a "two-species" non-Hermitian structure. The resulting SSB-enhanced nonreciprocity substantially promotes traveling-band formation and, more strikingly, drives a novel real-space condensation of identical active particles, characterized by a "traveling line" with vanishing longitudinal width. Our findings uncover a fundamental mechanism by which microscopic single-species nonreciprocity can exert strong macroscopic influences in complex systems.

### [37] [Tunable information insulation induced by constraint mismatch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00732)
*Akshay Panda,Anwesha Chattopadhyay*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 研究由两个具有双重约束的一维PXP链组成的复合模型，其连接点（junction）形成无限运动学势垒，阻碍量子信息交换。通过放松连接点约束可使硬壁变得可渗透，多个冻结连接点将希尔伯特空间分裂为不连通的Krylov片段。该架构可在可编程里德堡原子平台中实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有双重约束的一维PXP链复合模型，探索连接点作为量子信息交换屏障的特性。通过工程化缺陷和约束调节，研究希尔伯特空间的分裂、能谱统计特性以及手性保护零能模的存在性。

Method: 采用两个具有双重约束的一维PXP链组成复合模型，通过放松连接点约束使硬壁变得可渗透。分析多个冻结连接点导致的希尔伯特空间分裂为不连通的Krylov片段，研究各对称性分辨扇区的能级统计特性。引入具有空间可调热和非热区域的新型Fock态。

Result: 连接点作为无限运动学势垒完全反射量子信息，但放松约束后可变为可渗透。多个冻结连接点使Krylov片段数量随工程缺陷指数增长，各对称扇区能级统计严格泊松分布。发现手性保护零能模存在于物理边界和连接点附近的体区，且不受手性保持无序的影响。非零能scar态数量因本征函数张量积结构而倍增。

Conclusion: 复合PXP链模型中的连接点可作为可调控的量子信息屏障，通过工程化约束可实现希尔伯特空间的分裂和特殊量子态的保护。该架构可在可编程里德堡原子平台中利用光学镊子、寻址光束和促进技术实现，为量子信息处理和量子模拟提供新平台。

Abstract: We study a composite model of two $1D$ $PXP$ chains with dual constraints, forming a junction that acts as an infinite kinematic barrier to quantum information exchange. Moreover, the hard wall at the junction which acts as a perfect reflector, preventing any quantum information leakage between the two sides of the composite chain, can be made permeable by relaxing the constraint at the junction sites. Multiple frozen junctions shatter the Hilbert space into disjoint Krylov fragments, the number of which increases exponentially with the engineered defects. Furthermore, the energy level statistics in each symmetry-resolved sector are strictly Poissonian, demonstrating that the tensor sum of the disjoint Hamiltonians results in a pure superposition of the chaotic spectra of the sub- $PXP$ chains. We also find that a chirally protected zero-energy mode can exist which has local peaks at the physical edges and within the bulk near the junction sites. This state is protected from hybridization with bulk states induced by any chirality preserving disorder. Due to the tensor product structure of the eigenfunctions, the non-zero energy scar states also multiply in number. Finally, we introduce novel Fock states with spatially tunable thermal and athermal regions. This architecture can be readily realized in programmable Rydberg atom platforms using optical tweezers, addressing beams and facilitation techniques.

### [38] [Negative Differential Heat Conductivity in a Harmonic Chain Coupled to a Particle Reservoir](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00777)
*Simon Krekels,Christian Maes,Ion Santra,Ruoxun Zhai*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究证明负微分热导率（negative differential thermal conductivity）可源于热浴本身特性及其与介质的耦合，而非仅由介质非线性相互作用引起。通过构建过阻尼热粒子浴与谐振链耦合的系统，发现当两热浴温差增大时，稳态热流反而减小至零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为负微分热导率主要源于连接介质中的非线性相互作用。本研究旨在探索该效应是否可纯粹由热浴性质及其与系统的耦合方式产生，揭示非平衡输运性质受环境结构影响的机制。

Method: 构建由过阻尼热粒子（overdamped thermal particles）组成的热浴，将其与谐振链（harmonic chain）一端耦合，另一端连接标准朗之万热浴（standard Langevin heat bath）。通过分析稳态热流（steady-state heat current）研究热输运特性。

Result: 观察到显著的负微分热导率现象：当两热浴温差增大时，稳态热流反而减小；温差发散时，通过链的稳态热流趋近于零。计算有效耗散系数发现，高温极限下其与粒子浴温度的平方成反比，导致热浴与链渐近解耦。

Conclusion: 负微分热导率可纯粹由热浴结构及其与系统耦合产生，无需介质非线性相互作用。该热动力学效应（thermokinetic effect）表明非平衡输运性质强烈依赖于环境结构，即使在原本线性的系统中也是如此。

Abstract: When coupling thermal baths at different temperatures, negative differential thermal conductivity is typically attributed to nonlinear interactions in the connecting medium. In this work, we demonstrate that such an effect can arise purely from the nature of the thermal baths and their coupling with the medium. Specifically, we construct a bath composed of overdamped thermal particles, which is coupled to one end of a harmonic chain, while the other end is connected to a standard Langevin heat bath. By analyzing the steady-state heat current, we observe significant negative differential thermal conductivity. In particular, as the temperature difference between the two baths diverges, the steady-state heat current through the chain vanishes. The effect is thermokinetic: we compute the effective dissipative coefficient and we find that it scales inversely with the square of the temperature of the particle bath in the high-temperature limit, resulting in an asymptotic decoupling between the bath and the chain. Our results highlight that nonequilibrium transport properties can be strongly influenced by the structure of the environment and its coupling to the system, even in otherwise linear systems.

### [39] [Statistical Physics of Coding for the Integers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00858)
*Neri Merhav*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过zeta分布（zeta distribution）探索自然数压缩编码范式，建立统计力学解释，并开发接近理想码长的简单编码方案。研究揭示了Hagedorn型相变（Hagedorn-type phase transition）导致系综部分等价性（partial equivalence of ensembles）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索基于zeta分布的自然数压缩编码范式，并建立其统计力学解释，特别是通过Hagedorn系统和以素数对数（logarithms of prime numbers）为能级的玻色气体（Bose gas）框架。

Method: 方法包括：为zeta分布设计简单编码方案；推导自然数向量块编码（block coding）的微正则熵函数（micro-canonical entropy function）；分析大偏差率函数（large deviations rate function）；确定大偏差意义下的最优编码参数。

Result: 结果显示：微正则熵函数具有渐近线性，行为类似于Hagedorn系统；由于Hagedorn型相变导致配分函数（partition function）定义域退化，仅存在系综的部分等价性（partial equivalence of ensembles）。

Conclusion: 结论表明：基于zeta分布的自然数压缩编码具有统计力学解释，其行为与Hagedorn系统类似；相变现象导致系综等价性不完全，为编码参数优化提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We study a paradigm of coding for compression of the natural numbers via the zeta distribution and develop a statistical-mechanical interpretation, both in terms of Hagedorn systems and a Bose gas with energy levels given by logarithms of prime numbers. We also propose a simple coding scheme for the zeta distribution that nearly achieves the ideal code length. For block coding of vectors of natural numbers, we derive the micro-canonical entropy function and demonstrate its asymptotic linearity implying that its behavior is analogous to that of a Hagedorn system. We also derive the large deviations rate function, and provide a formula for the best coding parameter in the large deviations sense. We show that due the Hagedorn-type phase transition there is only partial equivalence of ensembles, due to the degeneration of the domain of the partition function.

### [40] [The Klein bottle ratio of two-dimensional ferromagnetic Potts models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00870)
*Zi-Han Wang,Li-Ping Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究采用密度矩阵和张量网络重整化群方法，通过克莱因瓶比（Klein bottle ratio）分析二维5态铁磁Potts模型的弱一级相变特性，精确确定了q=4,5,6的临界点，并提取了中心电荷以验证理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维5态铁磁Potts模型的弱一级相变特性给数值研究带来挑战，需要开发有效方法来准确表征这类相变的临界行为。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group）和张量网络重整化群（tensor-network renormalization group）方法，通过克莱因瓶比（Klein bottle ratio）g在原格子和对偶格子上分析Potts-q模型的相变。

Result: 通过横向系统尺寸Ly的有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）精确确定了q=4,5,6的临界点；对于q=5，提取的中心电荷c≈1.14811接近复共形场论（complex conformal field theories）的理论预测值c5-Potts=1.1375±0.0211i。

Conclusion: 标度指数b的漂移有效区分了连续相变与弱一级相变区域，且g的外推发散证实了q=5 Potts模型的一级相变本质。

Abstract: The weakly first-order nature of the two-dimensional 5-state ferromagnetic Potts model poses challenges for numerical study. Using density-matrix and tensor-network renormalization group methods, we investigate these transitions of the Potts-$q$ model via the Klein bottle ratio $g$ on original and dual lattices. Finite-size scaling of $g$ as a function of transverse system size $L_y$ accurately locates the critical points for $q = 4, 5, 6$. We further examine the transfer-matrix spectra and entanglement entropy, extracting central charges through toroidal and Klein bottle boundary conditions. For $q = 5$, the extracted central charge ($c \approx 1.14811$) is close to the real part of the theoretical value $c_{5\text{-Potts}} = 1.1375 \pm 0.0211 i$ predicted by complex conformal field theories. The observed drift in the scaling exponent $b$ effectively distinguishes the continuous transition from the weakly first-order regime. Furthermore, the extrapolated divergence of $g$ confirms the first-order nature of the $q=5$ Potts model.

Abstract: We study non-equilibrium quantum dynamics by performing principal component analysis on the data sets of wavefunction snapshots. This connection enables us to explain the dynamical features revealed by such a dimensionality-reduction scheme. We demonstrate this using quantum dynamics of the Heisenberg spin chain, starting from different initial states, and further extend the approach to extract higher-order correlations. Our framework should also be applicable to other unsupervised machine-learning methods based on dimensionality-reduction schemes and is highly relevant to experiments with quantum simulators, including those in higher dimensions.

### [43] [Eppur non si trovano Vol. 2: No Planetary-mass Primordial Black Holes toward the Andromeda Galaxy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00111)
*Przemek Mróz,Andrzej Udalski*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究重新分析了Subaru望远镜对仙女座星系（M31）的观测数据，发现先前报道的12个短时标微引力透镜（gravitational microlensing）候选体实际上都是变星，而非原始黑洞（primordial black holes）的微透镜信号，从而否定了行星质量原始黑洞作为暗物质（dark matter）主要成分的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前Sugiyama等人基于Subaru Hyper Suprime-Cam对仙女座星系（M31）的高频测光观测，报告了12个短时标（小于一天）微引力透镜（gravitational microlensing）候选体，并将其归因于可能构成银河系和M31晕中全部暗物质（dark matter）的大量行星质量原始黑洞（primordial black holes）。然而，这些结果与先前对麦哲伦云的短时标微透镜搜索（如OGLE巡天）存在明显矛盾，且候选体的时空分布与微透镜事件的预期不一致。

Method: 本研究使用独立的差分图像分析（difference image analysis）测光流程重新分析了Subaru数据。通过检查候选体的光变曲线（light curves）特征和多个观测夜间的变异性，对先前报道的候选体进行了重新评估。

Result: 分析发现所有12个候选体都表现出不对称的光变曲线（asymmetric light curves）和/或在多个观测夜间的变异性。其中10个是室女座RR型变星（RR Lyrae stars），1个是食双星（eclipsing binary），1个是未分类的变星（unclassified variable star）。在Subaru数据集中未发现短时标微引力透镜事件的有力证据，也未发现行星质量原始黑洞作为暗物质重要成分的显著群体。

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了在使用大型望远镜进行高频微透镜搜索时，必须采用稳健的变星排除方法。该分析否定了先前关于行星质量原始黑洞作为暗物质主要成分的发现，表明这些候选体实际上都是已知类型的变星。

Abstract: A recent preprint by Sugiyama et al. reported the discovery of twelve candidates for short-timescale (less than one day) gravitational microlensing events based on high-cadence photometric observations of the Andromeda Galaxy (M31) using the Subaru Hyper Suprime-Cam. These detections were attributed to a large population of planetary-mass primordial black holes (PBHs) that could account for the entirety of the dark matter in the Milky Way and M31 halos. However, these results are in clear tension with previous searches for short-timescale microlensing events toward the Magellanic Clouds, such as those by the OGLE survey. In addition, both the temporal and spatial distributions of the Subaru candidates are inconsistent with expectations for microlensing events. Here, we reanalyze the Subaru data using an independent difference image analysis photometric pipeline. We find that all twelve candidates identified by Sugiyama et al. exhibit asymmetric light curves and/or variability on multiple nights of Subaru observations. Our analysis reveals that among them ten objects are RR Lyrae stars, one is an eclipsing binary, and one is an unclassified variable star. We find no compelling evidence for short-timescale microlensing events among the candidates identified in the Subaru data set, nor for a significant population of planetary-mass PBHs as dark matter components. Our results underscore the necessity of robust variable-star rejection in high-cadence microlensing searches using large telescopes.

### [44] [Relic Magnetic Fields from Non-Adiabatic Photon Freeze-Out at Recombination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00454)
*Hyeong-Chan Kim*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种在宇宙复合-退耦（recombination-decoupling）过渡期间产生原始电磁遗迹的新机制，基于宇宙光子气体的速率相关热力学。该机制通过非绝热模式挤压（non-adiabatic mode squeezing）产生电磁遗迹，其峰值尺度对应于现今的10-20 Mpc，但场强极小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在解释原始电磁遗迹的产生机制，特别是在宇宙复合-退耦（recombination-decoupling）过渡期间。现有理论可能无法充分解释观测到的宇宙磁场起源，因此需要探索基于非平衡热力学的新机制。

Method: 将光子扇区（photon sector）视为与电子等离子体耦合的开放系统，考虑有限汤姆逊弛豫率（Thomson relaxation rate）导致的非瞬时热平衡偏离。通过正则变换（canonical transformation）将简化演化方程重铸为具有平滑有效势的受迫振子（forced oscillator），阐明挤压起源和遗迹尺度的选择。

Result: 该机制产生一个冻结的非平衡电磁遗迹，其特征峰值由加权组合 \(k^3\mathscr S_k\) 控制，而非仅由挤压参数（squeezing parameter）决定。在典型实现中，峰值对应现今尺度为10-20 Mpc，但现今场振幅极小。

Conclusion: 该机制应被视为冻结非平衡电磁遗迹的来源，而非对观测宇宙磁场的完整解释。它描述了从绝热跟踪（adiabatic tracking）到弛豫后冻结（post-relaxation freeze-out）的狭窄过渡层（transition layer）中的动力学过程。

Abstract: We propose a new mechanism for generating a primordial electromagnetic relic during the recombination--decoupling transition, based on the rate-dependent thermodynamics of the cosmic photon gas. Treating the photon sector as an open system coupled to the electron plasma, we show that a finite Thomson relaxation rate generates a departure from instantaneous thermal equilibrium, leading to non-adiabatic mode squeezing. As this relaxation rate rapidly decreases across recombination, the system quickly loses the ability to further amplify the deviation, and the squeezing freezes out at a small but finite value. This dynamics is naturally described as a narrow transition layer between an adiabatic tracking regime and a post-relaxation freeze-out regime. By a canonical transformation, the reduced evolution equation is recast into a forced oscillator with a smooth effective potential, clarifying the origin of the squeezing and the selection of the relic scale.
  Projecting the resulting non-equilibrium electromagnetic relic onto the magnetic sector, we derive the corresponding spectrum and show that its characteristic peak is controlled not by the squeezing parameter alone but by the weighted combination \(k^3\mathscr S_k\). In representative realizations, the peak corresponds today to scales of order \(10\)--\(20\) Mpc, while the present-day field amplitude remains extremely small. The mechanism is therefore better viewed as a source of a frozen non-equilibrium electromagnetic relic than as a complete explanation of the observed cosmic magnetic fields.

</details>


### [45] [Universal Non-Gaussian Signatures from Transient Instabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01035)
*Shuntaro Aoki,Diederik Roest,Denis Werth*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究识别了暴胀期间熵涨落瞬态不稳定在双谱中产生的普适特征，通过精确数值计算揭示了轻质量和重质量情况下的不同双谱特征，并提出了适用于观测的形状模板。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在识别双谱（bispectrum）中由暴胀期间熵涨落（entropic fluctuations）瞬态不稳定（transient tachyonic instability）产生的普适特征，这种现象在双曲场空间几何（hyperbolic field-space geometries）中自然出现。研究动机包括理解非标准暴胀吸引子（non-standard inflationary attractors）的特征。

Method: 采用精确数值计算直接处理涨落层面，不依赖特定背景模型，区分轻质量（light case）和重质量（heavy case）两种情况。对于轻质量情况（质量接近哈勃尺度），首次计算了此类不稳定产生的双谱；作为示例，计算并分析了角暴胀（angular inflation）中的双谱。

Result: 在轻质量情况下，发现折叠构型（folded configuration）的普适放大，以及挤压极限（squeezed limit）中已知的非解析标度行为；角暴胀示例显示与当前观测限制兼容。在重质量情况下，双谱显示增强折叠构型与温和挤压极限中"不稳定共振（tachyonic resonance）"的独特关联，共振尺度由不稳定强度设定。

Conclusion: 研究证明不存在任何紫外匹配（UV matching）能使通过积分掉熵模式获得的单场有效描述（single-field effective description）准确捕捉所有运动学构型的双谱。为促进观测应用，引入了适用于当前和未来宇宙学巡天的简单双谱形状模板（bispectrum shape templates）。

Abstract: We identify universal signatures in the bispectrum arising from a transient tachyonic instability of entropic fluctuations during inflation, a phenomenon that naturally arises in hyperbolic field-space geometries. We perform exact numerical calculations directly at the level of fluctuations, without relying on a specific background model, and distinguish two cases. In the light case, with masses around the Hubble scale, our results provide the first-ever computation of the bispectrum due to such tachyonic instabilities. We find a universal magnification of the folded configuration, together with the known non-analytic scaling in the squeezed limit. As an illustrative example, we compute and analyse the bispectrum in angular inflation, demonstrating compatibility with current limits. In the heavy case, with masses well above the Hubble scale, the bispectrum exhibits a distinctive correlation between enhanced folded configurations and a `tachyonic resonance' in mildly squeezed limits, with the resonance scale set by the strength of the instability. While the main qualitative features are reproduced, we show that there exists no UV matching for which a single-field effective description, obtained by integrating out the entropic modes, accurately captures the bispectrum for all kinematic configurations. To facilitate observational applications, we introduce simple bispectrum shape templates suitable for current and forthcoming cosmological surveys. Our model-independent results allow for constraining non-standard inflationary attractors characterised by strongly non-geodesic motion.

</details>

Abstract: This overview of the study arXiv:2407.18845, regarding the possibility of generating gravitational waves from a curvature-induced phase transition of a non-minimally coupled scalar dark matter field with a Higgs-portal, was showcased at the "Workshop on Standard Model and Beyond 2025" of the Corfu Summer Institute 2025. The phase transition dynamics during the transition from inflation to kination were calculated for various inflationary scales, considering both positive and negative values of the non-minimal coupling, while also examining the potential for triggering electroweak symmetry breaking. Notably, kination enhances the GW amplitudes, significantly restricting the viable parameter space. While the GW spectra follow the usual rule for high-frequencies from high inflationary scales, certain regions of the parameter space allow for a potential detection with future experiments.

### [47] [Cosmological zoom-in perturbation theory as a consistent beyond point-particle approximation framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01112)
*Obinna Umeh*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文开发了一个协变多尺度框架，通过将时空分解为由物质视界分隔的层次区域，解决了宇宙学中全动力学范围结构建模的挑战。该框架为宇宙学放大模拟提供了第一性原理理论基础，并产生了一个有效能量-动量张量来捕捉几何反作用效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建模宇宙全动力学范围的结构形成仍然是宇宙学的主要挑战。这一困难源于广义相对论中测地线的基本限制：单参数测地线族可能在有限时间内不再是测地线，这意味着测地线流的崩溃限制了跨尺度的一致性描述。

Method: 开发了一个协变多尺度框架，通过将时空分解为由物质视界分隔的层次区域来解决该问题。在作用量层面一致地匹配共享边界，从而产生协变反作用贡献。

Result: 该构造为宇宙学放大模拟（cosmological zoom-in simulations）提供了第一性原理理论基础，并产生了一个有效能量-动量张量（effective energy-momentum tensor）来捕捉几何反作用效应（geometric backreaction effect）。作为应用，证明这种反作用自然地产生平坦的星系旋转曲线，无需引入额外的暗物质成分。

Conclusion: 研究结果为非线性结构形成建立了新视角，其中长动力学范围通过离散测地线域（discrete geodesic domains）的层次结构得以解析。该框架解决了跨尺度一致性描述的根本限制。

Abstract: Modelling structure formation across the full dynamical range of the Universe remains a major challenge in cosmology. This difficulty originates from a fundamental limitation of geodesics in general relativity: a one-parameter family of geodesics can cease to be geodesic at a finite time. This implies that the conventional point-particle approximation is not the primary issue; rather, the breakdown of geodesic flow restricts a consistent description across scales. We develop a covariant multi-scale framework that resolves this problem by decomposing spacetime into hierarchical regions separated by matter horizons. We show how to match shared boundary consistently at the level of the action, leading to a covariant backreaction contribution. The resulting construction provides a first-principles theoretical foundation for cosmological zoom-in simulations and yields an effective energy-momentum tensor capturing the impact of the geometric backreaction effect. As an application, we demonstrate that this backreaction naturally produces flat galaxy rotation curves without invoking an additional dark matter component. Our results establish a new perspective on nonlinear structure formation, in which long dynamical range is resolved through a hierarchy of discrete geodesic domains.

</details>

### [48] [Wormhole Dynamics: Nonlinear Collapse and Gravitational-Wave Emission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00071)
*Nikita M. Shirokov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值相对论模拟研究了不稳定Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞的演化，展示了在压缩性演化中形成陷获面（trapped surface）并产生引力波信号的过程，以及幻影物质（phantom matter）引发的"幻影反弹"现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究不稳定Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞的动力学演化，特别是其在扰动下的压缩性演化和引力波发射特性，为通过引力波观测探测虫洞提供理论依据。

Method: 使用GRTeclyn进行三维数值相对论模拟，从精确的各向同性初始数据出发，通过减少幻影应力-能量支撑至S_support=0.5并添加四极标量场扰动（A_phi=+0.02, sigma_phi=0.5）来打破球对称性。

Result: 压缩性演化形成了陷获面（trapped surface），并发射了峰值以近似光速传播的引力波信号；视界形成后，被吞噬的幻影物质触发了剧烈的反弹（"phantom bounce"），向外发射曲率激波。

Conclusion: 对于中等扰动振幅，中等质量（10^3太阳质量）虫洞在1 Mpc距离处略低于Advanced LIGO设计灵敏度；探测需要更近的源、更大的初始不对称性或下一代探测器。

Abstract: We present 3D numerical-relativity evolutions of the unstable Ellis-Bronnikov wormhole using GRTeclyn, starting from exact isotropic initial data for the coupled Einstein-phantom-scalar system. With a flat initial lapse (alpha=1) and full phantom support, truncation-level noise eventually drives the rarefactive instability and rapid throat expansion. To force a clean collapse while breaking spherical symmetry, we reduce the phantom stress-energy support to S_support=0.5 and add a quadrupolar scalar-field perturbation (A_phi=+0.02, sigma_phi=0.5). The resulting compressive evolution forms a trapped surface and emits a gravitational-wave signal whose peak propagates between extraction radii at v approx c, distinct from superluminal CCZ4 constraint modes. After horizon formation the swallowed phantom matter triggers a violent rebound ("phantom bounce") that launches an outward curvature shock. For the moderate perturbation amplitude simulated here, an intermediate-mass (10^3 solar mass) wormhole at D=1 Mpc falls slightly below the Advanced LIGO design sensitivity; detection requires either closer sources, larger initial asymmetries, or next-generation detectors.

Result: 论文提出通过退化时空度规可以消除大爆炸曲率奇点，这一方案在研讨会上进行了主要讨论。同时，论文还探讨了CPT共轭世界的可能性和扩展爱因斯坦场方程的理论意义。

Abstract: The Friedmann cosmological solution of the standard Einstein gravitational field equation has a curvature singularity at a moment in time known as the Big Bang.
