### [50] [Regular Black Strings and BTZ Black Hole in Unimodular Gravity Supported by Maxwell Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00078)
*G. Alencar V. H. U. Borralho*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在单模引力（unimodular gravity）框架下，为规则黑洞弦（regular black string）和BTZ黑洞（BTZ black hole）构建了麦克斯韦源（Maxwell source），并推导出支持这些解的真空贡献函数Λ(r)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索单模引力这一广义相对论替代理论的应用，该理论通过施加时空体积元素恒定的条件来限制微分同胚不变性（diffeomorphism invariance），并将宇宙常数（cosmological constant）处理为场方程的积分常数而非直接出现在作用量中。

Method: 采用单模引力框架，利用能动张量（energy-momentum tensor）的非守恒性，将积分常数转化为径向坐标函数Λ(x)；通过几何函数H(r)的定义验证麦克斯韦电动力学（Maxwell electrodynamics）作为解的源的有效性。

Result: 成功获得规则黑洞弦和BTZ黑洞的麦克斯韦源，并计算出支持这些解的真空贡献函数Λ(r)，该函数被解释为依赖于径向坐标的真空贡献。

Conclusion: 在单模引力框架下，麦克斯韦电动力学可作为规则黑洞弦和BTZ黑洞的有效源，且宇宙常数以径向依赖的真空贡献函数Λ(r)形式出现，支持了相关黑洞解的存在。

Abstract: In this work, we obtain a Maxwell source for regular black string and BTZ black hole using the framework of unimodular gravity. This type of alternative to general relativity imposes an additional condition on the spacetime volume element, namely that it is constant, $\det(g_{μν}) = g_0$, and thus restricts diffeomorphism invariance to volume-preserving transformations. In this procedure, the cosmological constant does not appear directly in the action, but rather as an integration constant of the field equations. By using the non-conservation of the energy-momentum tensor, we show that the integration constant becomes a function $Λ(x)$, which is interpreted as a vacuum contribution depending on the radial coordinate, in our case. From the definition of the geometric function $H(r)$, we verify the validity of Maxwell electrodynamics as a source for the solutions and compute the vacuum contribution $Λ(r)$ that supports the solutions.

### [51] [Distinguishing Black Holes and Neutron Stars via Optical Imaging Illuminated by Thick Accretion Disks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00117)
*Chen-Yu Yang,Xiao-Xiong Zeng*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用多方状态方程（polytropic equation of state）模型，数值求解中子星结构后，结合测地线方程（geodesic equations）和辐射传输方程（radiative transfer equation）进行数值计算。

Result: 在光子轨迹终止于中子星表面的假设下，图像显示为内部暗区被明亮高阶结构环绕。随着多方指数N增加，高阶图像尺寸逐渐扩大；观测者倾角θ_o增大时，赤道面外辐射对中子星轮廓的遮蔽更显著。与相同参数下的黑洞阴影相比，中子星的高阶图像更大、内部暗区遮蔽更广，而黑洞的高阶图像更易区分。

Conclusion: 中子星和黑洞的光学外观存在显著差异，这些结果为通过高分辨率成像技术区分这两类致密天体提供了理论依据。

Abstract: This paper investigates the optical images of neutron stars within the framework of the radiatively inefficient accretion flow model, taking into account a polytropic equation of state. After obtaining the numerical solutions of the neutron star, we solved numerically the geodesic equations together with the radiative transfer equation. We mainly examine the effects of the polytropic index $N$ and the observer inclination angle $θ_o$ on the image morphology. The obtained images are also compared with the shadow of a Schwarzschild black hole. It is shown that, under the assumption that photon trajectories are terminated at the neutron star surface, the image exhibits a bright higher order structure surrounding an inner dark region. As $N$ increases, the size of the higher-order image gradually expands. As $θ_o$ increases, the obscuration of the neutron star silhouette by radiation originating outside the equatorial plane becomes more pronounced. Compared with the black hole shadow obtained under the same parameter configuration, the neutron star exhibits a larger higher order image and a more extended obscured inner dark region, whereas the higher order image of the black hole is more readily distinguishable. These results indicate significant differences in the optical appearance of neutron stars and black holes, and thus provide a theoretical basis for distinguishing between them through high resolution imaging.

### [52] [Does a wormhole survive a cosmological bounce?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00134)
*Daniela Pérez,Gustavo E. Romero,Santiago E. Perez Bergliaffa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在宇宙反弹（cosmological bounce）过程中动态虫洞（dynamical wormhole）能否持续存在，发现至少对于Kim和Pérez-Raia Neto解，在反弹宇宙模型中虫洞能够持续存在且没有拓扑结构变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探究在经历宇宙学反弹的宇宙中，动态虫洞是否能够从收缩相持续到膨胀相。这涉及到理解虫洞在宇宙演化关键阶段的稳定性问题。

Method: 方法包括：首先提出虫洞在宇宙收缩到膨胀相持续存在的条件；然后分析爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein's equations）中仅有的两个已知代表虫洞的宇宙学解；最后详细分析这类时空的因果结构和虫洞的物质成分。

Result: 结果表明，两个动态虫洞解在反弹宇宙的所有宇宙时间（包括反弹时刻本身）都存在。研究还提供了此类时空因果结构和虫洞物质成分的详细分析，并讨论了反弹宇宙中存活虫洞可能的天体物理表现。

Conclusion: 结论显示，至少对于Kim和Pérez-Raia Neto解，在选择的反弹宇宙模型中不存在拓扑结构变化（topology change），虫洞能够持续存在。

Abstract: We investigate whether a dynamical wormhole could survive in a universe that undergoes a cosmological bounce. First, the conditions under which a wormhole could persist from a contracting to an expanding phase of the cosmos are presented. Then, the only two known cosmological solutions of Einstein's equations representing wormholes are analyzed, and it is shown that both dynamical wormholes exist for all cosmic times on both sides of a bouncing universe and at the bounce itself. We also provide a detailed analysis of the causal structure of such spacetimes and the matter content of the wormhole. Finally, some possible astrophysical manifestations of surviving wormholes in a bouncing universe are mentioned. Our results show that, at least for the Kim and Pérez-Raia Neto solutions, there is no topology change in the chosen cosmological model with a bounce.

</details>


### [53] [Thermodynamics of dynamical black holes beyond perturbation theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00170)
*Abhay Ashtekar,Daniel E. Paraizo,Jonathan Shu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文探讨黑洞力学定律与热力学定律的相似性，指出传统事件视界（event horizon）范式的局限性，并提出使用准局域视界（quasi-local horizons）来克服这些限制，将黑洞熵与准局域视界中的边际俘获面（marginally trapped surfaces）面积相关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bardeen、Carter和Hawking发现的黑洞力学三定律与热力学定律的密切相似性，促使人们将事件视界面积与熵联系起来。然而，过去二十年的发展表明这一范式存在重要局限性，特别是由于事件视界的"目的论性质（teleological nature）"。

Method: 通过使用准局域视界（quasi-local horizons）来克服传统事件视界范式的局限性。新方法适用于广义相对论中可"任意远离平衡态（arbitrarily far from equilibrium）"的黑洞，并涉及由视界处"物理过程（physical processes）"引起的"有限（finite）"变化。

Result: 新的第一定律适用于任意远离平衡态的黑洞，第二定律成为将动力学视界段面积变化与落入黑洞的能量通量相关联的"定量（quantitative）"陈述。这导致将黑洞熵与准局域视界中边际俘获面（marginally trapped surfaces）的面积等同起来，而非事件视界面积。

Conclusion: 准局域视界方法克服了传统事件视界范式的局限性，将黑洞熵重新定义为准局域视界中边际俘获面的面积，这推广了近期微扰（perturbative）研究的发现，为黑洞热力学提供了更物理的基础。

Abstract: The close similarities of the three laws of black hole mechanics, discovered by Bardeen, Carter and Hawking, with the laws of thermodynamics led to the identification of a multiple of the area of the event horizon with entropy. However, developments over the past two decades have shown that this paradigm has some important limitations, especially because of the teleological nature of event horizons. After a brief review of these limitations, we will show that they can be overcome using quasi-local horizons. Specifically, the new first law applies to black holes in general relativity that can be \emph{arbitrarily far from equilibrium} and refers to \emph{finite} changes that occur due to \emph{physical processes} at the horizon. The second law is now a \emph{quantitative} statement that relates the change in the area of a dynamical horizon segment due to fluxes of energy falling into the black hole. Together, they lead one to identify black hole entropy with the area of marginally trapped surfaces in quasi-local horizons, generalizing recent {perturbative} findings that it should be identified not with the area of the event horizon but with the area of a marginally trapped surface inside it.

</details>


### [54] [No-Go Theorem for Singularity Resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00204)
*Zhen-Xiao Zhang,Chen Lan,Yan-Gang Miao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文证明了一个关于引力坍缩中奇点消解的"不可行定理"（No-Go theorem）：在包括广义相对论和所有多项式作用量理论在内的任何解析引力理论中，仅作为有效物质源引入的量子修正不足以阻止奇点形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨量子引力方法中奇点消解（singularity resolution）的可能性，特别是检验仅通过有效能量密度（effective energy density）修正是否能够避免引力坍缩中的奇点形成。

Method: 采用内在的$f(\mathbb{Q})$引力框架，通过几何三位一体（geometrical trinity）将其普遍扩展到广义相对论、$f(\mathbb{R})$和$f(\mathbb{T})$理论。该方法基于非度量性（non-metricity）建立正则性判据和连接条件，避免使用标准广义相对论工具。

Result: 证明结果表明，在包括渐近安全（asymptotic safety）和非对易几何（noncommutative geometry）在内的广泛量子引力方法中，仅通过有效能量密度消解奇点的方案必然导致有限时间奇点或测地不完备性（geodesic incompleteness）。

Conclusion: 奇点消解严格需要两种途径之一：要么对引力作用量进行非解析修正，要么实现高密度下有效能量密度趋近于零（如圈量子引力中的普朗克星（Planck stars）所实现）。该定理排除了仅通过有效物质源修正消解奇点的可能性。

Abstract: We prove a No-Go theorem for singularity resolution in gravitational collapse: within any analytic gravitational theory, including general relativity and all theories with polynomial actions, quantum corrections introduced solely as effective matter sources are insufficient to halt singularities. This rules out singularity resolution via effective energy density in a broad class of quantum gravity approaches, including asymptotic safety and noncommutative geometry, which inevitably yield finite-time singularities or geodesic incompleteness. Resolution strictly requires either non-analytic modifications to the gravitational action, or a vanishing effective energy density at high densities (as realized in loop quantum gravity's Planck stars). The theorem is proved via an intrinsic $f(\mathbb{Q})$ gravity framework, extended universally to general relativity, $f(\mathbb{R})$, and $f(\mathbb{T})$ through the geometrical trinity--with regularity criteria and junction conditions grounded in non-metricity, free of standard GR tools.

Abstract: Quasinormal modes describe the relaxation of perturbed black holes and relate ringdown observables to the background geometry. ### [56] [Big bang stability and isotropisation for the Einstein-scalar field equations in the ekpyrotic regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00297)
*Florian Beyer,David Garfinkle,James Isenberg,Todd A. Oliynyk*

TL;DR: 本文证明了在势能参数 s > s_c 且 V_0 < 0 的 ekpyrotic 标量场势能下，爱因斯坦-标量场方程中的 FLRW 解在时间反演方向是非线性稳定的，并在大爆炸奇点处各向同性化。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析爱因斯坦-标量场方程在 ekpyrotic 势能 V_0 e^{-s φ}（其中 s > s_c 且 V_0 < 0）下的动力学行为，研究 FLRW 解在时间反演方向的非线性稳定性。

Result: 证明了在 ekpyrotic 参数范围内，FLRW 解在时间反演方向是非线性稳定的，并终止于一个静态的、压碎的渐近速度项主导（AVTD）大爆炸奇点。这些扰动时空的显著特性是它们在大爆炸奇点附近各向同性化。

Conclusion: 与 s < s_c 情况不同，ekpyrotic 势能（s > s_c, V_0 < 0）下的 FLRW 解不仅稳定，而且扰动解在大爆炸奇点处表现出各向同性化行为，这是该参数区域的一个区分性特征。

In particular, the spatially homogeneous and isotropic solutions, the Friedman-Lemaitre-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) spacetimes, to the Einstein-scalar field equations are stable in this sense for $s<s_c$ and $V_0\in\mathbb{R}$.
  While perturbations of the sub-critical Kasner-scalar field family of solutions, including the FLRW solutions, are asymptotically velocity term dominated (AVTD) near the big bang, they do not in general isotropise near the big bang singularity. Rather, they remain highly anisotropic, even for small perturbations of the isotropic FLRW solutions.
  In this article, we establish the stability of FLRW solutions to the Einstein-scalar field equations for the potential parameter values $s>s_c$ and $V_0<0$. Such scalar field potentials are known in the literature as \textit{ekpyrotic}. In particular, we prove that the FLRW solutions to the Einstein-scalar field equations are nonlinearly stable to the past and terminate at a quiescent, crushing AVTD big bang singularity. A distinguishing property of these perturbed spacetimes is that they isotropise towards the big bang.

Abstract: Primordial black holes (PBHs) are widely considered as candidates for dark matter in many recent studies, and they are often modeled as Schwarzschild or Kerr black holes (BHs), which have curvature singularities. Nevertheless, resolving the classical singularity may require quantum gravity motivated corrections, thereby yielding an effective quantum corrected BH spacetime geometry different from the Schwarzschild or Kerr cases. Therefore, it is well motivated to consider BHs beyond the Schwarzschild or Kerr as viable PBH candidates. Based on these considerations, we investigate quantum Oppenheimer Snyder BHs as PBHs which could account for all the dark matter. Our results show that these BHs have temperatures and greybody factors markedly different from the Schwarzschild case, suppressing Hawking emission and thereby relaxing the $γ$-ray constraints from HEAO-1, COMPTEL, and EGRET, which, relative to the Schwarzschild case, broadens the allowed PBH mass window in the asteroid-mass range where PBHs can constitute all of the dark matter.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We investigate kinematic and optical signatures of Lorentz-violation in the strong-field region of a rotating bumblebee black hole generated by a scalar-gradient bumblebee field. Through the analysis of spin precession of test gyroscopes and timelike geodesic motion in the spacetime, we find that Lorentz-violating effect suppresses the Lense-Thirring precession near the horizon, while enhancing geodetic precession in the static, spherically symmetric limit. For bound circular orbits in the equatorial plane, the Lorentz-violation leads to an increase in the periastron precession frequency. Furthermore, images of a geometrically thin accretion disk reveal that the Lorentz-violation has a negligible impact on the critical curve, but significantly shrinks the inner shadow and enhances the lensed ring. These results indicate that inner shadow measurements, combined with selected precession observables, may provide complementary probes of Lorentz-violating effects in strong-field gravity.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The breakdown of Lorentz invariance, a potential signature of quantum gravity, offers a window into physics beyond general relativity. Specifically, we study the quantum steering and Bell nonlocality between modes trapped inside and outside the event horizon of an Einstein-Bumblebee black hole. Our analysis demonstrates that quantum steering for an initially correlated state is confined to a narrow region near the event horizon, with the Lorentz-violating parameter further constraining this domain. Notably, the degree of steering asymmetry is significantly modulated by both the distance from the horizon and the Lorentz-violating parameter, with the two spatially separated regions exhibiting opposite trends. Furthermore, the Bell nonlocality measurable by an external observer strengthens with increasing distance from the black hole. These findings confirm the persistence of nonclassical correlations in a Lorentz-violating gravitational background and and offer a novel perspective on the interplay between quantum information and fundamental spacetime symmetries.

*Zi-Qiang Zhao,Mei-Ling Yan,Zhang-Yu Nie,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

TL;DR: 研究全息超流模型中的动力学稳定性与相变行为，该模型包含高阶自相互作用项和最小耦合修正。发现热力学稳定性与动力学稳定性一致，相图分析揭示了丰富的临界和超临界现象，首次报告了由单一参数驱动的双临界现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究包含高阶自相互作用项 $λ|ψ|^4$、$τ|ψ|^6$ 和非最小耦合 $h(ψ)=e^{α|ψ|^2}$ 的全息超流模型中的动力学稳定性和相变行为。探索这些相互作用项如何影响系统的稳定性和相变特性。

Method: 采用热力学稳定性分析和动力学稳定性分析，研究包含高阶自相互作用项和非最小耦合的全息超流模型。通过相图分析探讨不同参数条件下的相变行为。

Result: 热力学稳定性与动力学稳定性一致。相图分析揭示了丰富的临界和超临界现象：固定 $λ<0$ 和 $α$ 时，增加 $τ$ 会缩小一阶相变区域至临界点，然后进入超临界区域。改变 $α$ 时，系统可表现出无临界点，以及首次报告的双临界现象——随着 $α$ 增加，系统先进入超临界区域，然后重新进入一阶相变区域。

Conclusion: 在全息超流模型中首次发现了由单一参数驱动的双临界现象，揭示了非最小耦合与高阶相互作用项之间复杂的非单调耦合效应。这一发现丰富了全息超流模型的相变行为理解。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamical stability and phase transition behavior in a holographic superfluid model incorporating higher-order self-interaction terms $λ|ψ|^4$, $τ|ψ|^6$, and a non-minimal coupling $h(ψ)=e^{α|ψ|^2}$. Thermodynamic and dynamical stability analyzes show that the thermodynamic stability and dynamical stability of the system are consistent. Phase diagram analysis reveals rich critical and supercritical phenomena. For fixed $λ<0$ and $α$, increasing $τ$ shrinks the first-order phase transition region to a critical point and then enters the supercritical region. When varying $α$, the system can exhibit no critical point and, most notably, a double critical phenomenon in which, as $α$ increases, the system first enters the supercritical region and then re-enters the first-order phase transition region. This double critical phenomenon driven by a single parameter is reported for the first time in holographic superfluid models, revealing a complex nonmonotonic coupling effect between the non-minimal coupling and higher-order interaction terms.

</details>


### [63] [Nonlinearities in Gravity: Gravitational Wave Ringdown](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00972)
*Macarena Lagos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文总结了引力波（gravitational wave）铃荡（ringdown）模型中二次效应（quadratic effects）的主要特性和最新进展，这些非线性效应有望被下一代引力波探测器探测到，并为广义相对论（general relativity）提供新的检验方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统引力波铃荡建模主要依赖线性微扰理论（linear perturbation theory），仅能描述黑洞（black hole）受扰后的晚期行为。然而，对更精确铃荡模型的需求推动了对非线性引力效应（nonlinear gravitational effects）的理解。

Method: 论文采用总结性方法，系统梳理了铃荡模型中二次效应的主要特性和最新发展。该方法聚焦于非线性效应在引力波信号建模中的理论进展。

Result: 研究总结了二次效应在铃荡模型中的关键特性，这些非线性效应预计能够被下一代引力波探测器（next-generation gravitational wave detectors）探测到。这将为广义相对论提供新的自洽性检验（consistency tests）。

Conclusion: 二次效应在引力波铃荡建模中具有重要意义，其可探测性将开启对广义相对论的新检验途径。非线性效应的研究对于提高引力波信号建模精度至关重要。

Abstract: The modeling of gravitational wave ringdown has traditionally relied on linear perturbation theory, which mainly describes the late-time behavior of a perturbed black hole after a binary merger. However, the need for more accurate ringdown models has motivated the understanding of nonlinear gravitational effects. In this paper, we summarize the main properties and latest developments of quadratic effects in ringdown models, which are expected to be detectable with next-generation gravitational wave detectors, and will allow for new consistency tests of general relativity.

### [64] [Nonlinear Lattice Framework for Inflation: Bridging stochastic inflation and the $δ{N}$ formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00978)
*Pankaj Saha,Yuichiro Tada,Yuko Urakawa*

Method: 引入基于无剪切局部Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker（FLRW）几何的单场暴胀非线性晶格框架。该方法在均匀密度切片上构建完全非线性的δN可观测量，以及其他实用的时间相关曲率扰动估计量。

Result: 在标准慢滚（slow-roll）机制中验证框架后，应用于Starobinsky线性势模型，该模型具有间歇性超慢滚（ultra-slow-roll, USR）阶段和尖锐势能转变。晶格方法捕捉到曲率扰动估计量的分离、非高斯性（non-Gaussianity）的增长与稳定，以及当暴胀子速度极小时无剪切近似的瞬态弱化。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了刚性背景晶格模拟与完全数值相对论之间的实用中间方法，在晶格方法、δN形式主义和随机暴胀形式主义之间建立了非线性桥梁。

Abstract: Understanding when inflationary perturbations become genuinely nonlinear near the horizon crossing requires methods that go beyond both linear perturbation theory and the gradient expansion. In this work, we introduce a nonlinear lattice framework for single-field inflation based on a shear-free, locally Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker geometry. This approach captures inhomogeneous local expansion rates, curvature contributions to the local Friedmann equation, and proper-volume weighting at a fraction of the computational cost of full numerical relativity. We construct fully nonlinear $δN$ observables on uniform-density slices, together with other practical time-dependent estimators for the curvature perturbations. After validating the framework in a standard slow-roll regime, we apply it to Starobinsky's linear-potential model featuring an intermittent ultra-slow-roll (USR) phase and a sharp potential transition. During this non-attractor USR regime, the lattice captures the separation of curvature perturbation estimators, the growth and subsequent stabilisation of non-Gaussianity, and a transient weakening of the shear-free approximation when the inflaton velocity becomes very small. Our framework provides a practical intermediate approach between rigid background lattice simulations and full numerical relativity, offering a nonlinear bridge between lattice methods, the $δN$ formalism, and the stochastic inflation formalism.

Method: 采用数值计算方法，研究定义在由单个六价顶点（six-valent vertex）形成的自旋网络图（spin network graph）希尔伯特空间上的简单半经典态的时间演化，这些态描述均匀各向同性的空间几何。

Abstract: We compute numerically the time evolution of simple semiclassical states describing homogeneous and isotropic spatial geometries in quantum-reduced loop gravity under a deparametrized formulation of the dynamics, in which a reference matter field is taken as a relational time variable for the dynamics of quantum states of the gravitational field. The states which we consider are defined on the Hilbert space of a spin network graph formed by a single six-valent vertex. We find that the quantum dynamics is generally in close agreement with the semiclassical effective dynamics of a homogeneous and isotropic universe throughout the range of validity of the numerical approximation. In particular, an initial state describing a contracting geometry undergoes a dynamical "bounce", where the contraction is halted and turned into an expansion by the quantum dynamics.

### [66] [Thermodynamics, Shadow, and Quasinormal Modes of AdS Ayón--Beato--García Massive Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01065)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析吉布斯自由能（Gibbs free energy）的极限行为，研究光子球（photon sphere）和阴影（shadow）的几何特征，并计算准正则模（quasinormal mode, QNM）来评估动力学稳定性。

Result: 吉布斯自由能展现出三种极限行为：磁荷为零时退化为AdS大质量黑洞，引力子质量为零时退化为AdS ABG黑洞，渐近区域平滑过渡到AdS大质量Reissner-Nordström情况。引力子质量增加会扩大光子球和阴影半径，而磁荷增加导致收缩。准正则模虚部保持负值，证实了动力学稳定性。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamics, photon sphere, and dynamical stability of an AdS Ayón--Beato--García (ABG) massive black hole with graviton mass and magnetic charge. The Gibbs free energy exhibits distinct limiting behaviors: it reduces to that of an AdS massive black hole when magnetic charge vanishes, to that of an AdS ABG black hole when graviton mass is zero, and smoothly interpolates to the AdS massive Reissner-Nordström case in the asymptotic regime. Furthermore, the photon sphere and shadow analysis indicate that increasing the graviton mass expands their radii, while increasing the magnetic charge causes contraction, in agreement with earlier studies of black hole spacetimes. Quasinormal mode (QNM) calculations further confirm dynamical stability, as the imaginary part remains negative, ensuring decay of perturbations. Additionally, the real part of the frequency decreases with graviton mass, while the imaginary part initially grows before saturating at higher values. Together, these results provide meaningful insights into the interplay between graviton mass, magnetic charge, and stability, thereby enriching the understanding of black holes in modified gravity theories.

Method: 使用非微扰泛函重整化群（non-perturbative functional renormalisation group）方法，在渐近安全范式下分析具有矢量凝聚的广义Proca理论（generalised Proca theories）。该方法用于识别理论中的固定点（fixed points）。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，所得到的紫外临界表面（UV critical surface）对晚期宇宙学（late-time cosmology）具有约束作用，为矢量-张量理论在渐近安全框架下的紫外完备性提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Effective field theories for cosmology offer a powerful framework to investigate the dynamics of space--time and address longstanding open puzzles. In this work, we initiate a programme to analyse the ultraviolet completion of vector--tensor quantum field theories within the asymptotic safety paradigm, focusing on generalised Proca theories with a vector condensate. This enables us to assess whether a consistent fundamental UV completion exists and to constrain the set of viable infrared scenarios. Using the non--perturbative functional renormalisation group, we identify several fixed points, including Proca--type candidates, and, among them, a particularly remarkable one with four relevant directions: two associated with gravity and two induced by matter. This provides evidence for the non--perturbative renormalisability of vector--tensor theories. We further outline how the resulting UV critical surface constrains late--time cosmology.

### [68] [Minimal Length Effects on Keplerian Scattering and Gravitational Lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01177)
*Mykola Samar,Mariia Seniak*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法基于变形海森堡代数（deformed Heisenberg algebra）框架，通过分析哈密顿矢量（Hamilton vector）的进动来探测轨道扰动。哈密顿矢量的进动作为轨道扰动的灵敏探针，用于推导最小长度效应引起的轨迹修正。

Result: 研究结果显示，量子引力修正导致散射角减小。特别地，对于光子等无质量粒子，空间量子化会减弱引力透镜效应（gravitational lensing effect）。利用爱因斯坦环（Einstein ring）观测的实验数据，作者估算了电子和水星的变形参数及相应的最小长度。

Conclusion: 结论指出，这些发现突显了最小长度情景在高能天体物理学和引力光学中的潜在观测特征。研究为通过引力透镜观测探测量子引力效应提供了理论框架和参数估计。

Abstract: We study the impact of a minimal length, implied by generalized uncertainty principles and quantum gravity models, on unbounded (scattering) trajectories in the Kepler problem. The analysis is based on the precession of the Hamilton vector, which serves as a sensitive probe of orbital perturbations. Within the framework of the deformed Heisenberg algebra, we derive the correction to the trajectory arising from minimal length effects. It is shown that these quantum-gravitational corrections lead to a reduction in the scattering angle. In particular, for massless particles such as photons, the quantization of space results in a weakening of the gravitational lensing effect. Using available experimental data from the observation of the Einstein ring, we estimate the deformation parameter and the corresponding minimal length for the electron and Mercury. These findings highlight potential observational signatures of minimal length scenarios in high-energy astrophysics and gravitational optics.

### [69] [Universal $T$-matrices for quantum Poincaré groups: contractions and quantum reference frames](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01058)
*Angel Ballesteros,Diego Fernandez-Silvestre,Ivan Gutierrez-Sagredo*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法包括：重新审视量子群的通用T矩阵（universal T-matrices）或Hopf代数对偶形式（Hopf algebra dual forms）；发展其收缩理论（contraction theory）；首先以(1+1)类时κ-Poincaré T矩阵为例进行具体计算；然后构造新的(1+1)中心扩展Poincaré李代数的量子形变（quantum deformation）。

Abstract: Universal $T$-matrices, or Hopf algebra dual forms, for quantum groups are revisited, and their contraction theory is developed. As a first illustrative example, the (1+1) timelike $κ$-Poincaré $T$-matrix is explicitly worked out. Afterwards, motivated by recent results on the role of the Hopf algebra dual form of a quantum (1+1) centrally extended Galilei group as the algebraic object underlying non-relativistic quantum reference frame transformations, a new quantum deformation of the (1+1) centrally extended Poincaré Lie algebra is obtained, and its universal $T$-matrix is presented. Finally, the Hopf algebra dual form contraction is applied to this Poincaré $T$-matrix, showing that its corresponding non-relativistic counterpart is precisely the Galilei $T$-matrix associated with quantum reference frames. In this way, the Poincaré Hopf algebra dual form introduced here stands as a natural candidate for describing the symmetry structure of relativistic quantum reference frame transformations. In the appropriate basis, the associated quantum Poincaré group is recognized, remarkably, as a non-trivial central extension of the (1+1) spacelike $κ$-Poincaré dual Hopf algebra.

### [70] [Simple spatial processes can generate heterogeneous contact distributions in face-to-face interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00652)
*Juliette Gambaudo,Mathieu Génois*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过添加简单目标机制到二维随机游走模型中，探索了空间约束对人面对面接触模式的影响。研究发现，仅基于空间规则的模型能够重现接触次数的广泛分布，表明观察到的异质性不一定源于社会关系，而可能由局部化阶段和受控群体混合产生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 面对面互动显示出重复模式，表明可能存在共享的底层机制。特别是接触间隔时间、接触持续时间和每条边的接触次数在许多实证环境中都呈现相似的重尾分布。一个常见直觉是，面对面互动可能受到空间约束的影响，观察到的复杂行为可能源于这种物理限制。

Method: 研究通过模拟行人动力学（pedestrian dynamics）来探索空间约束的影响，并研究生成的接触时间网络（temporal network of contacts）。在二维随机游走（two-dimensional random walk）基础上添加简单的目标机制（targeting mechanisms），构建仅基于空间规则的模型。

Result: 这些模型能够重现接触次数（number of contacts）的广泛分布，揭示了两个关键要素的重要性：局部化阶段（localized phases）和受控群体混合（controlled population mixing）。这表明观察到的接触次数异质性不一定源于个体间的社会关系。

Conclusion: 仅基于空间规则的模型能够重现与实证数据相当的接触次数分布，无需记忆机制（memory mechanisms）。这表明面对面互动中的复杂模式可能主要源于空间约束，而非社会关系或记忆效应。

Abstract: Face-to-face interactions reveal recurring patterns, suggesting the possibility of shared underlying mechanisms. More specifically, inter-contact durations, contact durations and number of contacts per edge share similar heavy-tail distributions in many empirical settings. A common intuition is that face-to-face interactions may be influenced by spatial constraints, and that the observed complex behaviors could arise from such physical limitations. Our models explore the impact of this constraint by simulating pedestrian dynamics, and studying the generated temporal network of contacts. Previous work showed that the inter-contact duration distribution is recovered with a pedestrian dynamic as simple as the two dimensional random walk, but this approach doesn't allow to recover the distribution of the number of times a pair of individuals has been in contact. One assumption is that the number of contact between individual arises from the social relationship between them, in other words a memory of past interactions. However, we here present models that are based on solely spatial rules, by adding simple targeting mechanisms to the two-dimensional random walk. We show that these models allow to recover a broad distribution of the number of contacts, revealing the importance of two ingredients: localized phases and controlled population mixing. This suggests that the observed heterogeneity in the contact numbers within the data does not necessarily emerge from underlying social relationships between individuals, since an equivalent distribution may be reproduced using a purely spatially based model, without the need for memory mechanisms.

</details>


### [71] [Message passing and cyclicity transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01201)
*Takayuki Hiraoka*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 该研究澄清了渗流（percolation）问题中消息传递（message passing）框架的数学解释，指出传统上认为消息传递解对应巨连通分量（giant component）概率的解读实际上识别的是从环（cycles）出发的可达性（reachability）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 消息传递（message passing）或信念传播（belief propagation）是分析网络模型的多功能框架，但其在渗流（percolation）问题中的解释仍然模糊不清。研究旨在澄清消息传递解在渗流中的确切数学意义。

Method: 通过理论分析，重新解释消息传递框架在渗流问题中的数学解。该方法适用于任意无向或有向网络上的键渗流（bond percolation）和点渗流（site percolation）。

Result: 研究发现，传统上认为消息传递解对应巨连通分量（giant component）概率的解读实际上识别的是从环（cycles）出发的可达性（reachability）。这一解释揭示了环性（cyclicity）转变与巨连通分量出现之间的区别。

Conclusion: 研究强调了环性（cyclicity）转变与巨连通分量（giant component）出现之间的重要区别，为渗流问题中消息传递框架提供了更精确的数学解释。

Abstract: Message passing, also known as belief propagation, is a versatile framework for analyzing models defined on networks. Its most prototypical application is percolation; yet, the interpretation of the message passing formulation of percolation remains elusive. We show that the message passing solutions commonly associated with the probability of belonging to the giant component actually identify reachability from cycles. This interpretation applies to bond and site percolation on arbitrary undirected or directed networks. Our findings emphasize the distinction between transition in cyclicity and the emergence of the giant component.

</details>

### [72] [Crystals Caught Doping: Metallic Wigner Crystals in Rhombohedral Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00114)
*Junkai Dong,Tomohiro Soejima,Daniel E. Parker,Ashvin Vishwanath*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了当共格（commensurate）维格纳晶体（Wigner crystal）自发掺杂并产生巡游载流子时，会形成非共格（incommensurate）金属维格纳晶体（metallic Wigner crystal, MWC）。研究建立了共格晶体不稳定性的通用判据，并将其应用于菱面体多层石墨烯（rhombohedral multilayer graphene），揭示了其相图中存在与绝缘维格纳晶体相相邻的宽MWC相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 维格纳晶体（electron crystals）是当前实验和理论研究的焦点，但大多数已提出的晶体相是共格的（commensurate），在弱钉扎（pinning）下会变为绝缘体。本研究旨在探讨共格维格纳晶体何时会自发掺杂并发展出巡游载流子，从而形成非共格的金属维格纳晶体（MWC）。

Method: 研究首先建立了一个关于共格晶体不稳定性的通用判据，该判据涉及共格时的电荷能隙（charge gap）与"堆积偏好"（packing bias）之间的竞争。随后将该理论应用于菱面体多层石墨烯，对共格晶体进行计算以揭示其自发掺杂的不稳定性，并通过在非共格晶体构型空间中进行自洽哈特里-福克（self-consistent Hartree-Fock）计算来揭示相图。

Result: 计算揭示了菱面体多层石墨烯中，共格晶体存在向自发掺杂的不稳定性。相图显示，一个宽广的金属维格纳晶体（MWC）相直接与一个绝缘维格纳晶体相相邻。该理论自然地解释了近期在菱面体石墨烯中，在推测的维格纳晶体相附近观察到的反常霍尔电导（reversed Hall conductance）区域。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了共格维格纳晶体向金属态转变的通用理论框架，并成功应用于菱面体多层石墨烯体系，解释了其实验观测现象。研究结果表明，通过自发掺杂机制，绝缘的共格维格纳晶体可以转变为非共格的金属维格纳晶体，为理解强关联电子体系中的金属-绝缘体转变提供了新视角。

Abstract: Nearly a century after Wigner's initial proposal, electron crystals are now a topic of intense experimental and theoretical interest. However, most proposed crystalline phases are commensurate and therefore become insulating in the presence of even weak pinning. In this work we discuss when a commensurate Wigner crystal will spontaneously self dope and develop itinerant carriers, giving rise to an incommensurate and thus metallic Wigner crystal (MWC). We develop a general criterion for the instability of the commensurate crystal which involves the competition between the charge gap at commensurability and a ``packing bias'' whose sign selects whether electron or hole doping is preferred. We then apply these insights to rhombohedral multilayer graphene, where calculations for commensurate crystals reveal instabilities towards self-doping. Carrying out self-consistent Hartree-Fock over the landscape of incommensurate crystals reveals the phase diagram, where a broad MWC phase appears directly adjacent to an insulating Wigner crystal phase. Recent observations of an island of reversed Hall conductance near a putative Wigner crystal phase in rhombohedral graphene are naturally explained by our theory.

</details>


### [73] [Lieb-Schultz-Mattis Anomalies and Anomaly Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00347)
*Liujun Zou,Meng Cheng*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文是一篇关于Lieb-Schultz-Mattis（LSM）异常及其匹配机制的综述性论文，系统介绍了LSM异常在量子多体系统中的对称性约束作用及其在不同维度、系统类型中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LSM异常是基于对称性的强大约束条件，对量子多体系统的关联、纠缠和动力学具有重要影响。本文旨在全面综述各类LSM异常及其匹配机制，为相关研究提供系统性的理论框架。

Method: 采用综述性方法，首先从量子自旋链（quantum spin chains）的教学性介绍入手，然后将讨论推广到更高维度和其他系统类型。涵盖标准LSM异常相关主题，并扩展到无序系统、费米子系统等特殊情形。

Result: 系统梳理了LSM异常在不同维度（从一维到高维）和不同系统（包括无序系统、费米子系统）中的表现形式。特别指出在对称短程纠缠态可能但必须是非平凡对称保护拓扑相（symmetry-protected topological phases）的系统中的LSM异常特征。

Conclusion: LSM异常作为基于对称性的约束机制，在量子多体系统的理论研究中具有广泛适用性。该综述为理解LSM异常在不同物理系统中的作用提供了全面框架，并指出了其在无序系统、费米子系统等扩展领域的研究价值。

Abstract: Lieb-Schultz-Mattis (LSM) anomalies are powerful symmetry-based constraints on the correlation, entanglement and dynamics of quantum many-body systems. In this review, we discuss various LSM anomalies and anomaly matching. We start with a pedagogical introduction to these subjects in quantum spin chains, and then generalize the discussion to higher dimensions and other systems. Besides covering the topics related to the standard LSM anomalies, we also review LSM anomalies in disordered systems where the lattice symmetries are only preserved on average, fermionic systems, and systems where the symmetric short-range entangled states are possible but must be nontrivial symmetry-protected topological phases.

</details>


### [74] [The $\mathbb{Z}_N^{\times 3}$ symmetry protected boundary modes in two-dimensional Potts paramagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00910)
*Hrant Topchyan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究构建并分析了一类源于二维对称保护拓扑相的一维边界哈密顿量，揭示了边界理论结构与N的算术性质之间的深刻联系，并展示了非在位、反常的对称性实现方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解二维对称保护拓扑相（symmetry-protected topological phases）在边界上的物理表现，特别是针对具有$\mathbb{Z}_N^{\times 3}$对称性的三角晶格系统，探索边界模式的理论结构及其与全局对称性的关系。

Method: 采用基于上同调（cohomology-based）的变换方法，从二维晶格模型显式推导出一维边界哈密顿量。通过分析N的算术性质（质数与合数），研究边界理论的不同代数结构，包括Temperley-Lieb代数和分层/因子化结构。

Result: 对于质数N，边界理论可用相互对易的Temperley-Lieb代数描述；对于合数N，模型呈现分层或因子化结构。所有相均可通过主模型（primary models）增强局部缺陷自由度来理解，这些缺陷将系统划分为独立片段。全局对称性在边界上通过投影表示（projective representation）以非在位（non-on-site）且反常的方式实现，直接体现了相应的't Hooft反常。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了二维对称保护拓扑相边界理论结构与N算术性质之间的系统对应关系，揭示了边界对称性实现的非在位和反常特性，为理解拓扑相的边界物理提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We construct and analyze a class of one-dimensional boundary Hamiltonians arising from two-dimensional symmetry-protected topological phases with $\mathbb{Z}_N^{\times 3}$ symmetry on a triangular lattice. Using a cohomology-based transformation, the lattice models for the edge modes are explicitly obtained, and their structure is shown to be governed by the arithmetic properties of $N$. For prime $N$, the boundary theory admits a formulation in terms of mutually commuting Temperley-Lieb algebras. For the composite values of $N$, the models exhibit hierarchical or factorized structures. We demonstrate that all phases can be understood in terms of primary models augmented by local defect degrees of freedom that partition the system into independent segments. Finally, the global symmetry is realized on the boundary in a non-on-site and anomalous manner via a projective representation, directly realizing the corresponding 't Hooft anomaly.

</details>


### [75] [Magnetoelectric Control of Toroidal Moment in Ferroaxial Crystal PbMn$_{2}$Ni$_{6}$Te$_{3}$O$_{18}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00526)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁性多极序（ferroic multipole orders）破坏某些对称性并常激活独特的物理性质，如非互易方向二色性（nonreciprocal directional dichroism）和线性磁电效应（linear magnetoelectric effects）。研究旨在探索控制磁环矩取向的方法，并理解其与晶体铁轴矩和磁电单极子的耦合机制。

Method: 通过在两种不同构型中施加电场和磁场来控制PbMn₂Ni₆Te₃O₁₈中的磁环矩取向。利用方向二色性技术成功可视化磁铁环畴，从而建立磁环矩、晶体铁轴矩和磁电单极子之间的内在耦合关系。

Conclusion: 该研究不仅提出了控制磁环矩的有效途径，还为研究铁轴序（ferroaxial ordering）提供了新颖方法。这些发现对于开发基于多极序的新型功能材料和器件具有重要意义。

Abstract: Ferroic multipole orders break some symmetry and often activate unique physical properties, such as nonreciprocal directional dichroism and linear magnetoelectric effects. Here, we demonstrate the control of magnetic toroidal orientation in PbMn$_{2}$Ni$_{6}$Te$_{3}$O$_{18}$ through the application of electric and magnetic fields in two distinct configurations. Through directional dichroism, we successfully visualize magnetic ferrotoroidic domains, establishing the intrinsic coupling among magnetic toroidal moment, crystallographic ferroaxial moment, and magnetoelectric monopoles. Our findings not only present an effective pathway for controlling magnetic toroidal moment but also provide a novel approach for investigating ferroaxial ordering.

### [76] [Excitations across the equilibrium and photoinduced `hidden' states of magnetoresistive manganites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00991)
*Shiyu Fan,Feng Jin,Taehun Kim,Umesh Kumar,Zixun Zhang,Vivek Bhartiya,Jiemin Li,Brandon Yalin,Yanhong Gu,Mingqiang Gu,Wen Hu,Claudio Mazzoli,G. Lawrence Carr,Osor S. Barišić,Andrey S. Mishchenko,Valentina Bisogni,Sobhit Singh,Wenbin Wu,Jonathan Pelliciari*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过超快激光激发结合原位输运、X射线吸收和共振非弹性X射线散射技术，揭示了La₂/₃Ca₁/₃MnO₃（LCMO）中光诱导"隐藏相"的激发特性，建立了极化子相图并识别了各相的光谱特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: "隐藏相"（hidden phases）因其长寿命（数小时至数周）和可逆性而具有技术应用潜力。LCMO材料因其可通过外延应变（epitaxial strain）调控从铁磁金属（FMM）转变为反铁磁绝缘体（AFI），且对光诱导转变敏感，成为研究光诱导相变的理想体系。

Method: 研究结合近红外超快光激发（ultrafast photo-excitation）与原位输运测量、X射线吸收谱（XAS）和共振非弹性X射线散射（RIXS）技术，系统研究了LCMO光激发相的激发特性（极化子、声子和轨道激发），并与通过应变和温度调控的热力学相进行对比。

Result: 在热力学区域，研究建立了极化子与输运性质的相关性，将其置于Holstein模型的"强耦合"（strong coupling）区域。光激发LCMO-AFI产生长寿命相，其特征包括极化子激发软化、Jahn-Teller畸变部分抑制，以及几乎不变的声子谱，表明存在平衡相图中未出现的光激发态。通过调控温度、外延应变和光激发通量，构建了极化子相图并识别了各相的关键光谱特征。

Conclusion: 该激光-RIXS方法为非频闪条件下探索量子材料中的光诱导"隐藏相"建立了一个多功能平台，揭示了光激发态在平衡相图之外的独特性质，为理解光诱导相变机制提供了新见解。

Abstract: "Hidden" phases, generated using ultrafast laser pulses (few hundred femtoseconds), with properties distinct from thermodynamic equilibrium, are appealing for technologies because they can be long-lived, with lifetimes of hours or weeks, and reversible with temperature sweeping or extra pulses. In this regard, La$_{2/3}$Ca$_{1/3}$MnO$_3$ (LCMO) stands out due to its tunability through epitaxial strain, which can drive the bulk ferromagnetic metal (FMM) into an antiferromagnetic insulator (AFI), and its susceptibility to photo-induced transitions. Indeed, AFI LCMO displays a long-lived photo-induced transition into a putative 'hidden' phase whose exact nature and excitations are still largely unknown. Here, we combine ultrafast photo-excitation in the near infrared with in situ transport, x-ray absorption (XAS), and Resonant Inelastic X-ray Scattering (RIXS) to investigate the excitations (polarons, phonons, and orbital) of the photo-excited phase of LCMO and contrast them with the thermodynamic phases achieved through strain and temperature. In the thermodynamic regime, we establish the correlation between polarons and transport, placing them in the 'strong coupling' regime of the Holstein model. Upon photo-excitation of LCMO-AFI, we uncover a long-lived phase characterized by the softening of the polaron excitations, the partial suppression of the Jahn-Teller distortion, and nearly unchanged phonons, showing the emergence of a photo-excited state absent in the equilibrium phase diagram. Finally, by varying temperature, epitaxial strain, and photo-excitation fluence, we construct a polaron phase diagram and identify the key spectroscopic signatures of each phase. Our laser-RIXS approach establishes a versatile platform for exploring photo-induced 'hidden' phases in quantum materials in non-stroboscopic conditions.

</details>


### [77] [The multichannel Dyson equation for double ionisation spectroscopies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01085)
*Pierre Sellié,J. Arjan Berger,Pina Romaniello*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种超越随机相位近似（RPA）的多通道Dyson方程方法，用于准确描述光电子能谱中的准粒子（quasiparticles）和卫星峰（satellites）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法使用随机相位近似（random phase approximation, RPA）模拟涉及双电离过程的光电子能谱（如俄歇光谱），但只能描述准粒子特征而无法捕捉卫星峰结构。

Method: 采用多通道Dyson方程（multichannel Dyson equation），将粒子-粒子二体格林函数（particle-particle two-body Green's function）与四体格林函数的3空穴-1电子（3-hole-1-electron）和3电子-1空穴（3-electron-1-hole）通道耦合。

Result: 该方法能够超越RPA近似，以直接的方式纳入更高级的相关性，从而同时描述光电子能谱中的准粒子和卫星峰特征。

Conclusion: 多通道Dyson方程方法为涉及双电离过程的光电子能谱模拟提供了超越标准RPA近似的有效框架，能够全面描述光谱特征。

Abstract: Several photoemission spectroscopies and, in particular, Auger spectroscopy, involve double-ionization processes. For the numerical simulation of these spectroscopies it is convenient to use the particle-particle channel of the two-body Green's functions since its poles correspond to excitation energies in which the final state has two more particles (holes or electrons) than the initial state. In standard approaches it is approximated within the random phase approximation. As a consequence only the quasiparticles of the photoemission spectrum are captured but none of the satellites features. In this work, we go beyond this approximation by employing the multichannel Dyson equation. By coupling the particle-particle two-body Green's function to the 3-hole-1-electron and 3-electron-1-hole channels of the four-body Green's function, the multichannel Dyson equation incorporates correlations beyond the RPA in a straightforward way. We are thus able to describe both quasiparticles and satellites in the photoemission spectra.

</details>


### [78] [Electronic structure and correlation of La$_4$Co$_2$NiO$_8$Cl$_2$: a theoretical proposal for a La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$-like high-temperature superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01223)
*Si-Yong Jia,Jing-Xuan Wang,Jian-Hong She,Rong-Qiang He,Zhong-Yi Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究基于双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇的高温超导发现，提出并研究了一种类似La₄Ni₃O₁₀结构的钴基材料La₄Co₂NiO₈Cl₂，通过电子掺杂和DFT+DMFT计算，发现其具有与高压下La₄Ni₃O₁₀相似的结构和强关联电子结构，可能具备高温超导潜力。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用密度泛函理论结合动力学平均场理论（DFT+DMFT）方法，对高压下的三层钴酸盐La₄Co₃O₁₀进行电子掺杂研究，分析新化合物La₄Co₂NiO₈Cl₂的晶体结构和电子结构特性。

Result: 计算结果表明，新化合物La₄Co₂NiO₈Cl₂展现出与高压下La₄Ni₃O₁₀相似的晶体结构和强关联电子结构（strongly correlated electronic structure）。这种结构相似性暗示该新材料可能具备高温超导特性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过电子掺杂高压三层钴酸盐La₄Co₃O₁₀获得的新化合物La₄Co₂NiO₈Cl₂，其结构和电子特性与已知高温超导材料La₄Ni₃O₁₀相似，因此可能成为潜在的高温超导体候选材料。

Abstract: Based on the discovery of high-temperature superconductivity in the bilayer nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$, several Co-based La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$-like materials were theoretically predicted as possible high-temperature superconductors by electron doping. Motivated by these findings and the subsequent discovery of superconductivity in the trilayer nickelate La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$ under high pressure, we propose and investigate a Co-based La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$-like material. With electron doping to the high-pressure trilayer cobaltate La$_4$Co$_3$O$_{10}$, using density functional theory combined with dynamical mean-field theory (DFT+DMFT), we find that the resulting compound La$_4$Co$_2$NiO$_8$Cl$_2$ exhibits a crystal structure and a strongly correlated electronic structure similar to those of La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$ under high pressure. This suggests that this new compound may host high-temperature superconductivity.

</details>

### [79] [Gradient systems and asymmetric relaxations in view of Riemannian geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00192)
*Alessandro Bravetti,Miguel Ángel García Ariza,José Roberto Romero-Arias*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文扩展了Amari在信息几何中的研究，将梯度流与预测地线的关系从对偶平坦流形推广到一般黎曼流形，并应用于高斯链弛豫过程的分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Amari在信息几何中建立了对偶平坦流形中梯度流与预测地线之间的深刻联系，本文旨在将这一关系推广到更一般的几何框架中。

Method: 研究在一般黎曼流形中建立梯度下降曲线与预测地线的关系，不要求联络的平坦性或非度量张量的对称性，从而超越Hessian流形的限制。

Result: 提出了比较函数沿两条不同梯度下降曲线弛豫的准则，该准则基于使梯度曲线成为预测地线的联络的非度量张量，并应用于高斯链弛豫过程。

Conclusion: 研究恢复了"升温比降温更快"的普遍不对称性结果，表明源于Amari传统的几何见解为优化问题和随机过程提供了新的视角。

Abstract: In dually flat manifolds, there is a deep connection between gradient flows and pregeodesics. This was one of the many important contributions of Amari to information geometry. In this paper, we extend the study of this relationship to general Riemannian manifolds. Our result does not impose conditions of flatness on the connection or symmetry on its non-metricity tensor, thus broadening the geometric setting beyond Hessian manifolds. Within this framework, we provide a criterion for comparing relaxation along two different gradient descent curves of a function, formulated in terms of the non-metricity tensor of a connection for which the gradient curves are pregeodesics. We use it to study Gaussian chains, whose relaxation trajectories coincide with gradient descent curves in the space of Gaussian distributions.Thus, we recover a recent result that establishes a universal asymmetry: warming up is faster than cooling down. Our work illustrates how geometric insights rooted in Amari's legacy offer new perspectives for optimization problems and stochastic processes.

</details>

### [80] [Observation of Floquet erratic non-Hermitian skin effect in photonic mesh lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00088)
*Yeyang Sun,Shu Yang,Yi Yang*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验揭示了无序驱动的非厄米趋肤效应（erratic non-Hermitian skin effect, ENHSE），这是一种边界无关、本质体态的趋肤局域化现象。利用可编程增益、损耗和相位调制的时序复用光子网格晶格，实现了全局互易性可调的非厄米系统，观测到无序驱动的拓扑相变，并展示了ENHSE与安德森局域化（Anderson localization）的竞争关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统有序平移不变非厄米系统中的趋肤效应（skin effect）被理解为边界现象，而非互易性跳跃驱动本征态向边缘的广泛积累。本研究旨在探索无序驱动的、边界无关的、本质体态的趋肤局域化现象，即最近预测的紊乱非厄米趋肤效应（erratic non-Hermitian skin effect, ENHSE）。

Method: 采用时序复用光子网格晶格（time-multiplexed photonic mesh lattice）平台，通过可编程增益、损耗和相位调制，工程化空间涨落的虚规范场（imaginary gauge fields）。实现了Floquet非厄米晶格，其全局互易性（global reciprocity）可在强局域非互易性条件下独立调节。进一步引入可控的现场无序（on-site disorder）来研究ENHSE与安德森局域化的竞争关系。

Result: 实验观测到无序驱动的非厄米拓扑相变，两个相反方向的紊乱趋肤相通过全局互易性临界点相互转换。在相变点，边界趋肤积累消失，但波动力学自组织成无界面的体局域化模式，直接证明了ENHSE的存在。测量到的局域化轮廓与模拟结果一致，并展现出不同本征态共享由无序虚规范场决定的共同体局域化包络的特征。进一步研究表明，增加散射会逐步抑制紊乱趋肤动力学。

Conclusion: 该研究帮助确立了ENHSE作为一种独特的无序诱导非厄米现象，为超越传统布洛赫（Bloch）和基于边界范式的局域化、输运和拓扑工程开辟了新途径。实验结果展示了无序在非厄米系统中诱导新型体局域化现象的能力。

Abstract: In ordered, translationally invariant non-Hermitian systems, the skin effect is understood as a boundary phenomenon: nonreciprocal hopping drives an extensive accumulation of eigenstates towards the edges, whereas the periodic-boundary spectrum remains Bloch extended. Here we experimentally reveal the opposite limit -- a disorder-enabled, boundary-independent, and intrinsically bulk form of skin localization -- the recently predicted erratic non-Hermitian skin effect (ENHSE), realized in a driven photonic platform. Using a time-multiplexed photonic mesh lattice with programmable gain, loss, and phase modulation, we engineer spatially fluctuating imaginary gauge fields and realize a Floquet non-Hermitian lattice whose global reciprocity can be tuned independently of strong local nonreciprocity. We observe a disorder-driven non-Hermitian topological transition between two oppositely directed disordered skin phases through a critical point of global reciprocity. At this transition, boundary skin accumulation disappears, yet the wave dynamics self-organizes into bulk-localized patterns without any interface, providing direct evidence of ENHSE. The measured localization profiles agree with simulations and exhibit the defining feature that distinct eigenstates share a common bulk-localized envelope determined by the disordered imaginary gauge fields. By further introducing controllable on-site disorder, we reveal the competition between ENHSE and Anderson localization, and show how increasing scattering progressively suppresses erratic skin dynamics. Our results help establish ENHSE as a unique disorder-induced non-Hermitian phenomenon and open a route to engineering localization, transport, and topology beyond conventional Bloch and boundary-based paradigms.

</details>


### [81] [Fractal hierarchy enables exponential scaling of topological boundary states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00814)
*Limin Song,Zhichan Hu,Ziteng Wang,Domenico Bongiovanni,Liqin Tang,Daohong Song,Roberto Morandotti,Jingjun Xu,Hrvoje Buljan,Zhigang Chen*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合长程周期序与自相似分形层级的新型晶格结构，实现了拓扑边界态数量的指数级增长。通过科赫曲线和谢尔宾斯基垫片两种分形单元构建的晶格，展示了边界态数量与拓扑微带隙数量随分形代数的指数缩放规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 指数增长是数学和物理、生物、技术系统中普遍存在的快速过程。本研究旨在探索如何通过分形层级结构控制拓扑边界态的多样性，揭示拓扑、自相似几何与周期序之间的相互作用。

Method: 引入一类受分形启发的晶格，结合长程周期序与自相似层级结构。具体构建了两种晶格：(i) 基于科赫曲线（Koch-curve）单元构建的准一维晶格链；(ii) 基于谢尔宾斯基垫片（Sierpinski-gasket）单元构建的二维周期铺砌晶格。采用多拓扑相理论分析，并在激光直写光子晶格中进行了实验验证。

Result: 在合适的耦合参数下，拓扑边界态数量$N_{\ell}$和拓扑微带隙（minigaps）数量$M_{\ell}$均随分形代数（fractal generation index）$\ell$呈指数增长。发现$N_{\ell}$是$M_{\ell}$的整数倍，该整数由底层对称性决定。这一层级缩放规律被多拓扑相理论所描述，并在实验中得到证实。

Conclusion: 分形层级被确立为控制边界态多样性的材料架构原理，揭示了拓扑、自相似几何与周期序之间的相互作用。这项工作为合成材料和集成光子平台提供了一条新途径，可在紧凑架构中设计大量鲁棒边界模式。

Abstract: Exponential growth describes an extremely rapid process ubiquitous across mathematics and diverse physical, biological, and technological systems. Here, we introduce a class of fractal-inspired lattices that combine long-range periodic order with self-similar hierarchy, establishing a structural motif that enables exponential scaling of topological boundary states. We demonstrate this phenomenon in (i) a quasi-one-dimensional lattice chain constructed from Koch-curve unit cells and (ii) a two-dimensional periodic tiling lattice composed of Sierpinski-gasket unit cells. We show that, for suitable coupling parameters, both the number of topological boundary states $N_{\ell}$ and the number of topological minigaps $M_{\ell}$ grow exponentially with the fractal generation index $\ell$. We find that $N_{\ell}$ is an integer multiple of $M_{\ell}$, with the integer determined by the underlying symmetry. This hierarchical scaling law is captured by multi-topological-phase theory and confirmed experimentally in laser-written photonic lattices. Our results identify fractal hierarchy as a materials architecture principle for controlling boundary-state multiplicity, revealing an interplay between topology, self-similar geometry, and periodic order. More broadly, this work suggests a route to synthetic materials and integrated photonic platforms in which large numbers of robust boundary modes can be engineered within compact architectures.

</details>

### [82] [Emergent Weyl Nodes and Berry Curvature in Bose Polarons via $p$-Wave Feshbach Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00797)
*Hiroyuki Tajima,Eiji Nakano,Kei Iida*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了玻色极化子（Bose polaron）在p波Feshbach共振下展现的非平凡拓扑性质，包括非零贝里曲率和外尔节点，这些特性可在冷原子实验中通过杂质云的霍尔输运观测验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索浸没在玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中的杂质准粒子（即玻色极化子）的拓扑特性，特别是关注在p波Feshbach共振条件下产生的非平凡拓扑结构。

Method: 通过理论分析表明，在种间p波Feshbach共振条件下，玻色极化子系统中会涌现出外尔节点（Weyl nodes），从而诱导产生非零贝里曲率（nonzero Berry curvature）。

Result: 研究发现玻色极化子展现出拓扑特性，其特征是非零贝里曲率，这些特性由p波Feshbach共振产生的外尔节点所诱导，且无需自旋自由度或自旋轨道耦合即可出现。

Conclusion: 对于带电杂质，相应的p波极化子伴随手征反常（chiral anomaly），这些理论预测可在冷原子环境中通过观测原子或离子杂质云的霍尔输运（Hall transport）进行实验验证。

Abstract: We show that an impurity quasiparticle immersed in a Bose-Einstein condensate, known as a Bose polaron, exhibits topological properties characterized by a nonzero Berry curvature, which is induced by Weyl nodes that emerge via interspecies $p$-wave Feshbach resonance. Such nodes occur even in the absence of spin degrees of freedom and spin-orbit coupling. For charged impurities, the corresponding $p$-wave polarons are shown to be accompanied by chiral anomaly. The above predictions can be tested in a cold atomic environment by observing the Hall transport of the atomic or ionic impurity cloud.

</details>


### [83] [Nonequilibrium phase transition of dissipative fermionic superfluids: Case study of multi-terminal Josephson junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00574)
*Soma Takemori,Kazuki Yamamoto*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了三个费米子超流体通过约瑟夫森结连接的非平衡动力学，分析了其中一个超流体中突然开启二体损耗后的演化。研究发现超流序参数会发生相位旋转，产生三种直流约瑟夫森电流，并观察到不同隧穿强度下非平衡动力学相变的两种不同模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索多体量子系统中耗散诱导的非平衡动力学，特别是三个费米子超流体通过约瑟夫森结连接时，其中一个超流体中突然开启二体损耗（two-body loss）后的演化行为。

Method: 研究方法基于林德布拉德方程（Lindblad equation）的耗散BCS理论（dissipative BCS theory），通过理论建模分析三个超流体之间的约瑟夫森结（Josephson junctions）动力学。同时采用简化模型进行解析研究以支持主要发现。

Result: 研究发现超流序参数（superfluid order parameter）表现出相位旋转，产生三种对应于不同结的直流约瑟夫森电流（dc Josephson currents）。当无损耗超流体间隧穿振幅$V_{31}$较弱时，观察到两步非平衡动力学相变（nonequilibrium dynamical phase transition, NDPT），耗散首先使一个直流约瑟夫森电流变为有限值，进一步增加耗散则使该电流消失。当$V_{31}$较强时，耗散诱导所有直流约瑟夫森电流同时消失的相变。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，在三个费米子超流体系统中，耗散可以诱导不同类型的非平衡动力学相变，具体模式取决于超流体间的隧穿强度。解析研究进一步支持了这一观察结果，揭示了多体量子系统中耗散与相干动力学之间的复杂相互作用。

Abstract: We investigate nonequilibrium dynamics of a triad of fermionic superfluids connected via Josephson junctions, following sudden switch-on of two-body loss in one of the three superfluids. By formulating the dissipative BCS theory for the Lindblad equation, we find that the superfluid order parameter exhibits a phase rotation, thereby giving rise to three types of dc Josephson currents corresponding to different junctions. We demonstrate that, when the tunneling amplitude $V_{31}$ between superfluids without two-body loss is weak, two-step nonequilibrium dynamical phase transition (NDPT) characterized by the vanishing dc Josephson currents occurs: dissipation first induces the NDPT by making one dc Josephson current finite, while further increasing dissipation makes this remaining dc Josephson current vanish. By contrast, when $V_{31}$ is strong, dissipation induces the NDPT in which all dc Josephson currents simultaneously vanish. An analytical study based on a simplified model further supports this observation.

</details>


### [84] [Ground-state solution of quantum droplets in Bose-Bose mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00889)
*Wei Liu,Limin Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了同核玻色-玻色混合物中量子液滴的基态计算，通过带Lee-Huang-Yang修正的扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程描述自束缚液滴的形成，开发了高效的梯度流离散化方案，并获得了三个主要数值发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于系统分析同核玻色-玻色混合物中量子液滴的基态计算问题，该体系由带Lee-Huang-Yang修正的扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程描述，能够捕捉由吸引平均场相互作用与排斥量子涨落之间微妙平衡所稳定的自束缚液滴形成。

Method: 方法包括：为一般双组分系统和约化的单组分密度锁定模型建立无量纲能量泛函；为高效计算基态，适配并基准测试多种梯度流离散化方案，确定基于拉格朗日乘子法的梯度流向后-向前正弦伪谱方案作为稳健求解器。

Result: 主要数值结果包括：密度锁定模型被定量验证为基态性质的可靠近似；在强耦合区域建立了Thomas-Fermi近似的维度依赖收敛率；数值确定了自由空间中自束缚的临界粒子数，为Petrov的分析预测提供了精确修正。

Conclusion: 结论表明，所开发的GFLM-BFSP方案是稳健的数值求解器，密度锁定模型可作为有效近似，Thomas-Fermi近似收敛率具有维度依赖性，且数值确定的临界粒子数修正了现有理论预测。

Abstract: In this paper, we present a systematic study on the ground state computation of quantum droplets in homonuclear Bose-Bose mixtures, governed by the extended Gross-Pitaevskii equations (eGPEs) with Lee-Huang-Yang (LHY) corrections. This model captures the formation of self-bound droplets stabilized by the delicate balance between the attractive mean-field interaction and the repulsive quantum fluctuations. We formulate dimensionless energy functionals for both the general two-component system and the reduced single-component density-locked model. To compute the ground states efficiently, we adapt and benchmark various gradient flow discretization schemes, identifying a backward-forward sine-pseudospectral scheme based on the gradient flow with Lagrange multiplier method (GFLM-BFSP) as the robust solver for our simulations. Utilizing this method, we report three main numerical observations: (i) the density-locked model is quantitatively validated as a reliable approximation for ground state properties; (ii) the dimension-dependent convergence rates of the Thomas-Fermi approximation are established in the strong-coupling regime; and (iii) the critical particle number for self-binding in free space is numerically determined, providing a precise correction to the analytical prediction by Petrov [Phys. Rev. Lett. 115, 155302 (2015)].

</details>

### [85] [Quantum ergodicity in the Benjamini--Schramm limit for locally symmetric spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01075)
*Farrell Brumley,Simon Marshall,Jasmin Matz,Carsten Peterson*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 该论文证明，对于几乎所有对称空间（symmetric spaces）$X$，以及任何满足一致离散（uniformly discrete）、具有一致谱间隙（uniform spectral gap）、并以Benjamini-Schramm意义收敛于$X$的紧致局部对称空间（compact locally symmetric spaces）序列$Y_n$，其所有不变微分算子（invariant differential operators）的联合特征函数（joint eigenfunctions）在平均意义上会去局域化（delocalize on average），前提是这些特征函数的谱参数（spectral parameters）位于固定的谱窗口（spectral window）内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在理解紧致局部对称空间序列上不变微分算子的联合特征函数的局域化行为。当序列以Benjamini-Schramm意义收敛到其通用覆盖对称空间时，研究者希望探究特征函数在谱参数位于固定窗口内的平均去局域化现象。

Method: 论文采用数学证明方法，针对满足特定条件的对称空间$X$和紧致局部对称空间序列$Y_n$进行分析。这些条件包括序列的一致离散性、一致谱间隙的存在性，以及Benjamini-Schramm收敛性。研究聚焦于所有不变微分算子的联合特征函数在固定谱窗口内的平均行为。

Result: 主要结果是证明了对于几乎所有对称空间$X$，以及满足上述条件的序列$Y_n$，当谱参数位于固定谱窗口内时，联合特征函数在平均意义上会去局域化。这意味着特征函数的质量不会集中在空间的任何小区域内，而是均匀分布。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了在Benjamini-Schramm收敛框架下，紧致局部对称空间序列上不变微分算子的联合特征函数的平均去局域化性质。这一结论深化了对对称空间上特征函数局域化行为的理解，并为相关数学领域提供了新的理论结果。

Abstract: We prove that for almost all symmetric spaces $X$ and for any sequence of compact locally symmetric spaces $Y_n$ which is uniformly discrete, has a uniform spectral gap, and converges in the sense of Benjamini--Schramm to $X$, the joint eigenfunctions of all invariant differential operators on $Y_n$ delocalize on average when their spectral parameters are taken to lie in a fixed spectral window.

</details>

### [86] [Distinct transverse-response signatures of retained-spin, eliminated-spin, and polynomial Burnett-type surrogate closures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00177)
*Satori Tsuzuki*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该研究通过横向线性响应分析，区分了不可压缩流动中高曲率观测量的三种产生机制：显式内部旋转、快速自旋变量的消除以及多项式高阶梯度闭合。研究比较了四种闭合模型，并通过多粒子事件驱动模拟验证了保留自旋动力学相对于瞬时绝热消除的优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不可压缩流动中的高曲率观测量（如$k^4$加权谱）可通过多种机制产生，包括显式内部旋转、快速自旋变量的消除以及多项式高阶梯度闭合。这些机制在动力学上是否可区分，以及如何通过实验观测进行鉴别，是本研究的主要动机。

Method: 基于从Boltzmann-Curtiss方程推导的保留自旋微极性闭合，研究在横向线性响应中分析不同机制。比较了四种闭合模型：不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程、多项式Burnett型替代模型、显式自旋微极性理论以及消除自旋有理核理论。通过多粒子事件驱动模拟完美粗糙球体进行验证。

Result: 在快速自旋区域，保留自旋理论简化为具有有理$k$依赖核的单场模型，其低$k$展开产生$k^4$和$k^6$项。显式自旋理论具有两个极点，消除自旋理论仅保留慢极点。有限多项式截断在定性上失败：严格的$k^4$截断变得过阻尼，匹配的$k^6$截断则出现近临界放大和有限$k$不稳定性。

Conclusion: 横向响应为区分保留旋转微观物理、消除自旋有效动力学和普通多项式高阶梯度闭合提供了实用诊断工具。多粒子模拟显示，固定$k$和多$k$谐波激励能够解析有限的自旋-涡度相位滞后，这强烈支持保留自旋动力学而非瞬时绝热消除，同时更强的驱动多$k$涡度响应拒绝了纯$k^2$闭合。

Abstract: High-curvature observables in incompressible flows, including $k^4$-weighted spectra, can arise from explicit internal rotation, elimination of a fast spin variable, or polynomial higher-gradient closure. Building on a retained-spin micropolar closure derived separately from the Boltzmann--Curtiss equation, we show that these mechanisms are dynamically distinguishable in transverse linear response. In a fast-spin regime the retained-spin theory reduces to a one-field model with a rational $k$-dependent kernel whose low-$k$ expansion generates $k^4$ and $k^6$ terms, while preserving the large-$k$ roll-off of the eliminated degree of freedom. We compare four closures: incompressible Navier--Stokes, a polynomial Burnett-type surrogate, the explicit-spin micropolar theory, and the eliminated-spin rational-kernel theory. The explicit-spin theory has two poles, the eliminated-spin theory retains only the slow pole, and finite polynomial truncations fail qualitatively: a strict $k^4$ truncation becomes over-damped, while a matched $k^6$ truncation develops near-critical amplification and finite-$k$ instability. Many-particle event-driven simulations of perfectly rough spheres show that these observables are measurable and, in targeted campaigns, discriminating at the microscopic level: fixed-$k$ and multi-$k$ harmonic forcing resolve a finite spin-to-vorticity phase lag that strongly favors retained-spin dynamics over instantaneous adiabatic elimination, while the stronger-drive multi-$k$ vorticity response rejects a pure $k^2$ closure and favors the rational eliminated-spin kernel over a polynomial surrogate. Transverse response thus provides a practical diagnostic for separating retained rotational microphysics, eliminated-spin effective dynamics, and ordinary polynomial higher-gradient closures.

</details>

### [87] [Stable Determinant Monte Carlo Simulations at Large Inverse Temperature $β$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00815)
*Thomas Luu,Johann Ostmeyer,Petar Sinilkov,Finn L. Temmen*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 该论文针对低温下行列式量子蒙特卡洛（DQMC）方法中出现的数值不稳定性和精度损失问题，提出了基于多种矩阵分解的解决方案，使模拟温度可扩展至β≳90，同时保持与原始实现相似的数值计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在低温条件下（1/T=β≫1），行列式量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo, DQMC）方法的原始实现面临精度损失和数值不稳定性问题，特别是在计算费米子行列式（fermion determinant）时。这些不稳定性会进一步影响依赖费米矩阵逆或格林函数（Greens function）的观测量计算。对于依赖哈密顿蒙特卡洛（Hamiltonian Monte Carlo, HMC）算法的DQMC方法，积分哈密顿运动方程所需的力项计算也存在类似的精度损失和数值不稳定问题。

Method: 作者通过采用多种矩阵分解（matrix decompositions）选择来解决上述所有数值问题。该方法能够处理费米子行列式计算、格林函数求逆以及HMC算法中的力项计算等关键环节的数值稳定性问题。

Result: 该方法成功将模拟温度扩展至β≳90，这对应于石墨烯结构的室温条件。同时，该实现的数值计算成本与原始实现相似，均为O(N_x^3N_t)，其中N_x和N_t分别表示空间和时间格点数。

Conclusion: 通过采用适当的矩阵分解技术，可以有效解决低温DQMC模拟中的数值不稳定性和精度损失问题，显著扩展了可模拟的温度范围，同时保持了计算效率。

Abstract: At low temperatures $T$ where $1/T=β\gg1$ the naïve implementation of determinant quantum Monte Carlo (DQMC) methods suffers from loss of precision and numerical instabilities when evaluating the fermion determinant.
  This instability propagates into the calculation of observables that rely on the evaluation of the inverse of the fermion matrix, or the Greens function.
  For DQMC methods that rely on the Hamiltonian Monte Carlo (HMC) algorithm, an additional complication comes from evaluating the force terms required for integrating Hamilton's equations of motion, since here loss of precision and numerical instabilities are also prevalent.
  We show how to address all these issues using various choices of matrix decompositions, allowing us to simulate at $β\gtrsim 90$, which corresponds to room temperature for graphene structures.
  Furthermore, our implementation has numerical costs that scale similarly to the naïve implementation, namely as $\mathcal{O}(N_x^3N_t)$, where $N_x$ ($N_t$) is the number of spatial (temporal) sites.

</details>


### [88] [A multiphysics model for triboelectric nanogenerator design with explicit surface roughness representation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01119)
*MD Tanzib Ehsan Sanglap,Jack Perris,Rudra Mukherjee,Charchit Kumar,Lukasz Kaczmarczyk,Chris J. Pearce,Daniel M. Mulvihill,Andrei G. Shvarts*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种多物理场有限元框架，用于预测摩擦纳米发电机（TENGs）的性能。该框架通过耦合机械接触分析与静电模拟，考虑真实表面粗糙度而非理想化统计近似，能够更准确地预测真实接触面积比和电气响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 设计高效的能量收集摩擦纳米发电机需要能够捕捉表面粗糙度、真实接触面积和静电行为之间相互作用的预测模型。现有模型通常使用理想化的统计近似，无法准确反映不同摩擦层材料和粗糙度水平下的复杂相互作用。

Method: 本文提出了一种多物理场有限元框架（multiphysics finite element framework），将机械接触分析与静电模拟相耦合。该方法采用精确的表面粗糙度表征而非理想化统计近似，并通过真实接触面积比对TENG表面电荷密度进行缩放。此外，通过积分时间相关的常微分方程来表征TENG电路。

Result: 与光学干涉显微镜测量相比，该框架比解析模型（analytical models）更准确地预测了真实接触面积比。在开路电压和电容方面，该方法相对于近似解析模型与实验数据的一致性更好。该框架能够评估不同负载条件下的电气响应，并阐明表面粗糙度、机械载荷、接触分离频率和电阻负载的作用。

Conclusion: 该框架为跨介电材料、机械行为和操作条件的性能优化提供了一个稳健、可扩展的工具。该方法易于扩展到其他表面依赖的能量收集设备，为TENG设计提供了更准确的预测能力。

Abstract: The design of triboelectric nanogenerators (TENGs) for efficient energy harvesting requires predictive models that capture the interplay between surface roughness, real contact area, and electrostatic behaviour across diverse tribolayer materials and roughness levels. To address this demand, this paper presents a multiphysics finite element framework that couples mechanical contact analysis with electrostatic simulations, considering exact surface roughness representations rather than idealised statistical approximations. Compared with optical interference microscopy measurements, the framework predicts the real contact area ratio more accurately than analytical models. The proposed approach captures the electrostatic behaviour by scaling the TENG surface charge density with the real contact area ratio between the rough tribolayers, computed for a given mechanical load. This method improves agreement with experiments for open-circuit voltage and capacitance relative to approximate analytical models. To represent the TENG circuit, a time-dependent ordinary differential equation is integrated, enabling evaluation of electrical responses under varying load conditions and elucidating the roles of surface roughness, mechanical load, contact-separation frequency, and resistive load. The framework provides a robust, scalable tool for performance optimisation across dielectric materials, mechanical behaviours, and operating conditions and is readily extendable to other surface-dependent energy-harvesting devices.

### [89] [Directional-dependent Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless transition at EuO/KTaO$_3$(111) interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00608)
*Zongyao Huang,Zhengjie Wang,Xiangyu Hua,Huiyu Wang,Zhaohang Li,Shihao Liu,Zhiwei Wang,Feixiong Quan,Zhen Wang,Jing Tao,James Jun He,Ziji Xiang,Xianhui Chen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统BKT理论认为二维超导态的临界温度由全局超流刚度决定，与电流方向无关。本研究旨在探索在铁磁邻近效应影响下的超导界面中，是否会出现超越传统BKT物理描述的新奇物相。

Method: 通过在(111)取向的KTaO₃与铁磁EuO界面构建二维超导系统，测量不同平面偏置电流方向下的BKT转变温度，并分析转变温度以上超导涨落产生的非互易信号。

Result: BKT转变温度表现出明显的方向依赖性，最高值出现在电流沿[11$\bar{2}$]晶轴方向时，表明晶格三重旋转对称性发生自发破缺。这种方向依赖性在超导涨落的非互易信号中得到一致反映。

Conclusion: 该现象归因于界面相分离机制：具有较高BKT转变温度的相自组织形成沿[11$\bar{2}$]方向伸展的准一维结构。研究结果表明在铁磁邻近效应下的超导界面中，出现了超越传统BKT物理描述的新奇物相。

Abstract: In two dimensions, a phase-coherent superconducting state is established via a Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless (BKT) transition, whose critical temperature $T_{\rm BKT}$ is determined by the global superfluid stiffness in uniform superconducting systems. We report that at the interface between (111)-oriented KTaO$_3$ and ferromagnetic EuO, the two-dimensional superconducting state exhibits a BKT transition relying on the direction of in-plane bias current. The highest $T_{\rm BKT}$ occurs when current is applied along one of the [11$\bar{2}$] axes of KTaO$_3$, underscoring a spontaneous breaking of the threefold lattice rotational symmetry. Such directional dependence of $T_{\rm BKT}$ is consistently reflected in the nonreciprocal signals stemming from superconducting fluctuations above the transition. We attribute this phenomenon to an interfacial phase segregation; the phase with higher $T_{\rm BKT}$ self-organizes into quasi-one-dimensional textures that stretch along one of the [11$\bar{2}$] directions. Our results point toward the emergence of exotic phases of matter beyond the description of conventional BKT physics at a superconducting interface that is subjected to ferromagnetic proximity.

### [90] [Improving YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{7-δ}$ annealing times through a combining-temperatures route](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00762)
*R. F. Luccas,L. Gallo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究系统探究了YBa₂Cu₃O₇-δ（YBCO）在300-800°C温度范围内的恒温氧合过程，发现高温促进快速氧吸收但导致较低饱和水平，而低温虽动力学缓慢但能实现更好的氧合状态。研究提出了一种基于多温度组合的氧合方案，显著缩短了达到特定δ值所需的时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在系统探究YBa₂Cu₃O₇-δ（YBCO）超导材料在不同温度下的氧合过程动力学，以优化其氧合条件并改善最终的超导性能。通过理解温度对氧合动力学和最终氧饱和水平的影响，为工业应用提供直接指导。

Method: 采用热重分析（thermogravimetric analysis）方法，将完全脱氧的YBCO粉末样品暴露于氧饱和气氛中，在300-800°C温度范围内记录其质量随时间的变化。特别对氧饱和附近区域（δ < 0.3）进行了比较分析，并提出了基于多温度组合的氧合方案。

Result: 结果表明氧合动力学和最终氧饱和水平对氧合温度有强烈依赖性：较高温度促进快速氧吸收但导致较低饱和水平（较高最终δ值），而较低温度虽动力学缓慢但能使系统接近更好的氧合条件。提出的双温度氧合方案（先高温后低温）显著缩短了达到特定δ值所需时间：达到δ < 0.1的时间减少约30%，达到δ ≈ 0.12的时间减少约60%。

Conclusion: 研究证实了温度对YBCO氧合过程的显著影响，并成功开发了一种优化的多温度氧合方案。该方案通过结合高温的快速动力学和低温的高饱和优势，显著提高了氧合效率。研究结果对工业应用具有直接价值，因为所用晶粒尺寸与典型超导带材厚度相当。

Abstract: The oxygenation process at constant temperature of YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{7-δ}$ (YBCO) was systematically investigated in the temperature range from 300 $^o$C to 800 $^o$C. With this purpose, fully deoxygenated powder samples was exposed to an oxygen saturated atmosphere, and the evolution of their mass was recorded as a function of time using a thermogravimetric balance. Results reveal a strong dependence of both: the oxygenation kinetics and the final oxygen saturation level, on the temperature used for oxygenation. Moreover, results show that higher oxygen temperatures promote faster oxygen absorption but lead to lower saturation levels (higher final $δ$ values), whereas lower oxygen temperatures result in slower kinetics but enable the system to approach better oxygenation conditions in order to improve the final superconducting properties of the material. In addition to our measurements, a comparative analysis between oxygenation levels at the oxygen temperatures under study was performed in the range around oxygen saturation ($δ$ $<$ 0.3). Consequently, an oxygenation protocol based on a combination of several oxygenation temperatures is proposed. As a first approach, results from a protocol with just two different oxygenation temperatures is compared with results coming from using just one oxygenation temperature. Outstandingly, a protocol with a first oxygenation step at high temperatures and a second one at low temperatures demonstrates to improve oxygenation times in near a 30 \% for reaching $δ$ values below 0.1 and in near a 60 \% for reaching $δ$ values around 0.12. Finally, we trust that our results are of direct application on industry since size of grain used herein are in scales of typical thickness of superconductor tapes.

</details>

Conclusion: 该新型层状钒氧硫族化合物家族在铜酸盐/镍酸盐和铁基高温超导体之间架起了"桥梁"，为扩展具有更高临界温度（T_c）的层状超导体类别提供了新希望和机会，并有助于加深对这些体系中基础机制的理解。

Abstract: Altermagnets (AMs), characterized by zero net magnetization and momentum-dependent spin splitting, are anticipated to hold significant potential for generating multiple exotic and uncommon superconducting states. However, superconductivity has not yet been realized in AMs to date. Our preliminary attempts to explore superconductivity in these materials by applying pressure or chemical doping were unsuccessful. Here we report the discovery of superconductivity at a relatively high transition temperature of ~ 16.3 K in a newly synthesized layered compound, Na$_{2-x}$V$_2$Se$_2$O, a variant of AV$_2$Ch$_2$O. This new family of layered vanadium oxychalcogenides, lacking inversion symmetry, represents an intriguing platform for exploring altermagnetic superconductors, and holds the potential to reveal novel phenomena, such as topological states, van Hove singularities, and finite-momentum superconductivity. Furthermore, this material acts as a "bridge" between the cuprate/nickelate and iron-pnictide high temperature superconductors, providing new hope and opportunity to expand the category of layered superconductors with higher critical temperatures (T$_c$) and enhancing our understanding of the underlying mechanisms in these systems.

### [92] [Detecting pairing symmetry of bilayer nickelates using electronic Raman scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01027)
*Jun Zhan,Matías Bejas,Andreas P. Schnyder,Andrés Greco,Xianxin Wu,Jiangping Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过电子拉曼散射（electronic Raman scattering）分析双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇的超导配对对称性，发现多轨道效应（multiorbital effects）对拉曼谱具有关键影响，拉曼响应可区分不同配对对称性并确定能隙各向异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇中高温超导性的发现引起了广泛关注，但块体和薄膜材料中相互矛盾的实验证据导致其配对对称性（pairing symmetry）在实验和理论研究上仍存在争议。

Method: 研究采用双轨道双层模型（two-orbital bilayer model），通过比较多轨道方法和能带叠加方法获得的拉曼磁化率（Raman susceptibilities），分析不同配对对称性在不同通道中的电子拉曼响应。

Result: 拉曼响应能够区分不同配对对称性，并确定完全能隙和节点超导态的能隙振幅。节点d_{x²-y²}/d_{xy}-波配对表现出明显的低能幂律行为，与完全能隙配对不同；对于s±-波配对，可以确定β口袋上的详细能隙各向异性。

Conclusion: 多轨道效应对拉曼谱的形成具有关键作用，电子拉曼散射可作为确定非常规超导体中超导能隙的强有力且具有对称性分辨能力的探测手段。

Abstract: The recent discovery of high-temperature superconductivity in both bulk and thin-film bilayer nickelates La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ has garnered significant attention. However, the corresponding pairing symmetry remains debated in both experiments and theoretical studies due to conflicting experimental evidence from bulk and thin-film materials. In this work, we examine the electronic Raman response across different channels for various pairing symmetries within a two-orbital bilayer model. By comparing Raman susceptibilities obtained from multiorbital and band-additive approaches, we demonstrate that Raman response can distinguish between different pairing symmetries and identify pocket-dependent gap amplitudes for both fully gapped and nodal superconducting states. Specifically, the nodal $d_{x^2-y^2}/d_{xy}$-wave pairing exhibits robust low-energy power-law behavior, distinct from a fully gapped pairing. Additionally, for the $s_{\pm}$-wave pairing, the detailed gap anisotropy on the $β$ pocket can be determined. Possible experimental implications are also discussed. Our results highlight the crucial role of multiorbital effects in shaping the Raman spectra and establish electronic Raman scattering as a powerful and symmetry-resolved probe for determining the superconducting gap in unconventional superconductors.

### [93] [Uniaxial Compression-Induced Anisotropy and Electronic Dimensionality in the Iron-Based Superconductor FeSe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01062)
*Alexy Bertrand,Masaki Mito,Kazuma Nakamura,Mahmoud Abdel-Hafiez*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过不同压缩模式（面内、面外、静水压）探究了FeSe超导转变温度（Tc）的演化规律。研究发现，Tc在初始阶段随压力增加而上升，但在向列序被抑制后表现出显著的方向依赖性：面外压缩与静水压类似促进超导，而面内压缩则抑制超导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解FeSe超导材料在不同压缩模式（in-plane, out-of-plane, hydrostatic compression）下超导转变温度（Tc）的演化规律，特别是探究向列序（nematic ordering）被抑制后Tc表现出的方向依赖性。

Method: 采用实验方法研究FeSe在面内、面外和静水压压缩下的Tc演化，并结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析电子结构变化。

Result: 在压力达到0.6 GPa前，无论压缩模式如何，Tc均随压力增加而上升，这与向列序被抑制一致。然而，一旦向列性被抑制，Tc表现出显著的方向依赖性：面外压缩与静水压类似导致Tc急剧上升，而面内压缩则抑制超导。计算表明面内压缩使Se pz和Fe dx²-y²杂化带沿Γ-Z方向穿过费米能级，形成额外金属带。

Conclusion: 电子结构的维度性（dimensionality）在决定FeSe在不同压缩模式下Tc响应中起关键作用。面内压缩导致的额外金属带增加了电子结构的三维性，这可能被解释为费米面（Fermi surface）的Lifshitz型转变。

Abstract: The evolution of the superconducting transition temperature ($T_c$) in FeSe was investigated under in-plane, out-of-plane, and hydrostatic compression. For pressures up to 0.6 GPa, $T_c$ increases regardless of the compression mode, consistent with the suppression of nematic ordering. However, once nematicity is suppressed, $T_c$ exhibits a striking directional dependence: out-of-plane compression shows behavior similar to the hydrostatic case, with a sharp increase in $T_c$, whereas in-plane compression suppresses superconductivity. First-principles calculations suggest that in-plane compression shifts a hybridized band of Se $p_z$ and Fe $d_{x^2-y^2}$ character so that it crosses the Fermi level along the $Γ$-Z direction, leading to the emergence of an additional metallic band. This leads to an increased three-dimensionality of the electronic structure and may be interpreted as a possible Lifshitz-type change in the Fermi surface. These results indicate that the dimensionality of the electronic structure plays a key role in determining the $T_c$ response of FeSe under different compression modes.

</details>

### [94] [Exact Solution of Chandrasekhar's H Function For the Isotropic Case](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00068)
*Fikret Anli*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本研究为各向同性散射（isotropic scattering）情况下的Chandrasekhar H函数提供了精确解。该函数在辐射传输理论中具有核心作用，通过推导积分方程的微分形式并求解，获得了H函数的精确表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Chandrasekhar的H函数在辐射传输理论中扮演核心角色，但受非线性积分方程控制。本研究旨在为该函数提供精确解，以改进各向同性散射情况下的理论计算精度。

Method: 采用经典积分技术推导非线性积分方程的微分形式，将原积分方程转化为可解的微分方程。通过求解该微分方程获得H函数的精确表达式。

Result: 成功获得了H函数的精确解，并将数值结果与Chandrasekhar报告的数据进行比较。差异以表格形式呈现，验证了解析解的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究实现了各向同性散射条件下Chandrasekhar H函数的精确求解，为辐射传输理论提供了更准确的计算工具。数值比较证实了该精确解相对于先前结果的改进。

Abstract: This study provides an exact solution to Chandrasekhar's H function for isotropic scattering. The H function, which is governed by a nonlinear integral equation, plays a central role in radiative transfer theory. To facilitate the solution, the differential form of the integral equation is derived using classical integral techniques. The resulting differential equation is then solved to yield an exact expression for the H function. Numerical results obtained from the exact solution are compared with those reported by Chandrasekhar, and the differences are presented in tabular format.
