### [95] [Symmetric Nonlinear Cellular Automata as Algebraic References for Rule~30](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00165)
*E. Chan-López,A. Martín-Ruiz*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究为初等元胞自动机（elementary cellular automata）建立了一个基于空间对称性的比较代数框架，以Rule 22为核心研究对象，并以其为对称参考分析Rule 30的对称破缺效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是建立一个比较代数框架来分析初等元胞自动机，重点关注空间对称性的作用。选择Rule 22作为核心研究对象，因为它在代数正规形式$g(a,b,c)=a\oplus b\oplus c\oplus abc$下，结合了完整的$S_3$对称性和真实的非线性特性，是最简单的此类规则。

Method: 研究方法基于代数框架，以Rule 22为对称参考点。建立了三个闭式结果：支撑集基数的公式、支撑集的两步递归构造方法，以及连续极限下的抛物线反应-扩散方程。然后将Rule 22作为对称参考用于分析Rule 30。

Result: 研究获得了三个闭式结果：支撑集基数公式$|S_m|=2^{\mathrm{popcount}(\lfloor m/2 \rfloor)}\cdot 3^{m\bmod 2}$；支撑集的两步递归构造；以及连续极限下的抛物线反应-扩散方程$\partial_m u=u_{xx}+2u+u^3$。对于Rule 30，对称破缺偏差$\epsilon(m)=|S_m^{(30)}|-|S_m^{(22)}|$经验上符合幂律标度$m^b$（$b\approx 1.11$），量化了将对称三次项$abc$替换为非对称二次项$bc$的累积效应。

Conclusion: 该研究为初等元胞自动机建立了一个基于空间对称性的比较代数框架，以Rule 22为对称参考点。通过分析Rule 30的对称破缺效应，揭示了其中心列表现随机性的机制源于左置换结构和不对称布尔敏感性分布。研究量化了对称性破坏对系统行为的影响。

Abstract: A comparative algebraic framework for elementary cellular automata is developed, centered on the role of spatial symmetry. The primary object of study is Rule~22, the elementary cellular automaton with algebraic normal form $g(a,b,c)=a\oplus b\oplus c\oplus abc$ over $\mathcal{F}_2$, the simplest rule combining full $S_3$ symmetry with genuine nonlinearity. Three closed-form results are established: a formula for the support-set cardinality, $|S_m|=2^{\mathrm{popcount}(\lfloor m/2 \rfloor)}\cdot 3^{m\bmod 2}$; a two-step recursive construction of the support sets; and the continuous limit as a parabolic reaction--diffusion equation, $\partial_m u=u_{xx}+2u+u^3$. Rule~22 is then used as a symmetric reference for Rule~30. The symmetry-breaking deviation $ε(m)=|S_m^{(30)}|-|S_m^{(22)}|$ is empirically consistent with a power-law scaling of the form $m^b$ ($b\approx 1.11$), quantifying the cumulative effect of replacing the symmetric cubic $abc$ with the asymmetric quadratic $bc$. A mechanism for the apparent randomness of Rule~30's center column is identified through the left-permutive structure and asymmetric Boolean sensitivity profile.

</details>


### [96] [Local Rank-One Logarithmic Instability for the Mixed Hessian of the Dispersionless Toda $τ$-Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00240)
*Oleg Alekseev*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了多项式共形映射的色散less Toda τ-函数的混合Hessian矩阵在无标度参数下的行为，证明了在接近简单临界点时存在局部秩一对数不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析色散less Toda τ-函数（dispersionless Toda τ-function）的混合Hessian矩阵在无标度参数（scale-free parameters）下的行为，特别关注在接近临界点时的不稳定性机制。

Method: 方法基于显式的对数核恒等式（logarithmic-kernel identity）导出Hessian矩阵的对称块分解（symmetry-block decomposition），分析输入为逆映射生成函数U(x;ζ)及其主导奇点。研究假设沿横向亚临界路径（transversal subcritical path）接近简单临界点时，U的泰勒分支具有唯一的简单平方根分支点（simple square-root branch points）的s-轨道。

Result: 主要结果证明了局部秩一对数不稳定性（local rank-one logarithmic instability）：在固定加权重整化（weighted renormalization）下，恰好一个变分特征值（variational eigenvalue）对数发散，而所有高阶变分特征值保持有界。减去奇异秩一项后，余项在算子范数下收敛到紧极限（compact limit）。

Conclusion: 结论表明该结果是局部的而非全局的：它分离了导致首次不稳定性的机制，并记录了超越多项式叶（polynomial leaves）扩展的抽象准则。在拉普拉斯增长（Laplacian growth）中，如果临界穿越发生在单叶性（univalence）丧失之前，相同的光谱转变会先于几何崩溃发生。

Abstract: We study the mixed Hessian of the dispersionless Toda $τ$-function for polynomial conformal maps, in scale-free parameters. An explicit logarithmic-kernel identity yields a symmetry-block decomposition of the Hessian, while the analytic input is the inverse-map generating function $U(x;ζ)$ and its first dominant singularities. Along a transversal subcritical path approaching a simple critical point, assume that the Taylor branch of $U$ has a unique dominant $s$-orbit of simple square-root branch points and satisfies a uniform continuation hypothesis. Then, for a fixed weighted renormalization of each symmetry block, we prove a local rank-one logarithmic instability: exactly one variational eigenvalue diverges logarithmically, while all higher variational eigenvalues remain bounded. After subtraction of the singular rank-one term, the remainder converges in operator norm to a compact limit. Along Laplacian growth, if the critical crossing occurs before loss of univalence, the same spectral transition precedes geometric breakdown. The result is local rather than global: it isolates the mechanism responsible for the first instability and records an abstract criterion for extension beyond polynomial leaves.

</details>


### [97] [Localised Davies generators for unbounded operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00306)
*Jeffrey Galkowski,Maciej Zworski*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用时间局域化（localisation in time）的构造方法，将量子吉布斯采样器的构建从有限维希尔伯特空间扩展到包含无界算子（unbounded operators）的类别，特别是伪微分算子（pseudodifferential operators）。

Result: 证明了该构造方法同样适用于无界算子类别，包括用于研究Lindblad演化中经典/量子对应关系（classical/quantum correspondence）的伪微分算子。这表明量子吉布斯采样器可以在更广泛的数学框架下实现。

Conclusion: 时间局域化的构造方法不仅适用于有限维情况，也能成功扩展到无界算子类别，为研究Lindblad演化中的经典/量子对应关系提供了更广泛的数学工具基础。

Abstract: A classical Davies generator provides a Lindbladian for which the Gibbs state is stationary. Its construction involves precise knowledge of the Bohr spectrum or equivalently state evolution for all times. Recently Chen, Kastoryano and Gilyen proposed a construction involving localisation in time and carried out it out in the case of finite dimensional Hilbert spaces. The resulting generators are called quantum Gibbs samplers as the corresponding Lindblad is expected to settle to the Gibbs state. In this note, we show that the construction also works for classes of unbounded operators, including pseudodifferential operators used in the study of classical/quantum correspondence in Lindblad evolution.

### [99] [Spectral sum rules on a $d$--sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00845)
*Paolo Amore*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究推导了在任意密度分布下d维球面上亥姆霍兹方程（Helmholtz equation）特征值逆幂的谱求和规则（spectral sum rules），采用重整化方案（renormalization scheme）处理零模发散，并应用于具体密度函数验证数值方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于推导任意密度分布下d维球面上亥姆霍兹方程特征值的谱求和规则，这些特征值通常无法显式确定，需要发展不依赖特征值显式表达的分析方法。

Method: 采用严格的重整化方案（renormalization scheme）去除零模（zero mode）的发散贡献，从而获得谱求和规则的精确表达式，无需显式确定特征值。应用时采用瑞利-里兹方法（Rayleigh-Ritz method）近似低能谱部分，外尔公式（Weyl's formula）处理高能部分进行数值估计。

Result: 成功推导出d维球面上亥姆霍兹方程特征值逆幂的谱求和规则，并针对d=3,4,5维度和具体密度函数$Σ(Ω) = 1 + κY_{1,\vec{0}}(Ω)$获得了显式求和规则，与数值估计结果进行了比较验证。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了处理任意密度分布下球面亥姆霍兹方程谱求和规则的严格重整化框架，为无法显式确定特征值的系统提供了有效的分析工具，并通过具体应用验证了方法的有效性。

Abstract: We derive spectral sum rules for inverse powers of the eigenvalues of the Helmholtz equation on a $d$-sphere in the presence of an arbitrary density. By adopting a rigorous renormalization scheme, we remove the divergent contributions of the zero mode and obtain exact expressions for the sum rules without requiring an explicit determination of the eigenvalues, which is generally impossible. As an application, we derive explicit sum rules for the density $Σ(Ω) = 1 + κY_{1,\vec{0}}(Ω)$ in $d=3,4,5$ dimensions and compare them with numerical estimates obtained by approximating the low-lying part of the spectrum with the Rayleigh--Ritz method and the high-energy part with Weyl's formula.

Conclusion: 系统表现出晚期线性不稳定性，表明量子反作用驱动的向德西特宇宙时空的转变，当系统参数限制在物理相关区域时，该普适尺度与观测到的宇宙膨胀相符。

Abstract: We establish the linear instability of the semiclassical Einstein-Klein-Gordon system linearised about the Minkowski vacuum spacetime. The proof relies on formulating a forcing problem for both metric and state perturbations within the space of past-compact sections. This geometric framework admits a unique tensor decomposition which, in conjunction with the quantum Møller operator, enables the decoupling of the linearised system into two distinct Cauchy problems. Consequently, the metric perturbations are shown to be governed by a higher-order, nonlocal hyperbolic partial differential equation. By relegating the nonlocal contributions to subleading order, we establish the well-posedness of this forcing problem. Furthermore, we provide a rigorous asymptotic analysis for physically admissible choices of the renormalisation constants. We prove that the system exhibits a late-time linear instability: the metric perturbations grow exponentially, bounded strictly by a universal scale H, thereby indicating a quantum backreaction-driven transition toward a de Sitter cosmological spacetime. Provided the parameters governing the system are restricted to a physically relevant regime, this universal scale is compatible with the measured expansion of our universe.

</details>

### [104] [Propagation-mediated amplification of \{11\={2}0\}-biased inversion domain boundary alignment in polarity-mixed GaN lateral overgrowth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00233)
*Harim Song,Donghoi Kim,Chinkyo Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验和模拟分析，揭示了在混合极性GaN横向外延中，{11¯20}取向的反转畴界（IDB）偏向性如何通过传播过程被放大，而非仅由掩模边界几何决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于解释混合极性GaN横向外延中观察到的反转畴界（inversion domain boundaries, IDBs）取向偏向现象。传统几何闭合模型适用于单一极性情况，但无法完全解释混合极性区域内IDBs的{11¯20}取向偏向性。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）对圆形开口内的混合极性GaN进行平面扫描电镜（plan-view SEM）线迹统计分析；2）采用距离分辨、长度加权的取向分析，在从开口中心定义的同心环形区域中量化取向偏向；3）应用相同的环形分辨统计算子到最小二畴传播模拟中，验证传播介导的各向异性效应。

Result: 实验结果显示：1）IDB取向保持对{11¯20}晶面族的偏向性；2）随着传播距离增加，{11¯20}偏向性被渐进放大，取向分布变窄；3）模拟表明在固定圆形几何下，传播介导的各向异性能够复现观察到的径向放大现象。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，在图案化蓝宝石上的混合极性GaN横向外延中，{11¯20}偏向的IDB排列具有可量化的现象学特征。混合极性区域中IDB取向偏向主要由传播介导的放大机制解释，而非仅由掩模边界几何选择决定。

Abstract: GaN polarity inversion and the associated inversion domain boundaries (IDBs) are frequently observed during lateral overgrowth and are often discussed in terms of the small energetic spread among competing IDB structures predicted by first-principles calculations. In circular mask openings, \(\{11\bar{2}0\}\)-aligned IDBs have previously been explained by geometric closure of a single-polarity hexagonal domain at the circular boundary. Here we examine an experimentally distinct regime in which opposite-polarity domains already coexist within the opening before the later development of long, straight IDB traces. In this mixed-polarity regime, the final trace orientation cannot be attributed solely to the macroscopic circular boundary. Nevertheless, plan-view SEM line-trace statistics show that IDB orientations remain biased toward the \(\{11\bar{2}0\}\) family. To quantify how this bias develops during propagation, we perform distance-resolved, length-weighted orientation analysis in concentric annular regions defined from the opening center. The resulting metrics show that \(\{11\bar{2}0\}\)-biased alignment is progressively amplified with propagation distance, while the orientation distribution becomes narrower, indicating systematic sharpening of the preferred alignment state. We further apply the same ring-resolved statistical operators to minimal two-domain propagation simulations in a circular opening and find that a propagation-mediated anisotropy reproduces the observed radial amplification under fixed circular geometry. Together, these results establish a quantitative phenomenology of \(\{11\bar{2}0\}\)-biased IDB alignment in polarity-mixed GaN lateral overgrowth on patterned sapphire and indicate that, although mask-boundary-imposed selection may describe single-polarity closure cases, the present mixed-polarity regime is better explained by propagation-mediated amplification.

### [105] [Stress Asymmetry in Hard Magnetic Soft Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00238)
*H. Gökçen Güner,Francois Barthelat,John D. Clayton,Carlos Mora-Corral,Noel Walkington,Kaushik Dayal*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文探讨硬磁软材料（hard magnetic soft materials）连续介质磁力学模型中柯西应力（Cauchy stress）的对称性问题，比较了基于参考磁化（referential magnetization）和当前磁化（current magnetization）的两种能量等效公式化方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硬磁软材料（由硬磁颗粒嵌入软聚合物构成）的连续介质磁力学建模中，变形和磁化场是主要运动学变量。近期研究关注柯西应力是否对称的问题，这直接关系到框架不变性和角动量平衡。

Method: 通过分析能量等效的公式化方法，比较基于参考磁化（referential magnetization）描述和基于当前磁化（current magnetization）描述的两种变量变换关系。重点考察这两种公式化方法对柯西应力对称性的影响。

Result: 基于参考磁化的公式化产生对称的柯西应力，而基于当前磁化的公式化通常产生非对称的柯西应力。当内变量（磁化场）处于能量最小化平衡构型时，这两种应力的散度相同，且两者都变为对称。

Conclusion: 两种能量等效的公式化方法在柯西应力对称性上存在差异，但在磁化场达到能量最小化平衡时收敛为相同结果。这澄清了硬磁软材料连续介质模型中应力对称性与变量选择的关系。

Abstract: Hard magnetic soft materials -- soft polymers embedded with hard magnetic particles -- are modeled using continuum magnetomechanical formulations in which the deformation and the magnetization field are the primary kinematic variables. A recent question in such formulations is whether the Cauchy stress is symmetric, which is directly related to frame invariance and angular momentum balance. This note discusses energetically equivalent formulations, related by a change of variables between referential and current descriptions of the magnetization, and shows that they generally yield different Cauchy stresses, including a change in their symmetry. Specifically, the formulation based on a referential magnetization produces a symmetric Cauchy stress, while that based on a current magnetization generally yields an asymmetric Cauchy stress. We highlight that when the internal variable (magnetization field) is at the energy-minimizing equilibrium configuration, the divergences of these stresses are the same, and both stresses are symmetric.

</details>


### [106] [Spatially modulated morphotropic phase boundaries in a compressively strained multiferroic thin film](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00288)
*Ting-Ran Liu,Xiangwei Guo,Sajid Husain,Maya Ramesh,Pushpendra Gupta,Darrell Schlom,Ramamoorthy Ramesh,Yu-Tsun Shao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 在压缩应变铋铁氧体薄膜中观察到两种相界：平坦的形变相界（MPB）和新型锯齿状相界，后者由交替的R'/R'和T'/T'孪晶域组成，其形成源于朗道能与弹性能的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 压缩应变铋铁氧体薄膜中的菱形相（R'）和四方相（T'）单斜相共存表现出优异的压电和磁性性能。先前研究主要关注有序R'/T'孪晶组成的形变相界（MPB），但其自组织结构尚未被充分探索。

Method: 采用基于多模态衍射的电子显微镜观察60 nm厚BiFeO3薄膜，使用横截面多层电子叠层衍射术（multislice electron ptychography）确认原子尺度极化旋转，平面电子背散射衍射（electron backscatter diffraction）揭示晶格向错，并结合相场模拟（phase-field modeling）分析形成机制。

Result: 观察到两种相界：平坦MPB形成延伸>1 mm的线条，每~20 um重复；新型锯齿状相界由交替的R'/R'和T'/T'孪晶域组成。MPB处面外应变变化>15%，锯齿状相界处晶格向错约1.5度，MPB内>2.5度。相场模拟表明锯齿状相界形成源于朗道能（Landau energy）与弹性能的平衡。

Conclusion: 这种有序相界与介观尺度面内应变调制相关，为工程化调控其性能以应用于潜在器件提供了途径。

Abstract: The coexisting rhombohedral-like (R', MA) and tetragonal-like (T', MC) monoclinic phases in compressively strained bismuth ferrite thin films exhibit exceptional piezoelectric and magnetic properties. While previous studies have largely focused on probing the morphotropic phase boundaries (MPBs) comprising ordered R'/T' twins, their self-organizing structures remain not fully explored. Here, we observed two types of interphase boundaries in a 60 nm-thick BiFeO3 film epitaxially grown on a LaAlO3 substrate by employing multi-modal diffraction-based electron microscopy. First, the flat MPBs form lines extending >1 mm, and repeat almost every ~20 um. Additionally, we uncover a new type of phase boundary with zig-zag regions of alternating R'/R' and T'/T' twin domains. Cross-sectional multislice electron ptychography confirms the atomic-scale polarization rotation across the MPB, with out-of-plane strain varying >15%. Plan-view electron backscatter diffraction reveals the lattice disclination of ~1.5-degrees across the zig-zag interphase boundaries, while having >2.5 degrees within the MPB. Phase-field modeling suggests that the formation of zig-zag phase boundaries arises from balancing between Landau and elastic energies. We speculate that such well-ordered interphase boundaries are associated with mesoscale in-plane strain modulations, thus providing a way to engineer and harness their properties for potential device applications.

</details>


### [107] [Metallic d-wave altermagnetism in WFeB: a platform for electrically switchable perpendicular spin-splitter response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00325)
*Eranga H. Gamage,Zhen Zhang,Subhadip Pradhan,Ajay Kumar,David R. Ramgern,V. Ovidiu Garlea,Yaroslav Mudryk,Saeed Kamali,Douglas Warnberg,Kirill D. Belashchenko,Vladimir Antropov,Kirill Kovnir*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文报道了WFeB的合成与磁学表征，将其鉴定为金属性d波交变磁体（d-wave altermagnet），属于更广泛的TiNiSi型家族。研究通过中子衍射、穆斯堡尔谱学和磁测量建立了共线交变磁序，并得到第一性原理计算证实。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索新型交变磁体（altermagnet）材料，特别是TiNiSi型家族中的代表性体系，以理解其独特的磁序和自旋电子学特性。关注点在于发现具有高效自旋电流生成能力的材料平台。

Method: 采用材料合成与磁学表征相结合的方法，包括中子衍射（neutron diffraction）、穆斯堡尔谱学（Mössbauer spectroscopy）和磁测量（magnetometry）。同时进行第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和对称性分析（symmetry analysis）来验证和解释实验结果。

Result: WFeB被确认为共线交变磁体，其电子结构显示约100 meV的非相对论性自旋分裂（nonrelativistic spin splitting）。该材料表现出强自旋分裂输运响应（spin-splitter transport response），表明即使带分裂较小也能实现高效自旋电流生成。对称性分析显示特定薄膜取向允许通过电流诱导的交错力矩（current-induced staggered torques）确定性切换奈尔矢量（Néel vector）。

Conclusion: WFeB及相关TiNiSi型反铁磁体（antiferromagnets）构成了一个由交变磁对称性驱动的电可切换电荷-自旋转换（electrically switchable charge-to-spin conversion）平台。这一发现为自旋电子学应用提供了新的材料基础。

Abstract: We report the synthesis and magnetic characterization of WFeB and identify it as a metallic d-wave altermagnet representative of a broader TiNiSi-type family. Neutron diffraction, Mössbauer spectroscopy, and magnetometry establish a collinear altermagnetic ordering confirmed by first-principles calculations. The electronic structure shows a nonrelativistic spin splitting of approximately 100 meV, but it also supports a strong spin-splitter transport response. This demonstrates that efficient spin-current generation can occur even with such modest band splitting. Symmetry analysis shows that selected film orientations permit deterministic switching of the Néel vector by current-induced staggered torques, enabling electrical control of a perpendicular spin-splitter response. These results establish WFeB and related TiNiSi-type antiferromagnets as a platform for electrically switchable charge-to-spin conversion driven by altermagnetic symmetry.

Method: 提出了一种可调谐的人机协同工作流框架，集成了基于梯度的峰值检测与交互式校正模块。该系统作为基于Web的界面实现，直接处理TEM/EMD文件，应用降噪和界面跟踪算法。

Conclusion: 该架构展示了一种面向自适应、可重用计量工作流的通用方法，将人类洞察力与机器精度相结合，为半导体制造中的可扩展、标准化分析架起桥梁。

Abstract: Scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM) has become a cornerstone instrument for semiconductor materials metrology, enabling nanoscale analysis of complex multilayer structures that define device performance. Developing effective metrology workflows for such systems requires balancing automation with flexibility; rigid pipelines are brittle to sample variability, while purely manual approaches are slow and subjective. Here, we present a tunable human-AI-assisted workflow framework that enables modular and adaptive analysis of STEM images for device characterization. As an illustrative example, we demonstrate a workflow for automated layer thickness and interface roughness quantification in multilayer thin films. The system integrates gradient-based peak detection with interactive correction modules, allowing human input at the design stage while maintaining fully automated execution across samples. Implemented as a web-based interface, it processes TEM/EMD files directly, applies noise reduction and interface tracking algorithms, and outputs statistical roughness and thickness metrics with nanometer precision. This architecture exemplifies a general approach toward adaptive, reusable metrology workflows - bridging human insight and machine precision for scalable, standardized analysis in semiconductor manufacturing. The code is made available at https://github.com/utkarshp1161/thickness-mapping-webapp

### [109] [Comparative study of room temperature and quench condensed bismuth films: morphology and electronic characteristics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00369)
*Yulia Kirina,Prakash Sharma,Wyatt Thomas,Tristan Anderson,Arya G. Pour,Victoria Soghomonian,Jean J. Heremans*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究比较了在296K（室温）和77K（淬火冷凝）两种基底温度下沉积的铋薄膜特性，发现沉积温度显著影响薄膜的结晶性、形貌和电学输运性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在阐明铋薄膜沉积过程中先前未完全理解的过程，特别是通过比较不同基底温度（室温与淬火冷凝）对薄膜性质的影响，以揭示沉积温度对薄膜特性的调控机制。

Method: 研究采用对比实验方法，在296K（室温）和77K（淬火冷凝）两种基底温度下沉积铋薄膜，并在外延（epitaxial）、非晶（amorphous）和范德华（van der Waals）三种基底上进行系统比较。

Result: 实验结果表明，77K沉积的薄膜具有(110)择优取向，而室温沉积的薄膜为(111)取向；淬火冷凝薄膜表面粗糙度较低但晶粒尺寸较小，导致电阻率增加；在非晶和范德华基底上沉积时，降低基底温度会引入更多应变。

Conclusion: 该研究阐明了铋薄膜沉积中温度依赖性的关键机制，揭示了淬火冷凝薄膜具有较低的载流子迁移率和载流子密度，并提出了关于范德华表面生长过程的新问题。

Abstract: A comparison between properties of bismuth thin films deposited at substrate temperatures of 296 K (room temperature) and 77 K (quench condensed) is studied across epitaxial, amorphous, and van der Waals substrates. The experiments demonstrate changes in crystallinity, morphology, and electrical transport arising from the influence of substrate temperature. Moreover, the work highlights changes in grain size, roughness, X-ray diffraction peak intensities, and preferred orientation between the two deposition temperatures. The orientation of the films deposited at 77 K is preferentially (110), compared to (111) for films deposited at room temperature. Films grown at 77 K differ from those deposited at room temperature, exhibiting lower surface roughness but smaller grain size, which leads to increased electrical resistivity in quench condensed films. The decrease of substrate temperature during the deposition appears to induce slightly more strain in depositions on the amorphous and van der Waals substrates than on the epitaxial substrates. Lastly, quench condensed films exhibit lower carrier mobility and lower carrier density compared to room temperature films. This study elucidates previously incompletely understood processes in bismuth deposition and raises new questions regarding growth on van der Waals surfaces.

### [110] [Robust $d$-wave altermagnetism in $\mathrm{RbCr_2Se_2O}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00412)
*San-Dong Guo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究预测RbCr₂Se₂O是一种稳健的d波交变磁体（d-wave altermagnet），其C型和G型反铁磁构型能量差异显著，且可通过面内单轴应变产生净磁矩，为区分G型构型提供了实验策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对KV₂Se₂O、Rb₁₋δV₂Te₂O和Cs₁₋δV₂Te₂O中C型和G型反铁磁构型能量接近导致实验指认不一致的问题，需要寻找具有明确能量差异的体系来研究交变磁性（altermagnetism）。

Method: 通过理论预测方法研究RbCr₂Se₂O的磁构型能量差异，分析其对电子关联强度和范德华相互作用的独立性，并探讨面内单轴应变（in-plane uniaxial strain）对磁性的影响。

Result: 预测RbCr₂Se₂O是稳健的d波交变磁体金属，其C型和G型反铁磁构型能量差异大；施加面内单轴应变可通过直接压磁效应（direct piezomagnetic effect）产生净总磁矩，而G型构型在应变下磁矩保持为零。

Conclusion: RbCr₂Se₂O作为与KV₂Se₂O等结构相似的d波交变磁体，其明确的能量差异和应变响应特性为实验验证提供了便利，且该结论可推广至XCr₂Y₂O（X=K, Rb, Cs; Y=Se, Te）材料家族，扩展了交变磁体家族。

Abstract: The $\mathrm{KV_2Se_2O}$, $\mathrm{Rb_{1-δ}V_2Te_2O}$ and $\mathrm{Cs_{1-δ}V_2Te_2O}$ are experimentally confirmed to adopt either C-type or G-type antiferromagnetic configuration, corresponding to apparent or hidden altermagnetism. However, their nearly degenerate energies lead to inconsistent experimental assignments between the two antiferromagnetic configurations. Here, we predict that the experimentally synthesized $\mathrm{RbCr_2Se_2O}$ is a robust $d$-wave altermagnetic metal, since the energy difference between C-type and G-type configurations is large, which is independent of electron correlation strength and van der Waals interaction. Upon applying in-plane uniaxial strain, $\mathrm{RbCr_2Se_2O}$ can generate a net total magnetic moment via a direct piezomagnetic effect, which is distinct from semiconductor that typically requires carrier doping in addition to strain. This provides an experimental strategy for distinguishing the G-type antiferromagnetic configuration, in which the total magnetic moment remains zero under uniaxial strain. Our work presents an isostructural $d$-wave altermagnetic $\mathrm{RbCr_2Se_2O}$ analogous to $\mathrm{KV_2Se_2O}$, $\mathrm{Rb_{1-δ}V_2Te_2O}$ and $\mathrm{Cs_{1-δ}V_2Te_2O}$, which can facilitate further experimental verification. Furthermore, these results are universal across materials of this family $\mathrm{XCr_2Y_2O}$ (X=K, Rb, Cs; Y=Se, Te), thus expanding the family of altermagnets.

</details>


### [111] [Bipolar plates for the next generation of proton exchange membrane fuel cells (PEMFCs): A review of the latest processing methods for unconventional flow channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00461)
*Zahra Kazemi,Kamran Behdinan*

Result: 研究发现增材制造（additive manufacturing）等先进制造方法能够以有竞争力的成本生产复杂双极板几何形状，为先进PEMFC系统提供了可行的制造途径。

Abstract: The rapid, unsustainable depletion of finite fossil fuel resources and their environmental consequences demand the deployment of affordable clean and sustainable energy solutions. Polymer electrolyte membrane fuel cell (PEMFC) technology is an important pathway in decarbonization of modern energy systems, especially when fueled by high-purity green hydrogen. In PEMFCs, bipolar plates largely determine cell efficiency, longevity, and affordability, which in turn depends on both material selection and design of the embedded flow channels. Conventional manufacturing processes have long been used to fabricate standard bipolar plate designs; however, they are incompatible with unconventional, intricate geometries due to their insufficient resolution and precision in fabrication of fine features, and reliance on multi-step post-processing modifications that limit their design adaptability. This lack of design flexibility impedes the translation of innovative laboratory-scale concepts to industrial-scale production and their practical adoption. In recent years, a growing body of research publications and patent disclosures has reported advanced manufacturing methods, such as additive manufacturing, capable of producing intricate bipolar plate geometries at competitive costs. However, a discussion of these manufacturing approaches, along with an assessment of their scalability and industrial readiness, remains absent in the literature. This study aims to fill this gap. It outlines recent progress and proposes future research directions toward affordable and efficient bipolar plate solutions for advanced PEMFC systems.

Abstract: Radio-frequency excitation directly reshapes the mesoscale charge-density-wave landscape in quasi-two-dimensional 1T-TaS2 thin films. Under combined RF and DC bias, the hysteretic current-voltage characteristics associated with the nearly commensurate-incommensurate transition are strongly altered, displaying RF-driven collapse, branching, and multiple step-like features that depend on frequency and drive amplitude. In-situ Raman measurements show enhanced intensity and linewidth narrowing of low-frequency CDW phonon modes, consistent with reduced dephasing and increased coherence of the periodic lattice distortion under RF drive. This behavior is captured by combining an overdamped time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau description of the commensurate CDW with a morphology-informed percolative resistor-capacitor transport model. The simulations indicate that oscillatory driving anneals frustrated domain configurations, reduces domain-wall density, and reorganizes the discommensuration network, while the transport model reproduces the resulting hysteresis, avalanche-like pathways, and RF-induced conductance steps. RF driving therefore provides an effective route for controlling collective electron-phonon order and accessing metastable transport states in 1T-TaS2, with implications for reconfigurable RF electronics, memory, and unconventional computing based on correlated materials.

Abstract: Topological semimetals have emerged as an important class of quantum materials with novel electronic responses and unconventional transport phenomena. Among them, nodal-line semimetals are distinguished by band crossings that extend along one-dimensional lines in momentum space rather than occurring at discrete points, forming closed loops, chains, or extended lines. The stability of these nodal structures is governed by crystalline symmetries such as mirror, spin-rotation, and nonsymmorphic operations, which give rise to characteristic topological invariants and surface states, including drumhead-like bands. In this review, we present a comprehensive overview of the theoretical framework and experimental realization of nodal-line semimetals, with particular emphasis on symmetry protection and the consequences of symmetry breaking. Special attention is given to insights obtained from angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy and related probes. Abstract: Altermagnetism, the third class of collinear magnetic order, uniquely combines a zero net magnetization with spin polarized bands in reciprocal space, opening new avenues for two dimensional valleytronics and spintronics. Here, using first principles calculations, we predict that the Janus monolayer Cr2SSe, which possesses intrinsic inversion symmetry breaking, hosts a strain tunable multipiezo effect and exhibits distinctive valleytronic properties. The system displays pronounced spin splitting and band inversion at the X and Y high symmetry points in the Brillouin zone, giving rise to robust spin-valley locking. The degeneracy of these valleys is protected by diagonal mirror symmetry. Application of uniaxial strain breaks this symmetry, concurrently inducing piezovalley, piezoelectric, and piezomagnetic responses, a manifestation of the multipiezo effect. Critically, strain applied along orthogonal crystallographic directions yields opposite valley polarization, while under small compressive strain, we achieve selective reversal of valley polarization, enabling independent control of valence and conduction band valleys and promoting a single-spin-channel anomalous valley Hall effect. This structure appears as a result of spontaneous reconstruction of the wurtzite structure and differs from it by the stacking order of the bulk and near-surface Zn atomic layers. The phonon spectrum, electronic structure, and band gap of the obtained nanoplatelets are calculated. The phonon spectra of the nanoplatelets are in complete agreement with the spectra observed in experiment and differ strongly from the vibrational spectra of ZnSe nanoclusters. ### [119] [Microscopic Theory of Superionic Phase Transitions: Nonadiabatic Dynamics and Many-Body Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00665)

Method: 在回顾传统近似方法后，构建了一个适用于正常离子导体和超离子导体的通用晶格模型。通过自洽平均场方案结合非绝热协同跳跃机制（nonadiabatic concerted-hopping mechanism）和多体库仑相互作用（many-body Coulomb interaction）。

Result: 识别出非绝热协同跳跃机制和多体库仑相互作用分别是I型和II型超离子相变的基本驱动力。该模型直接复现了关键实验观测结果，并在统一框架内对两种相变类型进行了全面比较。

Conclusion: 该工作为超离子相变提供了微观洞察，并为先进固态离子导体的设计和优化提供了指导。

Abstract: Superionic phase transitions have attracted extensive interest for decades due to their promising applications and rich underlying physics. In particular, complicated many-body effects and nonadiabatic dynamics are believed to play essential roles, limiting the explanatory power of phenomenological approaches and obscuring the microscopic mechanisms at play. In this work, we develop a unified theoretical framework for describing solid-state ionic conduction. After reviewing the conventional approximations, we construct a general lattice model that applies to both normal ionic and superionic conductors. By incorporating the nonadiabatic concerted-hopping mechanism and the many-body Coulomb interaction within a self-consistent mean-field scheme, we identify these two effects as the fundamental driving forces behind type-I and type-II superionic phase transitions, respectively. Our model directly reproduces key experimental observations. Within this unified framework, we further provide a comprehensive comparison between the two types of transitions. Overall, our work offers microscopic insight into superionic phase transitions and provides guidance for the design and optimization of advanced solid-state ionic conductors.

</details>


### [120] [A comparison of the spin-phonon behaviour of Fe$_2$P-based magnetocaloric materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00695)
*Mikael S. Andersson,Simon R. Larsen,Erna K. Delczeg-Czirjak,Antonio Corona,Jacques Ollivier,Wiebke Lohstroh,Helen Y. Playford,Cheng Li,Pascale P. Deen,Johan Cedervall*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过磁测量、中子散射和理论建模分析Fe₂P和FeMnP₀.₅₅Si₀.₄₅的铁磁转变机制，揭示了Fe₃g位点在磁转变中的主导作用，以及两种化合物中存在的两种不同长度尺度磁过程，阐明了磁热效应的微观起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁制冷（magnetic refrigeration）技术可显著降低冷却设备的能耗，但需使用丰富材料以确保可持续性。Fe₂P基材料在磁热器件中展现出巨大潜力，因此需要深入理解其铁磁转变机制。

Method: 采用磁测量（magnetometry）、中子散射（neutron scattering）和第一性原理计算（first principles calculations）相结合的方法，对Fe₂P和FeMnP₀.₅₅Si₀.₄₅进行系统研究。

Result: Fe₂P的衍射分析表明Fe₃g位点驱动磁转变，而Fe₃f位点在磁转变温度无磁性贡献。FeMnP₀.₅₅Si₀.₄₅的磁转变更为渐进，顺磁和铁磁相在转变温度附近共存。两种化合物在S(Q,ω)谱中均显示两种不同长度尺度区域，可用不同自旋态（S）建模。

Conclusion: FeMn(P,Si)基化合物中存在双组分系统驱动磁转变，进而产生磁热效应（magnetocaloric effect）。低Q值准弹性中子散射显示两种化合物具有相似的磁过程，且磁各向异性在磁态形成中不起主要作用。

Abstract: Magnetic refrigeration can provide an environmentally friendly technology to reduce significantly the energy consumption of cooling devices. To retain the sustainability of the device, all parts must be made from abundant materials, excluding e.g. rare earth elements. As such, materials based on Fe$_2$P have shown great potential for magnetocaloric devices. In this study, Fe$_2$P and FeMnP$_{0.55}$Si$_{0.45}$, have been studied using magnetometry, neutron scattering and theoretical modelling with the aim to understand the ferromagnetic transition, related to the magnetocaloric effect. Analysis of the diffraction data of Fe$_2$P showed that it is the Fe$_{3g}$-site that drives the magnetic transition as the Fe$_{3f}$ does not have any magnetic contribution at the magnetic transition temperature. For FeMnP$_{0.55}$Si$_{0.45}$, the magnetic transition is more gradual, on both sites, with coexistence of the para- and ferromagnetic phases close to the magnetic transition. The temperature dependent magnetic structure behaviour are well in agreement with our first principles calculations.
  Both Fe$_2$P and FeMnP$_{0.55}$Si$_{0.45}$ showed two distinct regions, at different length scales, in their S(\textbf{Q},$ω$) spectra. The two length scales can be modelled using a different set of magnetic spin states (S), using S$\rm _{Fe}$~=~2 and S$\rm _{Mn}$~=~2.5, consistent with the ground state of the magnetic atoms. QENS at low Q (Q~\textless{}~0.5~Å) shows similar magnetic processes in both compounds with uncorrelated magnetism below the magnetic transition temperature. The uncorrelated state highlights that the magnetic anisotropy does not play a major role in the formation of the magnetic state. Furthermore, this emphasises the existence of a two part system in FeMn(P,Si)-based compounds, that drives the magnetic transition and in turn the magnetocaloric effect.

</details>


### [121] [First principles study of thermoelectric properties of $\text{Nb}_2\text{Co}_2\text{InSb}$ and $\text{Nb}_2\text{Co}_2\text{GaSb}$ double half-Heuslers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00775)
*Rajeev Ranjan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究探索了两种双半赫斯勒（double half-Heusler）化合物Nb₂Co₂InSb和Nb₂Co₂GaSb的热电性能，发现通过引入质量无序（mass disorder）可显著降低晶格热导率（lattice thermal conductivity），相比母体NbCoSn系统有显著改善。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 价电子数（valence electron count, VEC）为18的半赫斯勒（half-Heusler, hH）合金因高塞贝克系数（Seebeck coefficient）和机械稳定性而具有高温热电应用潜力，但其较高的晶格热导率（lattice thermal conductivity, kL）限制了热电性能。以NbCoSn为例，尽管具有2.1 mW/mK²的较高功率因子（power factor），但其晶格热导率高达13.25-18 W/mK，导致热电优值（figure of merit, zT）仅约0.05。

Method: 研究探索了NbCoSn在Sn位点取代衍生的Nb₂Co₂InSb和Nb₂Co₂GaSb两种化合物。同时考虑了有序结构和特殊准随机结构（Special Quasirandom Structures, SQSs）以理解构型无序（configurational disorder）的作用。采用德拜-卡拉韦模型（Debye-Callaway model）评估晶格热导率。

Result: 能量分析表明，对于Nb₂Co₂InSb，有序相最稳定；而对于Nb₂Co₂GaSb，SQS相在能量上更有利。室温下晶格热导率评估值为：Nb₂Co₂InSb为5.5-6.9 W/mK，Nb₂Co₂GaSb为4.7-5.8 W/mK，均显著低于母体NbCoSn系统（13.25-18 W/mK）。

Conclusion: 质量无序（mass disorder）能有效降低晶格热导率，Nb₂Co₂InSb和Nb₂Co₂GaSb这两种双半赫斯勒（double half-Heusler）化合物是改善热电性能的有前景候选材料。

Abstract: Valence electron count (VEC) 18 half-Heusler (hH) alloys are considered promising for high-temperature thermoelectric applications due to their high Seebeck coefficient, mechanical stability, and robustness. However, their relatively large lattice thermal conductivity ($k_{L}$) significantly limits their thermoelectric performance. Introducing mass disorder at lattice sites is an effective approach to suppress $k_{L}$ through enhanced phonon scattering. For instance, NbCoSn exhibits a low figure of merit ($zT \sim 0.05$) despite having a reasonably high power factor of 2.1~$\text{mW}/\text{mK}^{2}$ at room temperature, mainly due to its large lattice thermal conductivity, reported to be 13.25~$\text{W}/\text{mK}$ experimentally and 18~$\text{W}/\text{mK}$ theoretically.
  In this work, we explore the thermoelectric properties of $\text{Nb}_2\text{Co}_2\text{InSb}$ and $\text{Nb}_2\text{Co}_2\text{GaSb}$, which can be regarded as derivatives of NbCoSn with substitution at the Sn site. Both ordered and Special Quasirandom Structures (SQSs) are considered to understand the role of configurational disorder. Energetic analysis indicates that the ordered phase is most stable for $\text{Nb}_2\text{Co}_2\text{InSb}$, whereas the SQS phase is energetically favored for $\text{Nb}_2\text{Co}_2\text{GaSb}$. The lattice thermal conductivity is evaluated using the Debye-Callaway model, yielding values in the range of 5.5-6.9~$\text{W}/\text{mK}$ for $\text{Nb}_2\text{Co}_2\text{InSb}$ and 4.7-5.8~$\text{W}/\text{mK}$ for $\text{Nb}_2\text{Co}_2\text{GaSb}$ at room temperature. These values are significantly lower than those of the parent NbCoSn system, highlighting the effectiveness of mass disorder in reducing thermal conductivity. The results suggest that these double half-Heusler compounds are promising candidates for improved thermoelectric performance.

</details>


### [122] [Laser-generated CuPdAgPtAu High-Entropy Alloy Nanoparticles -- Thermal Segregation Threshold and Elemental Segregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00793)
*Felix Pohl,Robert Stuckert,Florent Calvo,Oleg Prymak,Christoph Rehbock,Ulrich Schürmann,Stephan Barcikowski,Lorenz Kienle*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过液相激光烧蚀（laser ablation in liquid）合成的高熵合金（high-entropy alloy, HEA）纳米颗粒在催化领域具有应用前景。研究发现，快速淬火过程抑制了热力学驱动的相分离，形成了亚稳态固溶体；后续加热可诱导相分离，揭示了动力学控制对合金结构稳定性的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高熵合金纳米颗粒因其在化学复杂性下仍能形成简单固溶体而在催化领域具有潜力。本研究旨在探究通过液相激光烧蚀合成的贵金属高熵合金纳米颗粒（CuPdAgPtAu）的结构、成分和热稳定性，以理解其相形成机制。

Method: 采用液相激光烧蚀技术从等摩尔及富铜或富银块体靶材制备贵金属高熵合金纳米颗粒。使用先进的电子显微镜、X射线衍射（XRD）和原子模拟进行结构和成分分析，并进行了热稳定性研究。

Result: 等摩尔靶材和纳米颗粒均呈现单一的面心立方（fcc）相。富铜或富银靶材显示相分离为两个fcc相，但在合成的纳米颗粒中未观察到相分离。模拟预测了由于表面能差异导致的银表面富集和铂核富集，但实验上单个纳米颗粒保持成分均匀。加热后诱导了铜-银相分离，形成与块体靶材相似的第二fcc相。

Conclusion: 激光烧蚀过程中的快速淬火抑制了热力学驱动的相分离，在动力学控制下稳定了亚稳态固溶体。后续缓慢加热克服了动力学势垒，使平衡相在更高温度下形成。这些纳米颗粒的热稳定性及其可调成分（包括超出平衡极限的铜富集）使其在高温催化应用中具有前景，同时减少了贵金属使用量。

Abstract: High-entropy alloy nanoparticles synthesized via laser ablation in liquid are promising for catalysis due to their ability to form simple solid solutions despite chemical complexity. In this study, noble metal HEA NPs (CuPdAgPtAu) are produced from equimolar and Cu- or Ag-enriched bulk targets. Advanced electron microscopy, XRD, and atomistic simulations are used for structural and compositional analysis. Equimolar targets and NPs exhibit a single fcc phase. In contrast, Cu- or Ag-enriched targets show phase segregation into two fcc phases, which is not observed in the synthesized NPs. Simulations predict segregation tendencies, including Ag surface enrichment and Pt core enrichment due to surface energy differences. However, experimentally, individual NPs remain compositionally homogeneous. Thermal stability studies reveal that phase segregation can be induced post-synthesis. Upon heating, Cu-Ag segregation occurs, forming a second fcc phase similar to bulk targets. These findings demonstrate that rapid quenching during laser ablation suppresses thermodynamically driven segregation and stabilizes metastable solid solutions under kinetic control. Subsequent slow heating overcomes kinetic barriers, enabling equilibrium phase formation at higher temperatures. The thermal stability of these NPs and their tunable composition, including Cu enrichment beyond equilibrium limits, make them promising for high-temperature catalytic applications while reducing noble metal usage.

### [123] [Cryogenic stabilization of molecular hydrogen in dense cubic ice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00907)
*Tomasz Poręba,Leon Andriambariarijaona,Richard Gaal,Kazuki Komatsu,Gaston Garbarino,Thomas Hansen,Stanislav Savvin,Livia E. Bove*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 研究发现立方冰（cubic ice）作为致密分子固体，能够在近环境压力下稳定储存分子氢（molecular hydrogen），其储氢性能与金属间隙储氢相当，为氢储存材料提供了新思路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢能（hydrogen energy）作为未来低碳能源技术的关键，面临缺乏安全、高效、可逆固态储存材料的挑战。尽管多孔框架和金属氢化物已被广泛研究，但致密分子固体在近环境压力下稳定氢的能力尚不清楚。

Method: 通过从高压氢水合物前驱体（high-pressure hydrogen hydrate precursor）进行受控减压，使完全结晶的立方冰（cubic ice）保留分子氢作为间隙客体（interstitial guest）。使用同步辐射X射线衍射（synchrotron X-ray diffraction）、中子衍射（neutron diffraction）和拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）进行表征。

Result: 氢可在冰结构中保留至约130K，产生可重现的晶格膨胀和明显的光谱特征。立方冰可在0.18GPa和130K下部分重新填充氢，完全氢填充的立方结构可在相同压力下保持至90K。保留的氢含量达到母体水合物组成的百分之几，其重量和体积储存密度与金属间隙储氢相当。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了致密氢键晶体结构（dense hydrogen-bonded crystal structure）在无永久孔隙或化学键合条件下容纳分子氢的意外能力，确立了立方冰作为氢-晶格相互作用的最小模型。这些发现将致密氢键固体确定为氢储存物理学中未探索的材料类别，对能源材料、行星和天体物理冰环境具有广泛意义。

Abstract: Hydrogen is widely regarded as a cornerstone of future low-carbon energy technologies, yet the lack of safe, efficient, and reversible solid-state storage materials remains a major barrier to its large-scale deployment. Although porous frameworks and metal hydrides have been extensively explored, far less is known about the ability of dense molecular solids to stabilize hydrogen at near-ambient pressure. Here we show that fully crystalline cubic ice, despite its non-porous nature, can retain molecular hydrogen as an interstitial guest following controlled decompression from a high-pressure hydrogen hydrate precursor. Using synchrotron X-ray diffraction, neutron diffraction, and Raman spectroscopy, we demonstrate that hydrogen is retained within the ice structure up to about 130 K, producing reproducible lattice expansion and distinct spectroscopic signatures. We further show that pure cubic ice can be partially refilled with hydrogen at 0.18 GPa and 130 K, while fully hydrogen-filled cubic structure can be preserved at the same pressure up to 90 K. The retained hydrogen content reaches several percent of the parent hydrate composition, corresponding to gravimetric and volumetric storage densities comparable to those of interstitial hydrogen in metals. These results reveal an unexpected ability of a dense hydrogen-bonded crystal structure to host molecular hydrogen without permanent porosity or chemical bonding, establishing cubic ice as a minimal model for hydrogen-lattice interactions. More broadly, our findings identify dense hydrogen-bonded solids as an unexplored class of materials for hydrogen storage physics, with implications extending from energy materials to planetary and astrophysical ice environments.

</details>

Method: 研究比较了不同微调策略对谐波声子带结构（harmonic phonon band structures）、热性质和沿虚声子模式的势能面的预测影响。引入了Equitrain微调框架，该框架基于LoRA（Low-Rank Adaptation）实现适配，使用最少仅10个额外训练结构即可获得显著改进。

Conclusion: 微调策略对机器学习原子间势能的声子相关性质预测具有重要影响，基于LoRA的Equitrain框架在保持计算效率的同时显著提升了预测准确性，为材料模拟提供了有效的优化方案。

Abstract: Machine-learning interatomic potentials are widely used as computationally efficient surrogates for density functional theory in atomistic simulations, enabling large-scale, long-time modeling of materials systems. We investigate how different fine-tuning strategies influence the prediction of harmonic phonon band structures, thermal properties, and the potential energy surface along imaginary phonon modes. We achieve substantial accuracy improvements with minimal additional data, with as few as 10 additional training structures already yielding significant gains. In addition to existing approaches, we introduce Equitrain, a finetuning framework that implements LoRA-based adaptation. Across 53 materials systems, we show that fine-tuned models consistently outperform both the underlying pretrained model and models trained from scratch. Equitrain achieves the best overall performance, and our results demonstrate that fine-tuning enables accurate phonon predictions.

### [126] [Number Theory in Quantum Physics: Minicharged Particles and the Prouhet-Tarry-Escott Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12320)
*Junseok Lee,Fuminobu Takahashi,Yu-Dai Tsai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了量子规范理论中反常消除条件与数论中三次Prouhet-Tarry-Escott问题的等价性，指出隐藏扇区至少需要四个迷你荷粒子，且质量谱通常呈现近简并双重态结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子规范理论中反常消除对允许的手征荷模式有严格限制。论文旨在研究现象学驱动的轻迷你荷粒子框架中，反常消除条件与数论问题的对应关系。

Method: 通过建立现象学驱动的轻迷你荷粒子框架，证明反常消除条件等价于数论中的三次Prouhet-Tarry-Escott问题。基于最小理想解构造分析隐藏扇区结构。

Result: 反常消除条件等价于三次Prouhet-Tarry-Escott问题，这意味着隐藏扇区必须包含至少四个迷你荷粒子状态。基于最小理想解的构造中，质量谱通常呈现近简并双重态结构。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了量子一致性与数论之间的意外联系，对模型构建和未来实验搜索具有直接意义：发现一个迷你荷粒子将指向具有相同迷你荷和相近质量的伙伴态。

Abstract: In quantum gauge theories, anomaly cancellation severely restricts the allowed patterns of chiral charges. Here we show that, in a phenomenologically motivated framework for light minicharged particles, the anomaly cancellation conditions are equivalent to the degree $k=3$ Prouhet-Tarry-Escott problem in number theory. This correspondence immediately implies that the hidden sector must contain at least four minicharged states. For constructions based on minimal ideal solutions, the mass spectrum generically exhibits a near-degenerate doublet structure, so that the discovery of one minicharged particle would point to a partner state with the same minicharge and a nearby mass. Our results uncover an unexpected link between quantum consistency and number theory, with direct implications for model building and future searches.

### [127] [Improving parton shower predictions via precision moments of energy flow polynomials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00084)
*Benoît Assi,Kyle Lee,Jesse Thaler*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究使用最大熵重加权（maximum-entropy reweighting）方法，基于更高精度的理论约束来改进部分子簇射（parton-shower）事件样本。该方法生成严格正的事件权重，在保持事件级排他性的同时提升预测精度，并证明即使部分子簇射先验被故意降级，少量精确计算仍能恢复物理行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索如何利用最大熵重加权方法，基于更高精度的理论约束来改进部分子簇射事件样本。该方法旨在生成严格正的事件权重，在保持完整事件级排他性（event-level exclusivity）的同时提升预测精度，使任何可观测量都能在重加权样本上计算而无需重新分箱或再生。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）使用最大熵重加权方法生成严格正的事件权重；2）采用能量流多项式（energy flow polynomials, EFPs）作为系统基组来组织红外和共线安全约束；3）在$e^+e^-\!\to$强子过程中进行概念验证研究，即使故意移除QCD分裂函数的非奇异部分来降级部分子簇射先验；4）研究信息从受约束可观测量到未受约束观测量的传递。

Result: 研究发现：1）即使部分子簇射先验被故意降级，少量精确计算仍能恢复期望的物理行为；2）观察到快速信息饱和现象，紧凑的EFP矩约束集能在可观测量空间实现广泛改进，包括从未用于训练的标准半球可观测量；3）基于共线幂次计数（collinear power counting）的物理动机基组简化与完整基组性能相当；4）结合多项式和对数项的混合矩优于纯替代方案。

Conclusion: 结论表明，最大熵重加权方法为改进部分子簇射事件生成器提供了系统化途径，其中最高精度的理论约束可以转化为具有实验相关性的完整相空间预测。该方法展示了理论原理如何帮助确定使用哪些约束以及哪些先验能实现高效重加权。

Abstract: In this paper, we study various conceptual and practical aspects of using maximum-entropy reweighting to upgrade parton-shower event samples based on higher-accuracy theoretical constraints. Our approach produces strictly positive per-event weights that improve parton-shower predictions while preserving full event-level exclusivity, allowing any observable to be computed on the reweighted sample without rebinning or regeneration. On the conceptual side, we explain how theoretical principles can help determine which constraints to use and which kinds of priors lead to efficient reweighting. On the practical side, we perform a proof-of-concept study with hemisphere observables in $e^+e^-\!\to$ hadrons, and show that even when the parton-shower prior is purposefully degraded by removing the non-singular parts of the QCD splitting functions, a small set of precision calculations can nevertheless restore the desired physical behavior. We use energy flow polynomials (EFPs) as a systematic basis to organize infrared- and collinear-safe constraints, and study how information transfers from constrained observables to unconstrained ones. We find rapid information saturation, where constraints from a compact set of EFP moments achieve broad improvements across observable space, including for standard hemisphere observables never used in training. Physics-motivated basis reductions guided by collinear power counting achieve comparable performance to complete bases, and mixed moments combining polynomial and logarithmic terms outperform pure alternatives. These results suggest a systematic approach to improving parton-shower event generators, where theoretical constraints of highest accuracy can be translated into full phase-space predictions of experimental relevance.

</details>

*Ajjath A H,Ekta Chaubey,Hua-Sheng Shao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光-光散射是量子电动力学（QED）的最早预测之一，随着LHC的实验观测和未来自由电子激光设施测量前景的出现，对该过程的兴趣重新燃起。

Method: 通过结合高能和低能渐近展开（asymptotic expansions）改进全费米子质量依赖的两圈QCD和QED螺旋度振幅（helicity amplitudes），并在阈值区域（threshold region）执行库仑重求和（Coulomb resummation）。

Result: 为标准模型中的光-光散射截面提供了最先进的理论预测，并开发了新的蒙特卡洛模拟事件生成器LbLatNLO。

Conclusion: 该研究显著提升了光-光散射过程的理论预测精度，为未来实验测量提供了更可靠的理论工具和模拟框架。

Abstract: Light-by-light (LbL) scattering is one of the earliest predictions of quantum electrodynamics (QED). Interest in this process has been renewed following its experimental observation at the LHC and the prospects of future measurements at free-electron laser facilities. In this paper, we refine theoretical predictions for LbL scattering by improving the full fermion-mass-dependent two-loop QCD and QED helicity amplitudes using high- and low-energy asymptotic expansions, and by performing Coulomb resummation in the threshold region. Due to this structure, the neutrinophilic charged Higgs bosons, once created, decay dominantly into heavy neutral leptons (HNLs) and charged leptons. This is a new mechanism to produce a gauge singlet HNL without suppressed cross sections. In the standard seesaw, one HNL can be long-lived, when the lightest neutrino is sufficiently light. We investigate displaced vertex signatures of the long-lived HNLs produced from the decays of the charged Higgs pair at the high luminosity LHC. Method: 采用群论框架，通过直接构造（direct construction）和卡西米尔算符分析（Casimir operator analysis）两种独立方法，显式构建了正定性锥（positivity cone）的极值射线（extremal rays）。该方法解决了宇称破坏算符（parity-violating operators）和连续参数简并（continuous parameter degeneracies）等复杂性。

Abstract: Electroweak boson scattering at the LHC provides a crucial avenue for probing physics beyond the Standard Model, particularly regarding deviations in quartic gauge couplings. Moving beyond previous studies limited to transverse vector bosons, our analysis incorporates all electroweak boson modes, explicitly constructing the extremal rays (ERs) of the positivity cone through a group theoretic framework. We utilize two independent methods--direct construction and Casimir operator analysis--to determine these rays, addressing complexities such as parity-violating operators and continuous parameter degeneracies. Our results indicate that the positivity bounds impose severe constraints, restricting the physically viable parameter space to approximately $0.0313\%$ of the naive total space. Furthermore, we derive linear analytical bounds for various operator combinations and provide an easy-to-use Python package, {\tt SMEFTaQGC}, which implements algorithms to numerically verify positivity and compute the optimized positivity bounds for general aQGC configurations.

### [134] [Mass Hierarchies Without Mixing: Abelian Froggatt-Nielsen Models with Uncharged Left-Handed Doublets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01055)
*Navid Ardakanian*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明在左手场不带电荷的阿贝尔（abelian）离散弗罗加特-尼尔森（Froggatt-Nielsen）模型中，无论群阶、电荷分配或马约拉纳（Majorana）质量结构如何，PMNS和CKM矩阵均服从哈尔随机（Haar-random）分布，导致混合角预测与实验观测严重不符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究阿贝尔离散味对称性（abelian discrete flavor symmetry）模型在解释中微子和夸克混合模式方面的局限性，特别是当左手场不带电荷时，这些模型是否能产生与实验一致的混合角。

Method: 通过数学证明和蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）扫描相结合的方法：首先理论证明所有左手场不带电荷的阿贝尔离散弗罗加特-尼尔森模型均产生哈尔随机混合矩阵；然后对ℤ₃到ℤ₇群进行系统扫描，每个群测试12种电荷分配，各生成10⁵个蒙特卡洛样本进行数值验证。

Result: 数值结果显示：ℤ₃模型特有的跷跷板（seesaw）过度抑制机制导致Δm²₂₁/Δm²₃₁降至~10⁻¹¹的质量谱问题仅存在于ℤ₃，N≥4时可避免；但混合角问题是普遍且不可约的，所有阿贝尔模型的PMNS角统计上均与哈尔随机酉矩阵一致，中值sin²θ₁₂≈sin²θ₂₃≈0.50，sin²θ₁₃≈0.31；CKM矩阵从一般O(1)系数获得CKM类混合的联合概率<2×10⁻⁶。

Conclusion: 阿贝尔群仅有一维表示（one-dimensional representations），导致三代作为独立单态（singlets）产生18个自由参数，远超10个物理可观测量，这是混合结构问题的代数根源；必须转向非阿贝尔味对称性（non-abelian flavor symmetry）如A₄，其三重态表示（triplet representation）可将领头阶自由参数降至4个，才能解释混合结构。此结论适用于左手场不带电荷的模型子类，而对左右手场均分配阿贝尔电荷的模型可规避此问题。

Abstract: Abelian flavor charges on right-handed fermions produce left-handed anarchy: we prove that all abelian discrete Froggatt-Nielsen models with uncharged left-handed doublets yield Haar-random PMNS and CKM matrices, regardless of $\mathbb{Z}_N$ group order, charge assignment, or Majorana mass structure. Scanning $\mathbb{Z}_3$ through $\mathbb{Z}_7$ with 12 charge assignments and $10^5$ Monte Carlo samples each, we demonstrate that the mass spectrum failure previously identified for $\mathbb{Z}_3$ -- the seesaw over-suppression mechanism that pushes $Δm^2_{21}/Δm^2_{31}$ to $\sim 10^{-11}$ -- is specific to $\mathbb{Z}_3$ and avoidable for $N \geq 4$. The mixing angle failure, however, is universal and irreducible. The PMNS angles from every abelian model are statistically consistent with Haar-random unitary matrices, with median $\sin^2θ_{12} \approx \sin^2θ_{23} \approx 0.50$ and $\sin^2θ_{13} \approx 0.31$ across all models tested. The same applies to the CKM: the joint probability of achieving CKM-like mixing from generic $O(1)$ coefficients is $< 2 \times 10^{-6}$. We identify the algebraic origin of this obstruction: abelian groups have only one-dimensional representations, so each generation transforms as an independent singlet with 18 free parameters for three Dirac mass matrices -- far exceeding the 10 physical observables. The transition to non-abelian flavor symmetries such as $A_4$, whose triplet representation reduces free parameters to 4 at leading order, is required specifically for mixing structure. This obstruction applies to the well-motivated subclass of models where left-handed fields are uncharged; models that assign abelian charges to both left- and right-handed fields can evade it.

</details>


### [135] [Integrating out a heavy Higgs singlet: on the edge between SMEFT and HEFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01125)
*Stefan Dittmaier,Sebastian Schuhmacher,Maximilian Stahlhofen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在单态扩展标准模型（SM）中，使用背景场形式和区域展开的功能性方法，在单圈水平上积分掉重希格斯场（H），获得大质量极限下的有效拉格朗日量至$\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^2)$阶，并探讨了参数标度行为如何决定有效理论属于SMEFT还是更一般的HEFT框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于发展一种系统性方法，在标准模型单态扩展中积分掉重希格斯场，获得一致处理希格斯混合和模型重整化效应的有效拉格朗日量。特别关注大质量极限下模型参数的标度行为如何决定有效场论（EFT）框架的选择。

Method: 采用基于背景场形式（background-field formalism）和区域展开（expansion by regions）的功能性方法，在单圈水平上积分掉重希格斯场。选择确保超出标准模型效应在$\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^0)$阶退耦的极限，要求希格斯混合角$\alpha$为$\mathcal{O}(M_h/M_H)$量级，并对其他输入参数施加最小约束。

Result: 获得了大希格斯质量极限下至$\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^2)$阶的有效拉格朗日量，明确证明任何仅包含玻色子SMEFT算符的自下而上（diagrammatic）匹配在$\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^2)$阶必然失败。通过验证多个电弱精确观测量在耦合展开次领头阶的预测差异，确认了有效理论结果的正确性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在大质量极限下，参数标度行为的选择决定了有效理论是否可纳入SMEFT框架，或需要更一般的HEFT框架。所考虑模型限制于无质量费米子，产生的有效场论除标准模型拉格朗日量外仅包含玻色子EFT算符，且完整理论和EFT预测在$M_H$很大时渐近趋近相应的标准模型结果。

Abstract: We use a functional approach based on the background-field formalism and the expansion by regions to integrate out the heavy Higgs field (associated with the mass eigenstate H) in a singlet extension of the Standard Model (SM) at the one-loop level. In this way, we obtain an effective Lagrangian to $\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^2)$ in the limit of large Higgs mass ($M_H \gg M_h\approx125$GeV) providing a consistent treatment of effects from Higgs mixing and the renormalization of the underlying model. In particular, we address how the choice of the scaling behaviour of the model parameters in the large-$M_H$ limit determines whether the effective Lagrangian can be accommodated in the SM Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) or involves non-SMEFT operators within the more general Higgs Effective Field Theory (HEFT) framework. For our calculation, we choose a limit that ensures decoupling of beyond-SM effects at $\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^0)$ by demanding that the Higgs mixing angle $α$ is of $\mathcal{O}(M_h/M_H)$ and putting minimal constraints on the other input parameters, which represents a phenomenologically viable scenario. The considered model is restricted to massless fermions, and the emerging Effective Field Theory (EFT) involves only bosonic EFT operators in addition to the SM Lagrangian. We explicitly show that any attempt of a bottom-up (diagrammatic) matching with only bosonic SMEFT operators at $\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^2)$ necessarily fails. We validate our results for the effective Lagrangian at next-to-leading order in the coupling expansion by verifying that the difference between EFT and full-theory predictions vanishes faster than $1/M_H^2$ for several electroweak precision observables in the large-$M_H$ limit. Moreover, both full-theory and EFT predictions asymptotically approach the corresponding SM results for very large values of $M_H$ as required by decoupling.

</details>

### [136] [Design and performance of a large-area scintillator-based chamber for the MID subsystem of ALICE 3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00176)
*Ruben Alfaro Molina,Juan Carlos Cabanillas Noris,Edmundo García Solis,Laura Helena González Trueba,Varlen Grabski,Gerardo Herrera Corral,Jesús Eduardo Muñoz Méndez,Ildefonso León Monzón,Antonio Ortiz,Antonio Paz,Ian Pérez García,Ricardo Rodríguez Pineda,Solangel Rojas Torres,Guillermo Tejeda Muñoz,Paola Vargas Torres,Victor Vázquez Campos,Yael Antonio Vásquez Beltran*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文报告了ALICE 3升级项目中μ子标识探测器（MID）室的设计与建造。该探测器室包含两层正交排列的闪烁体条，采用机器学习算法进行μ子识别，在CERN T10束流线上测试显示μ子探测效率超过99%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为ALICE 3升级项目的μ子标识探测器（muon identifier detector, MID）设计和建造一个原型室。该研究是ALICE 3意向书中提出的探测器设计的具体实现，旨在验证μ子探测技术的可行性。

Method: 探测器室由两层敏感层组成，中间有1厘米空气间隙。每层包含24个FNAL-NICADD制造的闪烁体条（1×4×100 cm³），配备Kuraray波长位移光纤和Hamamatsu硅光电倍增管（silicon photomultiplier）读出。第二层闪烁体条与第一层正交排列，形成4×4 cm²的重叠单元。在CERN T10束流线上使用3 GeV/c的π子富集束和μ子束进行测试，探测器放置在铁吸收体后方，测试了不同吸收体长度。

Result: 使用机器学习（Machine Learning, ML）算法进行μ子识别，该算法使用μ子（信号）和π子（背景）数据（可用统计数据的50%）进行训练和测试。在μ子数据中应用训练好的ML算法，对于OR条件（在第一层或第二层探测到）的μ子效率超过99%。在π子束数据中，伪μ子效率作为吸收体长度的函数呈指数衰减，斜率参数为18.79厘米。

Conclusion: 该探测器室的设计接近ALICE 3意向书中考虑的设计方案，测试结果表明μ子探测效率优异。论文概述了最终优化的后续步骤，为ALICE 3升级项目的μ子标识探测器开发提供了重要技术验证。

Abstract: This paper reports on the design and construction of a chamber for the muon identifier detector (MID) of the ALICE 3 upgrade project. The chamber consists of two sensitive layers separated by a 1 cm air gap. Each layer holds 24 scintillator bars ($1\times4\times100$ cm$^3$) manufactured by FNAL-NICADD. The bars are equipped with Kuraray wavelength shifting fibers and the readout is provided by a silicon photomultiplier from Hamamatsu. The bars in the second layer are orthogonal to the bars in the first layer, thus providing an overlapping cell size of 4$\times$4 cm$^{2}$. The bar assembly as well as the design of the mechanical structure is described. The design of the chamber is close to that considered in the ALICE 3 letter of intent. The chamber was tested at the CERN T10 beamline using 3 GeV/$c$ pion-enriched and muon beams. The chamber was placed behind an iron absorber, with different absorber lengths considered in the test. The muon identification is performed using a Machine Learning algorithm, which was trained and tested using muon (signal) and pion (background) data (50% of the available statistics). The trained ML algorithm was applied to muon data, yielding a muon efficiency above 99% for the OR condition (detection in either layer 1 or 2). The implementation in the pion-beam data gives the fake-muon efficiency as a function of the absorber length that is well described by an exponential function with a slope parameter of 18.79 cm. The next steps towards finalizing the optimization are outlined.

### [138] [Topology promotes length exploration in microtubule dynamic instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.14109)
*Chongbin Zheng,Jaime Agudo-Canalejo,Jonathon Howard,Evelyn Tang*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于拓扑边缘状态（topological edge states）的微管（microtubule）动力学模型，仅用两个参数即可定量重现实验观测到的灾难长度分布（catastrophe length distribution）及其对微管蛋白浓度（tubulin concentration）的依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微管在灾难事件中会在生长和收缩之间随机切换，其灾难长度分布呈现有限长度的峰值特征，这可能有助于有丝分裂期间对染色体的搜寻。现有模型需要解释这些独特的动力学特征。

Method: 研究者引入了微管双组分帽（two-component microtubule cap）的拓扑模型，其中受保护的边缘状态（protected edge states）产生了微管动力学的不同相：生长、收缩以及最近观察到的"停滞"相（"stutter" phase）。

Result: 该模型仅用两个自由参数即可定量重现实验数据中的峰值灾难长度分布及其对微管蛋白浓度的依赖性。模型进一步提供了灾难长度分布何时出现峰值的解析条件。

Conclusion: 研究表明微管可能利用拓扑边缘状态来促进长度探索，阐明了细胞生物学中搜寻和靶标到达的一种新机制。

Abstract: Microtubules stochastically switch between growth and shrinkage during catastrophe events across a very large range of filament lengths, with the length distribution at catastrophe peaking at a finite filament length, which can aid the search for chromosomes during mitosis. To model these distinct features, we introduce a topological model of a two-component microtubule cap, where protected edge states give rise to different phases of microtubule dynamics - growth, shrinkage, and a recently observed "stutter" phase. With only two free parameters, our model quantitatively reproduces the peaked catastrophe length distribution and its dependence on tubulin concentration from experimental data. The model further provides an analytical condition for when the catastrophe length distribution is peaked. Our work shows how microtubules may utilize topological edge states to promote length exploration, elucidating a novel mechanism for search and target reaching in cellular biology.

### [139] [Nucleoid clustering drives stepwise expansion and segregation of replicating bacterial chromosomes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29719)
*Giada Forte,Enzo Orlandini,Davide Marenduzzo*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过三维聚合物模型揭示细菌染色体复制如何与核蛋白相互作用协同驱动染色体组织和分离，表明细菌染色体是一个非平衡系统，复制力与蛋白质介导的相互作用共同塑造了核仁力学、动力学和分离过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细菌染色体复制缺乏典型纺锤体装置，却能可靠地产生有序且分离的基因组。本研究旨在探索复制驱动的动力学如何与核仁相关蛋白（nucleoid-associated protein, NAP）相互作用共同塑造染色体的时空组织。

Method: 采用三维聚合物模型（three-dimensional polymer model）显式模拟DNA合成，研究复制驱动动力学与核仁相关蛋白介导的相互作用如何共同影响染色体组织。

Result: 核仁相关蛋白介导的相互作用诱导DNA动态聚类，产生核仁密度波动。当与复制耦合时，这些聚类经历应力积累和释放循环，产生与实验观察一致的逐步扩张动力学。染色体分离在此机制中自然发生，但仅存在于有限的相互作用强度范围内。

Conclusion: 细菌染色体组织可被理解为一个非平衡系统（non-equilibrium system），其中复制力与蛋白质介导的相互作用之间的相互作用共同生成核仁力学、动力学和分离过程。

Abstract: Bacterial chromosome replication occurs in the absence of a canonical spindle apparatus; yet it reliably produces organised and segregated genomes. While both passive and active mechanisms have been investigated, DNA replication itself is a non-equilibrium process that continuously generates new genetic material and reorganizes the nucleoid. Here, we investigate how replication-driven dynamics, combined with nucleoid-associated protein (NAP) interactions, shape spatiotemporal chromosome organisation using a three-dimensional polymer model that explicitly simulates DNA synthesis. We show that NAP-mediated interactions induce dynamic clustering of DNA, generating density fluctuations in the nucleoid. When coupled to replication, these clusters undergo cycles of stress buildup and release that produce stepwise expansion dynamics consistent with experimental observations. Chromosome segregation occurs naturally in this regime, but only within a finite range of interaction strengths: weak interactions fail to structure the nucleoid, whereas strong interactions hinder replication progression. Within this optimal balance, replication also promotes the spontaneous formation of replication factories. Our results demonstrate that bacterial chromosome organisation can be understood as a non-equilibrium system in which the interplay between replication forces and protein-mediated interactions generates nucleoid mechanics, dynamics, and segregation.

### [140] [In-vivo entropy production of A. subaru](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00453)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 虽然熵产生能够提供非平衡系统能量消耗的理论下界，但在实际宏观系统中，该下界与真实值存在巨大差距（约25个数量级），表明其作为能量消耗代理指标的实用性有限。研究通过系统比较不同估计方法和提出新的kNN估计器，确保了结果的可靠性。

Abstract: Entropy production is often used as a proxy for energy consumption of a non-equilibrium system. Lower bounds can be estimated from coarse-grained observations, and this has been done for various biological systems. Here, we apply these tools to a more macroscopic system whose true energy consumption is also known. We find that while entropy production does give a lower bound, it is some 25 orders of magnitude away from being saturated. To be certain of this result, we survey different methods of estimating irreversibility, and write down a novel kNN estimator.

### [141] [Predictability is dynamically constructed by topological collective modes in deterministic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01088)
*Lars Koopmans,Elinor M. Kay,Hyun Youk*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 该研究表明，确定性多体系统的可预测性可以动态构建而非编码于初始配置中。通过研究分泌-感知细胞的自组织行为，发现宏观命运仅在轨迹后期才出现可预测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为确定性多体系统的长期行为由初始配置决定。本研究挑战这一假设，探索可预测性如何动态构建而非静态编码于初始状态。

Method: 研究采用广义细胞自动机模型，模拟分泌-感知细胞（secrete-and-sense cells）的自组织行为。将细胞状态视为离散相场，识别涌现的拓扑模式，包括带电涡旋及其连接弦形成的不可收缩环。

Result: 系统可从无序状态自组织为静态配置、直线波或螺旋波。虽然动力学是确定性的，但仅从初始状态无法可靠推断最终结果。宏观命运的可预测特征仅在轨迹后期出现：涡旋湮灭通过环损失可读，而涡旋持续存在直到螺旋波突然形成才可读。

Conclusion: 研究证明确定性非平衡系统中的可预测性可以动态构建，而非预先编码于初始配置。这一发现挑战了传统对确定性系统长期行为可预测性的理解。

Abstract: Deterministic many-body systems governed by simple interactions can self-organize into macroscopic patterns, and the determinants of long-time behavior are assumed to be encoded in the initial configuration. Here we show that predictability can instead be constructed dynamically rather than being accessible in the initial configuration. We study a generalized cellular automaton of secrete-and-sense cells that self-organizes from disorder into static configurations, rectilinear waves, or spiral waves. Although dynamics are deterministic, the final outcome cannot be reliably inferred from the initial state alone. Treating cell states as a discrete phase field, we uncover emergent topological modes - charged vortices connected by strings that form non-contractible loops. Tracking their dynamics reveals that predictive signatures of macroscopic fate appear only late in the trajectory: vortex annihilation becomes readable through loop loss, whereas vortex persistence remains unreadable until spiral waves form abruptly. These results show how predictability can be dynamically constructed in deterministic nonequilibrium systems.

</details>

# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [142] [Temporal Memory for Resource-Constrained Agents: Continual Learning via Stochastic Compress-Add-Smooth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00067)
*Michael Chertkov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于桥扩散（Bridge Diffusion）的持续学习框架，将记忆建模为随机过程而非参数向量，通过压缩-添加-平滑（CAS）递归整合新经验，在固定内存预算下实现经验保留与遗忘的精确控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 序列操作智能体需要在固定内存预算下整合新经验而不遗忘旧经验。传统方法通常将记忆视为参数向量，存在参数干扰导致的遗忘问题，需要一种新的记忆表示框架。

Method: 提出将记忆建模为回放区间$[0,1]$上的桥扩散（Bridge Diffusion）随机过程，其终端边际编码当前状态，中间边际编码过去经验。采用压缩-添加-平滑（Compress--Add--Smooth, CAS）三步递归整合新经验，使用固定分量数$K$的高斯混合模型表示边际概率密度，通过固定段数$L$的分段线性协议控制时间复杂性。

Result: 该框架计算成本为$O(LKd^2)$次浮点运算每天，无需反向传播、存储数据或神经网络。遗忘源于有损时间压缩而非参数干扰，保留半衰期线性缩放为$a_{1/2}\approx c\,L$，其中常数$c>1$具有信息论解释。桥扩散过程提供时间连贯的"电影"式回放，形成完全解析的持续学习"伊辛模型"。

Conclusion: 该框架为持续学习提供了完全解析的数学模型，能够精确研究遗忘机制、速率和形式。桥扩散表示实现了时间连贯的经验回放，常数$c$的信息论解释类似于香农信道容量，为理解记忆保留提供了理论基础。

Abstract: An agent that operates sequentially must incorporate new experience without forgetting old experience, under a fixed memory budget. We propose a framework in which memory is not a parameter vector but a stochastic process: a Bridge Diffusion on a replay interval $[0,1]$, whose terminal marginal encodes the present and whose intermediate marginals encode the past. New experience is incorporated via a three-step \emph{Compress--Add--Smooth} (CAS) recursion. We test the framework on the class of models with marginal probability densities modeled via Gaussian mixtures of fixed number of components~$K$ in $d$ dimensions; temporal complexity is controlled by a fixed number~$L$ of piecewise-linear protocol segments whose nodes store Gaussian-mixture states. The entire recursion costs $O(LKd^2)$ flops per day -- no backpropagation, no stored data, no neural networks -- making it viable for controller-light hardware.
  Forgetting in this framework arises not from parameter interference but from lossy temporal compression: the re-approximation of a finer protocol by a coarser one under a fixed segment budget. We find that the retention half-life scales linearly as $a_{1/2}\approx c\,L$ with a constant $c>1$ that depends on the dynamics but not on the mixture complexity~$K$, the dimension~$d$, or the geometry of the target family. The constant~$c$ admits an information-theoretic interpretation analogous to the Shannon channel capacity. The stochastic process underlying the bridge provides temporally coherent ``movie'' replay -- compressed narratives of the agent's history, demonstrated visually on an MNIST latent-space illustration. The framework provides a fully analytical ``Ising model'' of continual learning in which the mechanism, rate, and form of forgetting can be studied with mathematical precision.

</details>

Conclusion: 可持续进展依赖于开放数据与模型、可复用工作流以及领域专用AI系统，这些要素能最大化单位计算量的科学价值。同时必须弥合理想化计算预测与现实条件间的差距，考虑可合成性与多目标设计标准，这对实际应用至关重要。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence is transforming molecular and materials science, but its growing computational and data demands raise critical sustainability challenges. In this Perspective, we examine resource considerations across the AI-driven discovery pipeline--from quantum-mechanical (QM) data generation and model training to automated, self-driving research workflows--building on discussions from the ``SusML workshop: Towards sustainable exploration of chemical spaces with machine learning'' held in Dresden, Germany. In this context, the availability of large quantum datasets has enabled rigorous benchmarking and rapid methodological progress, while also incurring substantial energy and infrastructure costs. We highlight emerging strategies to enhance efficiency, including general-purpose machine learning (ML) models, multi-fidelity approaches, model distillation, and active learning. Moreover, incorporating physics-based constraints within hierarchical workflows, where fast ML surrogates are applied broadly and high-accuracy QM methods are used selectively, can further optimize resource use without compromising reliability. Equally important is bridging the gap between idealized computational predictions and real-world conditions by accounting for synthesizability and multi-objective design criteria, which is essential for practical impact. Finally, we argue that sustainable progress will rely on open data and models, reusable workflows, and domain-specific AI systems that maximize scientific value per unit of computation, enabling efficient and responsible discovery of technological materials and therapeutics.

### [144] [Bridging the Simulation-to-Experiment Gap with Generative Models using Adversarial Distribution Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01169)
*Kai Nelson,Tobias Kreiman,Sergey Levine,Aditi S. Krishnapriyan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种对抗性分布对齐（Adversarial Distribution Alignment, ADA）框架，通过预训练生成模型于模拟数据，然后将其与实验观测数据对齐，以弥合模拟与实验之间的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学与工程中的核心挑战是模拟与实验之间的差距（simulation-to-experiment gap）。物理定律通常难以对复杂系统精确求解，而模拟器（simulators）会引入计算近似；实验测量虽更真实地反映现实，但通常只能部分观测系统状态。

Method: 提出数据驱动的分布对齐框架：首先在完全观测但存在缺陷的模拟数据上预训练生成模型，然后将其与部分但真实的实验观测数据对齐。具体引入对抗性分布对齐（Adversarial Distribution Alignment, ADA）方法，该方法将原子位置（atomic positions）的生成模型（最初基于模拟的玻尔兹曼分布训练）与实验观测分布对齐。

Result: 理论证明该方法能够恢复目标可观测分布，即使存在多个潜在相关的可观测变量。在合成数据、分子数据和实验蛋白质数据上进行了实证验证，表明该方法能够将生成模型与多样化的可观测变量对齐。

Conclusion: 提出的对抗性分布对齐框架能够有效弥合模拟与实验之间的差距，通过将模拟训练的生成模型与真实实验观测对齐，为物理科学等领域提供了一种通用的数据驱动解决方案。

Abstract: A fundamental challenge in science and engineering is the simulation-to-experiment gap. While we often possess prior knowledge of physical laws, these physical laws can be too difficult to solve exactly for complex systems. Such systems are commonly modeled using simulators, which impose computational approximations. Meanwhile, experimental measurements more faithfully represent the real world, but experimental data typically consists of observations that only partially reflect the system's full underlying state. We propose a data-driven distribution alignment framework that bridges this simulation-to-experiment gap by pre-training a generative model on fully observed (but imperfect) simulation data, then aligning it with partial (but real) observations of experimental data. While our method is domain-agnostic, we ground our approach in the physical sciences by introducing Adversarial Distribution Alignment (ADA). This method aligns a generative model of atomic positions -- initially trained on a simulated Boltzmann distribution -- with the distribution of experimental observations. We prove that our method recovers the target observable distribution, even with multiple, potentially correlated observables. We also empirically validate our framework on synthetic, molecular, and experimental protein data, demonstrating that it can align generative models with diverse observables. Our code is available at https://kaityrusnelson.com/ada/.

</details>
