### [145] [Evidence of Metallic Wigner Crystal in Rhombohedral Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00113)
*Tonghang Han,Jackson P. Butler,Shenyong Ye,Zhenqi Hua,Surajit Dutta,Zach Hadjri,Zhenghan Wu,Jixiang Yang,Junseok Seo,Phatthanon Pattanakanvijit,Emily Aitken,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Peng Xiong,Eli Zeldov,Zhengguang Lu,Raymond Ashoori,Long Ju*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究在菱面体多层石墨烯中观测到维格纳晶体（Wigner crystal）和金属性维格纳晶体（metallic Wigner crystal）的输运证据，为探索新型电子晶体相提供了实验平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统维格纳晶体已在二维电子气和朗道能级中实现，但更奇异的电子晶体相如金属性维格纳晶体（mWC）虽被理论预言却难以实现。非抛物线型电子能带和量子几何可能促进这类新型拓扑电子晶体的形成。

Method: 研究采用菱面体四层、五层和六层石墨烯，在电荷密度0.3-0.5×10¹² cm⁻²范围内，通过栅极控制的位移场（displacement field）D调控导带平坦度，测量输运特性。

Result: 实验观测到非零电荷密度下的绝缘态，表现出非线性、滞回电流-电压关系，这是钉扎维格纳晶体（pinned WC）的特征。进一步增加D后，输运由空穴型载流子主导，其密度仅为标称电子密度的15%，符合金属性维格纳晶体（mWC）预期。mWC态在约0.4 T附近显示量子霍尔效应起始，且违反Streda关系。

Conclusion: 菱面体石墨烯为探索新型电子晶体、可能的非平凡拓扑结构以及新的集体模式提供了实验平台。金属性维格纳晶体与维格纳晶体紧密关联，两者随温度或偏压增加同时瓦解。

Abstract: When the Coulomb interaction dominates over kinetic energy, electrons can crystallize into a Wigner crystal (WC). This paradigmatic correlated electronic phase has been realized in two-dimensional electron gases with parabolic band dispersion and completely flat Landau levels under high magnetic fields. Beyond these conventional contexts of electron crystallization, more exotic electron crystals have been postulated but remain unexplored. For example, a metallic Wigner crystal (mWC), in which itinerant carriers coexist with a pinned electron lattice, has been proposed theoretically but considered difficult to realize. Non-parabolic electron bands and quantum geometry may facilitate mWC and other novel topological electron crystals. Here we report transport evidence for WC and mWC in rhombohedral tetra-, penta-, and hexalayer graphene in the charge density range 0.3-0.5x10^12 cm^-2. By flattening the conduction band with a gate-controlled displacement field D, we observe an insulating state at nonzero charge density that shows nonlinear, hysteretic current-voltage relations, signatures of a pinned WC, that are absent from the lower-density insulator. Further increasing D reveals transport dominated by hole-like carriers with density up to only 15% of the nominal electron density, consistent with mWC. This mWC state is closely tied to the WC state, as both collapse simultaneously with increasing temperature or bias voltage. The mWC state shows quantum Hall onset near 0.4 T and disobeys the Streda relation, indicating compressible charge exchange between itinerant holes and the transport-inert WC background. Our results establish rhombohedral graphene as a platform for exploring novel electron crystals, as well as possible nontrivial topology, and new collective modes.

</details>


### [146] [A footprint of zero-point entropy in higher-temperature magnetic thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00115)
*Sergey Syzranov,Arthur P. Ramirez*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种检测非零零点熵（zero-point entropy）的简单方法：通过麦克斯韦关系（Maxwell's relation）的违反现象来识别，并推导出在特征温度下非零零点熵的判据条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验上通过测量材料从高温冷却到低温释放的熵来寻找零点熵（ZPE）的方法往往不可靠且存在争议，因为可及温度可能不足以准确捕捉磁性材料的关键低温和高温特征。

Method: 利用麦克斯韦关系 $\left(\partial S/\partial H\right)_T = \left(\partial M/\partial T\right)_H$ 的违反现象作为非零零点熵的简单可及特征；当错误假设零点熵为零时，该关系会表现出违反。

Result: 推导出在特征温度下非零零点熵的简单判据形式：$\left(\frac{\partial C}{\partial H}\right)_T\left(\frac{\partial M}{\partial T}\right)_H<0$；该关系还可用于估算零点熵的大小。

Conclusion: 通过深入研究过的自旋冰材料 $Dy_2Ti_2O_7$ 作为基准测试案例，讨论了这些效应和非零零点熵的特征，为识别自旋液体候选材料和自旋冰中的广泛简并基态提供了新方法。

Abstract: Identifying extensively degenerate zero-temperature states is key in characterizing spin-liquid-candidate materials and spin ices. In experiments, finding zero-point entropy (ZPE) is often attempted by measuring the entropy released by a material when cooled down from very high to very low temperatures. Such investigations are often unreliable and lead to controversial results because accessible temperatures may be insufficient to accurately capture essential low- and high-temperature features of magnetic materials. The purpose of this paper is to point out a simple, easily accessible signature of nonzero ZPE: the Maxwell's relation $\left(\partial S/\partial H\right)_T = \left(\partial M/\partial T\right)_H$ can appear violated if a vanishing ZPE is assumed incorrectly. This relation can further be used for estimating the ZPE. In many materials below characteristic temperatures, the criterion of non-vanishing ZPE has a particularly simple form: $\left(\frac{\partial C}{\partial H}\right)_T\left(\frac{\partial M}{\partial T}\right)_H<0$. We discuss these effects and the ZPE signature in the benchmark test case of the well-studied spin ice $Dy_2Ti_2O_7$.

</details>


### [147] [Dielectric control of ultrafast carrier dynamics and transport in graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00217)
*Hai I. Wang,Xiaoyu Jia,Anand Nivedan,Mischa Bonn,Aron W. Cummings,Alessandro Principi,Klaas-Jan Tielrooij*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过调控石墨烯的介电环境来控制其超快载流子动力学，无需改变费米能、光功率或环境温度。增强的介电屏蔽抑制了载流子-载流子相互作用，减缓了加热和冷却过程，同时提高了电荷迁移率和塞贝克系数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解石墨烯中光激发电荷的超快动力学至关重要，因为这些微观机制决定了石墨烯的光学、光热和光电特性。这些特性对于石墨烯实现高速光电探测器等功能和设备至关重要，因此除了科学理解外，控制超快载流子动力学对实际应用也极为重要。

Method: 通过工程化调控石墨烯的介电环境来控制载流子动力学，同时结合光学泵浦-太赫兹探针实验与理论计算。该方法无需改变费米能、光功率或环境温度。

Result: 介电屏蔽抑制了载流子-载流子相互作用并减缓了动力学过程。具体而言，减少的载流子-载流子散射延迟了准平衡热电子分布的形成，从而减缓了载流子加热；同时由于光学声子发射后的再热化依赖于相同的相互作用，也减缓了载流子冷却。增强的屏蔽进一步降低了电子-空穴池的能量，从而提高了电荷迁移率和塞贝克系数。

Conclusion: 这种外部控制石墨烯内部动力学和输运特性的能力使得器件性能得以优化，例如提高用于数据通信和无线通信应用的光电探测器的灵敏度。

Abstract: Understanding the ultrafast dynamics of photoexcited charges in graphene is essential, as the microscopic mechanisms underlying these dynamics determine many of graphene's optical, optothermal, and optoelectronic properties. These are crucial properties for many functionalities and devices enabled by graphene, such as high-speed photodectors. Therefore, beyond scientific understanding, it is highly desirable to control ultrafast carrier dynamics for practical applications. Here, we establish this control by engineering the dielectric environment of graphene, thereby regulating both heating and cooling dynamics without altering the Fermi energy, optical power, or ambient temperature. By combining optical pump-terahertz probe experiments with theoretical calculations, we show that dielectric screening suppresses carrier-carrier interactions and slows the dynamics. In particular, reduced carrier-carrier scattering delays the formation of a quasi-equilibrium hot electron distribution, thus slowing carrier heating. It also slows carrier cooling because re-thermalization after optical-phonon emission depends on the same interactions. The enhanced screening further reduces the energy of electron-hole puddles, thereby increasing charge mobility and the Seebeck coefficient. This ability to externally control internal graphene dynamics and transport properties enables the optimization of device performance, such as the sensitivity of photodetectors for data communication and wireless communication applications.

</details>


### [148] [Field-unmasked quantum geometry in a symmetry-forbidden photocurrent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00221)
*Bumseop Kim,Aaron M. Burger,Zhenbang Dai,Sayed Ali Akbar Ghorashi,Adam Abirou,Md Al Helal,Vladmir M. Fridkin,Jonathan E. Spanier,Andrew M. Rappe*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过缺陷调控的场选择对称性破缺机制，揭示了手性立方硅酸盐中隐藏的量子几何响应，激活了原本被禁止的非线性光电流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 频率和偏振分辨的光电流（frequency- and polarization-resolved photocurrents）是探测量子材料中隐藏对称性和能带几何结构的灵敏探针。本研究旨在解决手性立方硅酸盐（chiral cubic sillenite）中观察到的纵向奇B磁光电流（longitudinal odd-in-B magneto-photocurrent）与全局晶体对称性禁止之间的矛盾。

Method: 结合实验观测与第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），研究通过氧空位（O vacancies）缺陷分析，揭示了场选择自旋有序化（field-selected spin ordering）机制。动量分辨计算（momentum-resolved calculations）用于关联Berry曲率（Berry-curvature）和量子度量（quantum-metric）丰富的布里渊区区域。

Result: 实验观察到显著的纵向响应，具有强螺旋选择性（helicity selectivity），圆偏振通道超过线性通道且随光螺旋性切换而反转符号。计算表明氧空位产生带隙内束缚态（in-gap bound states）和局域磁矩，强自旋轨道耦合（strong SOC）使其稳定。外加磁场选择时间反演破缺的缺陷系综，降低有效磁对称性，从而解除纵向选择规则。

Conclusion: 场选择缺陷对称性降低（field-selected defect symmetry lowering）是揭示手性量子材料中隐藏量子几何结构并激活禁止非线性光电流的有效途径。该机制不仅激活了名义上禁止的光电流，还揭示了电子结构中编码的潜在量子几何响应。

Abstract: Frequency- and polarization-resolved photocurrents provide a sensitive probe of hidden symmetry and band geometry in quantum materials. Here we study a chiral cubic sillenite whose global crystal symmetry forbids a longitudinal odd-in-B magneto-photocurrent in the Voigt geometry. Nevertheless, we observe a pronounced longitudinal response across the visible range that is predominantly linear in magnetic field, persists below the band gap, and exhibits strong helicity selectivity, with the circular channel exceeding the linear one and reversing sign upon switching light helicity. We resolve this apparent contradiction by identifying defect-enabled, field-selected spin ordering as the mechanism that lowers the effective magnetic symmetry without altering the global crystal structure. First-principles calculations show that O vacancies generate in-gap bound states and localized magnetic moments on neighboring Bi-O units, stabilized by strong SOC. Although symmetry-related vacancy configurations remain energetically degenerate and preserve the macroscopic T symmetry at zero field, an applied magnetic field selects a time-reversal-broken sector of the defect ensemble and reduces the effective magnetic symmetry to the subgroup that leaves B invariant, thereby lifting the longitudinal selection rule. Importantly, this field-selected symmetry reduction does more than activate a nominally forbidden photocurrent: it unmasks latent quantum-geometric responses encoded in the electronic structure. Momentum-resolved calculations show that the dominant circular and linear magneto-photocurrent channels spatially correlate with Berry-curvature-rich and quantum-metric-rich regions of the Brillouin zone, respectively. Our results establish field-selected defect symmetry lowering as a route to revealing hidden quantum geometry and activating forbidden nonlinear photocurrents in chiral quantum materials.

</details>


### [149] [Directly visualizing the energy level structure of quantum dot molecules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00232)
*Heun Mo Yoo,Tanner M. Janda,Connor Nasseraddin,Jason R. Petta*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅量子点中的轨道、自旋和谷自由度支持多种自旋量子比特操作模式，但传统方法难以在大范围参数空间内获取能级谱信息。

Method: 研究者开发了一种光谱技术，能够映射双量子点能级结构随能级失谐、点间隧穿耦合和磁场变化的函数关系。

Result: 在单电子区，直接观测到从孤立量子点的原子态能级到分子态成键与反键态的转变；在磁场中解析了基态和激发态谷态的塞曼分裂；在双电子区获得了失谐依赖的单重态-三重态劈裂。

Abstract: The orbital, spin and valley degrees of freedom in silicon quantum dots support many modes of spin qubit operation. However, it is generally challenging to obtain information about the energy level spectrum over large ranges of parameter space. We demonstrate a form of spectroscopy that is capable of mapping the energy level structure of a double quantum dot as a function of level detuning, interdot tunnel coupling, and magnetic field. In the one electron regime, we directly observe the transition from the atom like energy levels of isolated quantum dots to molecular like bonding and anti bonding states with increasing interdot tunnel coupling. We also resolve the Zeeman splitting of ground and excited valley states in a magnetic field. In the two electron regime, we gain access to the detuning dependent singlet triplet splitting. Our work may be extended to a broader class of systems, such as strong spin-orbit materials or proximitized quantum dots, allowing the direct extraction of various energy gaps.

### [150] [Nonlinear Frequency-Momentum Topology and Doubling of Multifold Exceptional Points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00366)
*Tsuneya Yoshida*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文建立了n重异常点（EPn）的倍增定理，引入了频率-动量绕数作为新的拓扑不变量，统一描述了线性与非线性系统中异常点的拓扑特性，并揭示了PT对称EP2s的ℤ拓扑结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多重复合异常点（higher-order exceptional points）在布里渊区（Brillouin zone）的拓扑特性缺乏普适表征，现有倍增定理（doubling theorem）主要局限于二重异常点（two-fold exceptional points）。需要建立适用于任意n重异常点的统一理论框架。

Method: 引入新的拓扑不变量——频率-动量绕数（frequency-momentum winding numbers），用于表征m带系统中任意n重异常点（n≤m）的拓扑特性。该方法适用于非线性通过本征值进入的系统，并能推广到一类耦合谐振器系统。

Result: 频率-动量绕数实现了倍增定理在无对称性及多种对称约束（包括宇称-时间对称性（parity-time symmetry）和电荷共轭宇称对称性）下的统一证明。在线性极限下，该不变量揭示了PT对称EP2s的ℤ拓扑结构，超越了先前报道的ℤ₂拓扑。

Conclusion: 频率-动量绕数为多重复合异常点的拓扑表征提供了普适框架，统一了线性与非线性系统中的异常点理论，并扩展了对称性约束下的拓扑分类。

Abstract: Even in the linear limit, the topology of multifold (also called higher-order) exceptional points across the Brillouin zone has lacked a general characterization, leaving the doubling theorem essentially limited to two-fold exceptional points. Here, we establish the doubling theorem of $n$-fold exceptional points [EP$n$s ($n=2,3,\ldots$)] for systems where nonlinearity enters through eigenvalues. To this end, we introduce new topological invariants, termed frequency-momentum winding numbers, which characterize nonlinear EP$n$s in $m$-band systems throughout the Brillouin zone for arbitrary $n$ and $m$ ($m\geq n$). These invariants enable a unified proof of the doubling theorem in the absence of symmetry and under several symmetry constraints, including parity-time ($PT$) and charge-conjugation-parity symmetries. Furthermore, even in the linear limit, the frequency-momentum winding number indicates $\mathbb{Z}$ topology of $PT$-symmetric EP$2$s which is beyond the previously reported $\mathbb{Z}_2$ topology. The frequency-momentum winding numbers can also be extended to a class of coupled resonators in which nonlinearity enters via the eigenvectors, whereas the spectrum is determined by a nonlinear scalar equation for the frequency.

</details>


### [151] [Gate-Tunable Photoresponse of Graphene Josephson Junctions at Terahertz Frequencies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00409)

Method: 研究通过低强度太赫兹辐照观察临界电流的显著抑制，在电流偏置下产生强光电压（photovoltage）。通过追踪光电压并独立测量电子温度随吸收功率的变化，提取了器件的响应度和噪声等效功率。

Result: 在1.7 K温度下获得了88 kV W^-1的响应度和45 aW Hz^-1/2的噪声等效功率。栅极可调性使器件能在高达0.9 K温度下保持滞回电流-电压特性，为实现超越毫开尔文（mK）温度的单光子太赫兹探测提供了可能路径。

Abstract: Graphene Josephson junctions (JJ) provide a promising platform for ultra-broadband quantum sensing of light owing to graphene's frequency-independent absorption, vanishing electronic heat capacity, and weak electron-phonon coupling, which enable rapid suppression of the critical current through radiation-induced electron heating. Existing investigations have been confined to the microwave and infrared regimes, where competing detector technologies are already established; by contrast, the terahertz (THz) band - where sensitivity is most urgently lacking and no mature quantum sensor exists - has remained largerly unexplored. Here we demonstrate a strong photoresponse of graphene JJs at THz frequencies, establishing a first experimental step towards graphene-based THz quantum sensors. Under low-intensity illumination, we observe a pronounced suppression of the critical current that generates a strong photovoltage (Vph) under current bias. By tracking this Vph and independently measuring the electron temperature as a function of absorbed power, we extract a responsivity of 88 kV W^-1 and a noise-equivalent power of 45 aW Hz^-1/2 at 1.7 K. Furthermore, gate tunability of our JJ enables access to a regime where hysteretic current-voltage characteristics persist up to 0.9 K, offering a potential route toward single-photon THz detection beyond millikelvin (mK) temperatures. These findings establish graphene JJ as a versatile platform for broadband cryogenic radiation sensing and point towards their use as quantum sensors at THz frequencies.

### [152] [Electronic Raman scattering from 2D metals with broken inversion symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00486)
*Mojdeh Saleh,Saurabh Maiti*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于电子拉曼散射（eRS）的理论，用于探测缺乏反演对称性金属中的自旋轨道耦合（SOC）效应。研究表明，在SU(2)对称性破缺条件下，eRS能够耦合自旋激发，无需激光调谐至内部共振，且信号强度在石墨烯系统中比传统二维电子气（2DEG）强数个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属中反演对称性的缺失导致SU(2)对称性破缺，产生由Dresselhaus、Rashba或Ising（亦称谷Zeeman）等自旋轨道耦合（SOC）引起的费米能级电子态自旋劈裂。这种劈裂不仅支持非相干自旋翻转激发和相干手性自旋模式，还引入了直接的自旋-光子相互作用，为探测SOC效应提供了新途径。

Method: 利用SU(2)对称性破缺引入的直接自旋-光子相互作用，构建了此类系统中电荷载流子非弹性光子散射理论[电子拉曼散射（eRS）]。作为具体实现，研究了具有强SOC衬底上掺杂/门控石墨烯，比较了包含不同Rashba和谷Zeeman SOC组合的谱图与模型二维电子气（2DEG）的差异。

Result: 研究表明，与传统拉曼散射理论不同，eRS探针在SU(2)破缺条件下能够耦合自旋激发，无需激光调谐至内部共振。光子散射诱导的自旋相关激发对偏振几何构型以及低能态希尔伯特空间的自旋结构敏感。在选定偏振几何构型中，SOC劈裂能量附近出现共振特征，且石墨烯与2DEG系统的谱图存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 石墨烯系统的eRS信号强度比2DEG强数个数量级，这归因于其大的狄拉克速度。谱图的线形可用于推断系统中SOC的各种组分，为探测缺乏反演对称性金属中的自旋轨道耦合效应提供了有效的理论框架和实验手段。

Abstract: Lack of inversion symmetry in metals breaks SU(2) symmetry which results in spin-splitting of the electronic states at the Fermi level due to various types of spin-orbit coupling (SOC) such as Dresselhaus, Rashba, or Ising (also called valley-Zeeman). This splitting is known to enable both incoherent spin-flip excitations and coherent chiral-spin modes. Another effect of breaking of SU(2) is the introduction of a direct spin-photon interaction. We use this concept to formulate a theory of inelastic scattering of photons from the charge carriers of such a system [electronic Raman scattering (eRS)]. As a result of broken SU(2), we show that the eRS probe, unlike conventional theory of Raman scattering, couples to spin excitations even without tuning the laser to an internal resonance. We show that the spin dependent excitations induced by photon scattering are sensitive to the polarization geometries as well as to the spin structure of the Hilbert space of the low-energy states. As a concrete realization, we examine doped/gated graphene on substrates with strong SOC with various compositions of Rashba and valley-Zeeman SOC and compare their spectra with those for a model 2D electron gas (2DEG). The spectra are shown to have a resonant feature in select polarization geometries near the SOC-splitting energy and, importantly, is shown to be different in the two systems. The signal in graphene systems is shown to be stronger than that in a 2DEG by orders of magnitude owing to the large Dirac velocity. We also outline how the lineshapes from the spectra can be used to infer various components of SOC in the system.

</details>

Method: 结合高质量输运实验与从头算（ab initio）计算，采用动态屏蔽远程相互作用的适当处理方法，系统分析电子与hBN声子的耦合机制。

Abstract: We study the impact of BN's phonons on the electrical resistivity of hBN-encapsulated graphene. While encapsulation yields high-mobility devices, the surrounding BN itself introduces remote scattering from polar optical phonons, whose role in standard resistivity measurements remains unclear. We combine high-quality transport experiments with ab initio calculations including a proper treatment of dynamically screened remote interactions. We demonstrate that hBN's out-of-plane phonons strongly influence resistivity between 150 K and room temperature, whereas higher-energy LO modes and intrinsic graphene phonons alone cannot explain the observed trends. The coupling between electrons and the BN's phonons becomes more pronounced at low carrier densities due to reduced screening. Our findings establish that remote phonon scattering fundamentally limits transport in encapsulated graphene, solving a longstanding debate.

By varying the staggered sublattice potential and intrinsic spin-orbit coupling, we identify distinct topological regimes and analyze their manifestations in the emergence of Landau levels, the evolution of the density of states, and the characteristics of M-O absorption spectra. Using the Kubo formalism, we compute the longitudinal and Hall M-O conductivities and show that inter-Landau-level (inter-LL) transitions produce characteristic resonance features that provide optical signatures of the underlying topological phases. This analysis reveals that, at sufficiently high nonlinearities, a nonlinearity-induced topological phase transition occurs, marked by a discontinuity in the nonlinear Zak phase. The second approach amounts to numerically obtaining other (non-Bloch) solutions under open boundary conditions, employing the Self-Consistent Field Iterative Method. Its main results include the observation of an edge state's energy that is independent of a nonlinear parameter, a persisting band touching point that only shifts in the presence of perturbations reminiscent of Weyl points in a Weyl semimetal, as well as delocalized solutions that persist even at extreme nonlinearity strengths. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究一维和二维极化激元凝聚体中相位动力学呈现KPZ标度行为的物理起源。KPZ普适类（KPZ universality class）在非平衡量子系统中的出现机制尚需深入理解。

Method: 采用数值模拟（numerical simulations）与解析理论（analytical theory）相结合的方法。通过分析由$U(1)$对称性自发破缺（spontaneous breaking of $U(1)$ symmetry）产生的Goldstone激发（Goldstone excitations）的动力学来研究KPZ标度行为。

Result: 研究证实描述KPZ普适类的临界指数（critical exponents）直接源于Goldstone激发的动力学。Goldstone模的布居数涨落是导致观测到的一阶关联函数$g^{(1)}$幂律行为的关键机制。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了激子-极化激元凝聚体阵列的微观参数与其发射光相干特性之间的直接联系，为理解非平衡量子系统中的KPZ标度行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: This work investigates the origin of Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ) scaling in the phase dynamics of one-dimensional and two-dimensional polariton condensates. We demonstrate that the key mechanism leading to the observed power laws for the first-order correlation function $g^{(1)}$ is the fluctuation of the population of Goldstone modes, which arise due to the spontaneous breaking of $U(1)$ symmetry. Numerical simulations and analytical theory confirm that the critical exponents describing the KPZ universality class directly follow from the dynamics of Goldstone excitations. Our results establish a direct connection between the microscopic parameters of arrays of exciton-polariton condensates and the coherent properties of the light they emit.

</details>


### [159] [Nonreciprocal spin waves of helical magnetization states in CoFeB/NiFe bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00922)
*Claudia Negrete,Omar J. Suarez,Attila Kákay,Jorge A. Otálora*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在阐明CoFeB/NiFe双层结构中螺旋平衡态的非互易自旋波特性，特别是频率偏移的物理机制。当前文献通常将频率偏移仅归因于偶极相互作用，而本研究试图揭示层间交换相互作用的重要贡献。

Method: 通过扩展动态矩阵形式（dynamic matrix formalism）至异质结构多层系统厚度方向上的任意非共线配置，分析双层厚度上反向传播模式的自旋波模式分布差异。该方法考虑了动态偶极和层间交换相互作用的差异。

Result: 研究发现层间交换相互作用在频率偏移中扮演关键角色，而当前文献未充分考量此因素。同时观察到大的频率偏移值与亚100纳米自旋波波长的组合，这些特性可通过外加磁场调节螺旋磁化态的扭曲程度以及NiFe亚层厚度进行调控或增强。

Conclusion: 研究通过扩展的动态矩阵形式揭示了层间交换相互作用在非互易自旋波频率偏移中的重要作用，修正了当前文献仅关注偶极相互作用的观点。这些发现对于磁子学（magnonic）应用具有高度相关性，并通过近期模拟和实验结果验证了模型与物理机制。

Abstract: We investigated the nonreciprocal spin-wave properties, including the frequency shift, of a helical equilibrium state in a versatile CoFeB/NiFe bilayer. Through an extension of the dynamic matrix formalism (developed in this work) to an arbitrary non-collinear configuration along a heterostructured multilayered system thickness, we explained the frequency shift via differences in the dynamic dipolar and interlayer exchange interactions arising from the distinct spin-wave mode profiles across the bilayer thickness for counterpropagating modes at the same wave vector. In contrast to recent literature wherein the frequency shift is attributed solely to the dipolar interaction, our results and explanations hereby presented involve a starring role of the interlayer exchange interaction not accounted in current literature. Furthermore, we also found a combination of large frequency shift values and sub-100 nm spin wave wavelengths that can be tuned or even enhanced with the twisting degree of the helical magnetization state by the application of the external field, and with the thickness of the NiFe sublayer, which might be highly relevant for magnonic applications. We validated our model and the physical mechanism that explains the frequency shift using recent simulations and experimental results.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用基于锗的可扩展2xN架构，构建了18量子比特阵列。通过并行操作模块化单元（modular unit cells），实现了整个阵列的同步初始化、控制和读取。

Abstract: Utility-scale quantum computing requires the integration and operation of a large-scale qubit register. Semiconductor spin qubits are a primary candidate for this, due to the prospects of building integrated hybrid quantum-classical architectures. However, scaling spin-qubit systems while preserving performance and control has remained a challenge. Here, we demonstrate the operation of an 18-qubit array in germanium based on an extendable 2xN architecture. We achieve simultaneous initialization, control, and readout across the entire array, enabled by parallel operation of modular unit cells. Across the array, we achieve average and median single-qubit gate fidelities of 99.8% and 99.9%, respectively. Finally, we characterize the nearest-neighbor exchange couplings throughout the device and implement high-quality controlled-Z gates to generate a three-qubit Greenberger-Horne-Zeilinger (GHZ) state. These results demonstrate that spin-qubit arrays can be scaled while maintaining high-fidelity operation and establish a modular, extendable architecture for planar semiconductor quantum processors.

### [161] [FerBo: a noise resilient qubit hybridizing Andreev and fluxonium states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01145)
*J. J. Caceres,D. Sanz Marco,J. Ortuzar,E. Flurin,C. Urbina,H. Pothier,M. F. Goffman,F. J. Matute-Cañadas,A. Levy Yeyati*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型超导量子电路FerBo，该电路在宽参数范围内对弛豫（relaxation）和退相干（dephasing）均具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发一种在实验可及参数范围内对弛豫和退相干均具有鲁棒性的超导量子电路，以提升量子比特的相干性能。

Method: 电路采用并联结构，包含大电感、小电容和高透射约瑟夫森弱连接（Josephson weak link）。通过弱连接中安德烈夫能级（Andreev levels）的费米子自由度与LC电路电磁模式的玻色子自由度之间的杂化（hybridization）实现弛豫保护。

Result: 该FerBo电路通过杂化机制提供弛豫保护，同时类似fluxonium量子比特，通过波函数在相空间（phase space）的离域化（delocalization）提供退相干鲁棒性。

Conclusion: FerBo电路设计在宽参数范围内同时实现了对弛豫和退相干的鲁棒性，为构建更稳定的超导量子比特提供了新方案。

Abstract: We propose a novel superconducting quantum circuit that should be robust against both relaxation and dephasing over a wide and experimentally accessible parameter range. The circuit consists of a parallel arrangement of a large inductance, a small capacitor, and a well-transmitting Josephson weak link. Protection against relaxation arises from the hybridization between the fermionic degree of freedom associated with Andreev levels in the weak link and the bosonic electromagnetic mode of the LC circuit, hence its name: FerBo. Furthermore, as in the fluxonium qubit, delocalization of the wavefunctions in phase space provides resilience against dephasing.

### [162] [Retained-spin micropolar hydrodynamics from the Boltzmann--Curtiss equation: a generalized Chapman--Enskog construction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00145)
*Satori Tsuzuki*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文从Boltzmann-Curtiss方程出发，通过广义Chapman-Enskog构造推导了保留自旋的微极性流体动力学闭合，其中局部平均自旋被保留为准慢变量。研究明确展示了标准微极性本构结构的出现，并对完美粗糙弹性硬球体系提供了旋转粘度和横向自旋扩散系数的稀薄气体估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于从Boltzmann-Curtiss方程出发，通过广义Chapman-Enskog构造推导保留自旋的微极性流体动力学（micropolar hydrodynamics）闭合。该方法将局部平均自旋保留为准慢变量，旨在明确展示标准微极性本构结构的出现机制。

Method: 采用广义Chapman-Enskog构造，从Boltzmann-Curtiss方程出发推导闭合。方法包括：从精确的动力学平衡定律出发，分离反对称应力与应力诱导自旋转矩的簿记关系，将一阶源分解为不可约标量、轴量和对称无迹部分。针对完美粗糙弹性硬球体系，通过均匀自旋弛豫和输运-弛豫计算获得系数估计，并使用事件驱动分子动力学模拟进行后验检验。

Result: 研究明确展示了标准微极性本构结构如何出现，系数为$(η,ξ,η_r,α,β,γ)$。分解表明单粒子动力学应力仅贡献于对称应力，而旋转粘度（rotational viscosity）$η_r$属于内在/碰撞转移通道。对于完美粗糙弹性硬球，获得了旋转粘度$η_r$的稀薄气体估计（来自均匀自旋弛豫）和横向自旋扩散组合$β+γ$的估计（来自输运-弛豫计算）。分子动力学模拟支持$η_r$的$n^2$和$K/(K+1)$趋势预测。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了一个自包含的保留自旋微极性流体动力学推导和系数水平估计，明确了闭合的哪些部分是精确的，哪些是一阶广义Chapman-Enskog结果，以及哪些仍是受控的粗糙球估计。这澄清了微极性流体动力学闭合的理论基础。

Abstract: We derive a retained-spin micropolar hydrodynamic closure from the Boltzmann--Curtiss equation using a generalized Chapman--Enskog construction in which the local mean spin is retained as a quasi-slow variable. Starting from the exact kinetic balance laws for mass, linear momentum, and intrinsic angular momentum, we isolate the bookkeeping relation between antisymmetric stress and stress-induced spin torque, decompose the first-order source into irreducible scalar, axial, and symmetric-traceless sectors, and show explicitly how the standard micropolar constitutive structure with coefficients $(η,ξ,η_r,α,β,γ)$ emerges. This decomposition makes clear that the one-particle kinetic stress contributes only to the symmetric stress, whereas the rotational viscosity belongs to an intrinsic/collisional transfer channel. For perfectly rough elastic hard spheres, we further obtain explicit dilute-gas estimates for the rotational viscosity $η_r$ from homogeneous spin relaxation and for the transverse spin-diffusion combination $β+γ$ from a transport-relaxation calculation. Targeted event-driven molecular-dynamics simulations are used as a posteriori checks: expanded homogeneous-spin density and roughness sweeps support the predicted $n^2$ and $K/(K+1)$ trends for $η_r$, while finite-$k$ transverse runs provide a qualitative diagnostic of the retained-spin response. The result is a self-contained derivation and coefficient-level estimate of retained-spin micropolar hydrodynamics that clarifies which parts of the closure are exact, which are first-order generalized Chapman--Enskog results, and which remain controlled rough-sphere estimates.

</details>


### [163] [Microscopic Basis for Recovery Rheology and the Nonequilibrium Structure,Yielding, and Flow of Dense Particle Suspensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00147)
*Anoop Mutneja,Kenneth S. Schweizer*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究基于恢复流变学（recovery rheology）框架，建立了非平衡微观流变学理论，将恢复流变学与微观结构、弛豫和弹性联系起来，并应用于胶体悬浮液体系，揭示了宏观与微观性质之间的定量关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 恢复流变学的引入为软物质体系在非平衡条件下的屈服和流动行为提供了新的物理见解，特别是通过将应变分解为可恢复和不可恢复分量。研究发现不可恢复应变的逐渐增加会导致从固体到液体的连续屈服转变，这需要建立更系统的理论框架。

Method: 基于非平衡微观流变学框架，构建了弹性集体非线性朗之万方程（Elastically Collective Nonlinear Langevin Equation）理论，建立了阶跃速率启动剪切响应的统计力学基础，将恢复流变学与微观结构、弛豫和弹性联系起来。

Result: 应用于亚稳态硬球和软球胶体悬浮液，获得了可验证的新预测：稳态可恢复应变与稳态剪切稀化直接相关；瞬态应力过冲振幅随堆积分数非单调变化并与稳态可恢复应变成定量关系；获得的不可恢复应变决定应力过冲应变；变形下结构弛豫时间的巨大减少与不可恢复应变率成反比。

Conclusion: 该研究为恢复流变学建立了系统的统计力学基础，揭示了宏观流变响应与微观结构、弛豫动力学之间的定量联系，为理解软物质体系的屈服和流动行为提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: The recent introduction of recovery rheology has provided qualitatively new physical insights into the yielding and flow of soft matter systems across diverse mechanically driven nonequilibrium protocols by separating the deformation strain into recoverable and unrecoverable components. A striking finding is that the fluid-like response associated with the gradually increasing unrecoverable strain ultimately leads to the continuous yielding transition from a solid to a liquid. We build on the force and particle level Elastically Collective Nonlinear Langevin Equation theory of activated dynamics within a nonequilibrium microrheological framework to formulate a general statistical mechanical foundation of step-rate start-up shear response that relates recovery rheology to microscopic structure, relaxation, and elasticity. Quantitative applications to metastable hard and soft sphere colloidal suspensions reveal testable new predictions and interconnections between macroscopic and microscopic properties: (i) the steady state recoverable strain is directly related to the steady-state shear thinning; (ii) the transient stress overshoot amplitude varies non-monotonically with packing fraction and is quantitatively linked to the steady-state recoverable strain; (iii) the acquired unrecoverable strain dictates the stress overshoot strain; (iv) the predicted enormous reduction of the structural relaxation time under deformation is inversely related to the unrecoverable strain-rate.

</details>


### [164] [Braiding and exchange statistics of liquid crystalline Majorana quasiparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00492)
*A. I. Tóth,G. Negro,A. D. Huxley,D. Marenduzzo*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了向列相液晶中缺陷（defects）的几何旋量（geometric spinors）性质，发现这些缺陷在参数空间大范围内表现出非阿贝尔任意子（non-Abelian anyons）的经典类似物行为，可通过缺陷双矢量（defect bivectors）在类布洛赫半球（Bloch-like hemisphere）上的运动描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维液晶缺陷可视为几何旋量，其涌现性质类似于量子凝聚态中的拓扑激发（如马约拉纳准粒子）。然而，这种类比是否深入、是否仅为数学映射，或是否延伸至交换统计（exchange statistics）或编织行为（braiding behaviour）等关键物理特征，尚不明确。

Method: 研究考虑了一个由四个向列相马约拉纳类缺陷轮廓（nematic Majorana-like defect profiles）组成的简单图案，通过反复编织这些缺陷轮廓来观察其变化。分析基于缺陷双矢量在类布洛赫半球上的运动描述。

Result: 在参数空间大范围内，缺陷轮廓表现出非阿贝尔任意子的经典类似物行为。弹性相互作用（elastic interactions）和动力学效应（dynamical effects）增强了通过编织这些准粒子可执行的门操作的复杂性。

Conclusion: 液晶旋量作为拓扑计算机（topological computers）组件的潜力显著，其缺陷的编织行为展现出类似非阿贝尔任意子的物理特征，超越了纯粹的数学映射。

Abstract: Liquid crystalline defects in 3D can be viewed as geometric spinors, whose emergent properties are reminiscent of those of topological excitations in quantum condensed matter, such as Majorana quasiparticles. However, it is unclear how deep this analogy is, and whether this is a purely mathematical mapping, or it extends to key physical features, such as the exchange statistics or braiding behaviour. To address this question, here we consider a simple pattern made up of four nematic Majorana-like defect profiles, and ask how the defect profiles change as we braid them repeatedly around each other. Surprisingly, we find that in a large range of parameter space the defect profiles behave as classical analogues of non-Abelian anyons, which can be described in our case by defect bivectors moving on a Bloch-like hemisphere. Elastic interactions and dynamical effects enhance the complexity of the gates which can be performed by braiding these quasiparticles, making these liquid crystalline spinors promising candidates as components of topological computers.

</details>


### [165] [Organic Electrochemical Transistor Arrays with Integrated Lipid-Sealed Femtolitre Chambers for Simultaneous Electrical and Optical Detection of Membrane Protein Activity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00501)

Method: 研究人员在玻璃盖玻片上制备了52个离子敏感PEDOT:PSS有机电化学晶体管阵列，每个晶体管底部集成氟聚合物微孔，采用水-有机-水液体交换技术用脂质双层密封微孔。以α-溶血素（α-hemolysin）为模型膜蛋白，嵌入脂质双层形成七聚体孔道。

Result: 实验显示，α-溶血素孔道允许K⁺离子扩散进入微孔，同时Alexa-488染料分子扩散出微孔，分别导致晶体管电导下降和微孔荧光强度降低。两种信号出现在不同时间尺度，与K⁺离子和Alexa-488分子尺寸差异一致。

Abstract: We report a method for producing an array of fifty two ion-sensitive PEDOT:PSS organic electrochemical transistors on a glass coverslip, each featuring an integrated fluoropolymer microwell sealed with lipid bilayer into which membrane proteins can be inserted for simultaneous electrical and fluorescence microscopy studies. To demonstrate capability, we fill the microwells with an `inner' phosphate assay buffer solution containing 20 $μ$M Alexa-488 dye and 50 mM KCl, seal the microwells with lipid bilayer using an aqueous-organic-aqueous liquid exchange technique, and then fill the common flow-cell volume above the sealed microwells with a dye-free `outer' phosphate assay buffer containing 100 mM KCl. We insert $α$-hemolysin, which embeds into the lipid bilayer forming a heptameric pore with diameter ~ 2.6 nm. The pore allows K$^{+}$ ions to diffuse into the microwell and Alexa-488 dye molecules to diffuse out of the microwell producing a corresponding drop in transistor conductance and microwell fluorescence intensity, respectively. These two signals occur at different timescales, consistent with the known size difference between K$^{+}$ ions and Alexa-488 molecules. Our approach to fabricating microwell arrays with PEDOT:PSS OECTs incorporated into the bottom of selected microwells distributed in the array is both scalable and versatile, opening a path to studies using larger arrays and with other membrane proteins embedded in the lipid bilayer sealing the microwells.

### [166] [Unambiguous characterization of in-plane dielectric response in nanoconfined liquids: water as a case study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00700)
*Jon Zubeltzu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出使用二维平面极化率（in-plane 2D polarizability）作为纳米受限水平面介电响应的明确表征，解决了传统介电常数在纳米尺度定义模糊的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米受限水的平面介电常数近年来受到广泛关注，但由于其依赖于水层厚度的任意选择，在纳米尺度上缺乏明确定义。因此需要一种无歧义的表征方法来量化二维约束下的平面介电响应。

Method: 采用经典分子动力学模拟（classical molecular dynamics simulations），通过两种独立且一致的方法计算二维平面极化率：基于涨落-耗散理论（fluctuation-dissipation theory），以及通过将水置于电容器中测量诱导偶极矩的方法。

Result: 研究结果为量化极性液体在模拟和实验中的平面介电响应提供了理论框架，建立了二维平面极化率作为明确表征参数的方法。

Conclusion: 二维平面极化率可作为纳米受限水平面介电响应的无歧义表征，解决了传统介电常数在纳米尺度定义模糊的问题，为跨模拟和实验的量化比较提供了统一框架。

Abstract: The in-plane dielectric constant of nanoconfined water has attracted growing interest over the last years. Nevertheless, this magnitude is not well-defined at the nanoscale due to its dependence on the arbitrary choice of water width. We propose the in-plane 2D polarizability, $α_{\parallel}$, as an unambiguous characterization of the in-plane dielectric response under 2D confinement, in analogy to what has been recently done for the perpendicular response. Using classical molecular dynamics simulations, we compute $α_{\parallel}$ via two independent and consistent methods: based on fluctuation--dissipation theory, and from the induced dipole moment when water is placed in a capacitor. Our results provide the framework to quantify the in-plane dielectric response of polar liquids across simulations and experiments.

</details>


### [167] [Slip-link simulations of long-fiber networks under uniaxial compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00749)
*Yuichi Masubuchi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究将原本用于缠结聚合物液体的粗粒度分子模拟方法扩展至长纤维网络力学行为建模，基于滑环（slip-link）概念描述纤维缠结，通过接触点力平衡和纤维滑移模拟纤维网络的压缩行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于滑环（slip-link）缠结图像，扩展了原本用于缠结聚合物液体的粗粒度分子模拟方法。模型解析接触点的力平衡，考虑拓扑约束下的纤维滑移，通过两个关键控制方程描述接触点位置的时间演化和相邻接触点间局部纤维分数变化。

Result: 对不同纤维长度和压缩速率下的网络进行单轴压缩模拟，模拟结果与长纤维热塑性塑料的实验观察定性一致。模型能够捕捉经典van Wyk理论无法描述的物理机制，包括纤维长度和压缩速率的影响。

Conclusion: 已在聚合物熔体中验证的滑环框架为理解和预测非热纤维网络的加工行为提供了一个有前景的介观尺度模拟工具，能够描述经典理论无法捕捉的物理现象。

Abstract: A coarse-grained molecular simulation approach originally developed for entangled polymeric liquids is extended to model the mechanical behavior of long-fiber networks. The model, based on the slip-link picture of chain entanglements, resolves the force balance at contact points and accounts for fiber slippage under these topological constraints. Two key governing equations describe the time evolution of contact-point positions and the local fiber fraction between adjacent contact points. A yield-force criterion determines whether contact points are displaced or remain pinned, as well as whether fiber slippage occurs at contact points. Uniaxial compression simulations corresponding to press molding of fiber-reinforced thermoplastics were performed for networks with varying fiber lengths and compression rates. The results were qualitatively consistent with experimental observations of long-fiber thermoplastics. The model captures physics inaccessible to the classical van Wyk theory of fiber network compression, which is quasi-static and insensitive to fiber length. This work demonstrates that the slip-link framework, already validated for polymer melts, provides a promising mesoscale simulation tool for understanding and predicting the processing behavior of non-thermal fiber networks.

### [168] [Glassy Arrest Behind the Apparent Second Liquid in Water](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00794)
*Florian Pabst,Ali Hassanali*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过机器学习加速的第一性原理模拟结合实验测量，揭示了水异常行为的起源：先前被解释为液-液相变（LLT）的特征实际上源于动力学阻滞（dynamical arrest）的开始，表现为高密度液体向动力学阻滞的低密度玻璃的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水异常行为的起源是物理科学中的核心开放问题，通常被归因于过冷区域高密度与低密度液态之间的液-液相变（liquid-liquid transition, LLT）。实验研究因快速结晶而受限，使得原子尺度模拟成为主要证据来源。

Method: 采用广泛的机器学习加速第一性原理模拟（machine-learning-accelerated first-principles simulations），并与光谱学、结构和动力学实验测量进行直接比较，以研究水的异常行为。

Result: 研究发现，通常被解释为双液行为的特征出现在动力学阻滞（dynamical arrest）开始时。先前与LLT相关的双态波动（two-state fluctuations）反映了从高密度液体向动力学阻滞的低密度玻璃（kinetically arrested low-density glass）的转变。

Conclusion: 通过映射压力与温度下的平衡动力学，结果表明需要重新评估水的亚稳态图景：明显的双态行为可能反映了常压下低密度水相对较高的玻璃化转变温度（glass-transition temperature）——189±8 K，该温度与先前与LLT相关的温度非常接近。

Abstract: The origin of water's anomalous behavior remains a central open problem in the physical sciences and is often attributed to a liquid-liquid transition (LLT) between high- and low-density liquid states deep in the supercooled regime. Experimental access to this region has been challenging due to rapid crystallization, leaving atomistic simulations as a major source of supporting evidence. Using extensive machine-learning-accelerated first-principles simulations in direct comparison with spectroscopic, structural, and dynamical experimental measurements, we show that features commonly interpreted as signatures of two-liquid behavior emerge at the onset of dynamical arrest. Specifically, we find that two-state fluctuations previously associated with an LLT reflect a transformation from a high-density liquid to a kinetically arrested low-density glass. By mapping equilibrium dynamics across pressure and temperature, our results suggest a reassessment of water's metastable landscape, in which apparent two-state behavior may reflect a relatively high glass-transition temperature of ambient-pressure low-density water, 189$\pm$8 K -- remarkably close to the temperature previously associated with the LLT.

### [169] [Phase separation by polar active transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01057)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究受到近期实验启发，实验中沿微管（microtubules）反向行走的分子马达（molecular motors）被分选到不同区域。这揭示了一种新的主动相分离机制，可为细胞内生物材料的空间组织提供理论模型。

Method: 研究提出了主动Cahn-Hilliard理论（active Cahn-Hilliard theory），其中第三种极性物种能够沿其极性方向反向运输另外两种组分，从而实现它们的分离。

Result: 理论预测了马达结构域（motor domains）的形成，并显示它们可能粗化（coarsen）形成宏观相，或通过活性作用抑制粗化过程，达到有限微/介观稳态尺寸。

Conclusion: 该理论描述了一种新的主动相分离机制，可作为细胞内生物材料空间组织的模型，揭示了活性如何调控相分离的最终尺度。

Abstract: We propose an active Cahn-Hilliard theory for the dynamics of a new type of phase transition where the driving force is not the direct interactions between the two separating components, but their active sorting by a third polar species. This third species can transport the other two along its polarity in opposite directions, thus separating them. Inspired by recent experiments where molecular motors that walk in opposite directions along microtubules are sorted into separated domains, our theoretical description of this process introduces a new mechanism for active phase separation and could serve as a model for the organization of biological material in space inside cells. We predict the formation of motor domains, and further show that they can either coarsen to form macroscopic phases or reach a finite micro- or mesoscopic steady state size, these latter due to an arrest of coarsening through activity.

### [170] [High-symmetry ill-fitting subunits in 3D form aggregates of all dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01109)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过理论模型研究三维空间中相同、不匹配的可变形亚基（模拟溶液中的球状蛋白质）的自组装。模型将亚基力学映射到两个不相容、互连网络的力学上，分析预测了聚集体基态形态与亚基粘附性（adhesivity）和弹性（elasticity）的函数关系。

Result: 研究发现，根据组装参数不同，可形成零维簇、三维块体以及对称性破缺的一维丝状体和二维层状结构。不可压缩、中等粘附性的亚基倾向于形成丝状体。

Conclusion: 这些发现提示了控制三维自组装的通用途径，并表明此类机制可在更现实的蛋白质模型中进行研究，为理解蛋白质聚集的形态多样性提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Proteins can combine into functional elements in living cells or self-assemble into unwanted structures in a number of diseases. The resulting aggregates often display filamentous morphologies across a large range of protein shapes and molecular interactions. This has led to the suggestion that filament formation could be a generic outcome of the aggregation of geometrically complex, ill-fitting objects, although such a mechanism has not been demonstrated in three dimensions. To address this problem, we theoretically study the self-assembly of three-dimensional identical, ill-fitting deformable subunits mimicking globular proteins in solution. In our model, self-assembling subunits incur deformations that accumulate as the aggregate size increases and can eventually hamper further assembly. We analytically predict the ground state morphologies of the resulting aggregates as a function of the subunit adhesivity and elasticity by mapping their mechanics onto those of two incompatible, interconnected networks. We find that zero-dimensional clusters, three-dimensional bulks as well as symmetry-broken one-dimensional filaments and two-dimensional layers can all form depending on assembly parameters. Incompressible, moderately adhesive subunits favor filaments. These findings hint at a generic pathway to control self-assembly in three dimensions and suggests that such mechanisms could be investigated in more realistic protein models.

### [171] [Polyelectrolyte adsorption at the solid-liquid interface favors receding contact line instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01185)
*Léa Delance,Diego Díaz,Arivazhagan G. Balasubramanian,Outi Tammisola,Kaloian Koynov,Hans-Jürgen Butt*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究开发了高速高分辨率反射显微镜，首次在滑动液滴中观察到黏弹性（viscoelasticity）导致的后退接触线（receding contact line）失稳和细丝形成现象，揭示了聚合物电荷对润湿特性的关键影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了高速高分辨率反射显微镜，可直接可视化滑动液滴的接触线。使用基于聚丙烯酰胺的水溶性聚电解质溶液，让液滴在Teflon AF-和PDMS-涂层玻璃片组成的疏水基底上滑动，基底倾斜角度在20°至45°之间变化。

Result: 实验表明黏弹性会破坏后退接触线的稳定性，引发细丝形成。这种之前在薄黏弹性膜涂层中观察到的失稳现象，首次在滑动液滴中被报道。聚合物电荷起关键作用：阳离子和非离子聚合物促进细丝形成，而阴离子聚合物则不会。

Conclusion: 阐明了流变学（rheology）、表面相互作用和液滴动力学之间的相互作用，将细丝形成的差异归因于溶液的不同润湿特性。

Abstract: Controlling the motion of non-Newtonian drops on surfaces is crucial for applications ranging from inkjet printing to biomedical devices and food processing. While the macroscopic behavior of viscoelastic drops sliding on tilted hydrophobic surfaces has been characterized, showing reduced velocities and elongation compared to Newtonian fluids, the underlying microscopic mechanisms remain poorly understood. To address this gap, we developed a high-speed, high-resolution reflection microscope that enables direct visualization of the contact line of sliding drops. We used water/soluble polyelectrolyte solutions based on polyacrylamide and let drops sliding on hydrophobic substrates composed of Teflon AF- and PDMS-coated glass slides. The substrate tilting angle was varied between 20° and 45°. We reveal how viscoelasticity influences the dynamics of the receding contact line and drop motion. Our experiments demonstrate that viscoelasticity can destabilize the receding contact line, triggering filament formation. This instability previously observed in the coating of thin viscoelastic films, is reported here for the first time in sliding drops. We further highlight the critical role of polymer charge in this process: while cationic and non-ionic polymers promote filament formation, anionic polymers do not, a difference we attribute to the distinct wetting properties of the solutions. In conclusion, we clarify the interplay between rheology, surface interactions, and drop dynamics.

### [172] [Arches of chaos, heteroclinic connections of first-order MMRs and the chaotic transport of small bodies in the Sun-Jupiter system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00679)
*Alessia Francesca Guido,Christos Efthymiopoulos*

Main category: astro-ph.EP

TL;DR: 该研究在日-木平面限制性三体问题中，计算了主要平均运动共振（MMRs）不稳定周期轨道的稳定与不稳定流形，发现了多种异宿连接通道，解释了小行星轨道平面中的"混沌拱门"结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索日-木平面限制性三体问题中，与主要平均运动共振（mean motion resonances, MMRs）相关的不稳定周期轨道的稳定与不稳定流形之间的异宿连接（heteroclinic connections）。特别关注粒子在木星轨道内外穿越的动力学机制。

Method: 采用平面限制性三体问题（planar restricted three-body problem）模型，显式计算了内共振2:1、3:2和外共振2:3的一阶共振不稳定周期轨道的稳定与不稳定流形。同时计算了短期快速李雅普诺夫指数（fast Lyapunov indicator, FLI）图来展示混沌鞍结构。

Result: 发现了多种异宿连接通道，包括Koon等人的经典连接之外的新连接：L3附近短周期轨道流形与内外一阶共振周期轨道流形之间的连接，以及不涉及共轨周期轨道的内外共振流形直接连接。这些流形和对应的FLI脊解释了小行星轨道平面(a,e)中的"混沌拱门"现象。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了在Tisserand参数小于3时，粒子可通过多种异宿通道在木星轨道内外穿越。追踪异宿轨迹的混沌轨道表现出共振跳跃（resonance hopping），暗示与准希尔达族小行星和木星族彗星的联系。这些结果在圆形限制性三体问题中获得，但在椭圆问题中依然成立。

Abstract: We investigate the heteroclinic connections between stable and unstable manifolds of unstable periodic orbits associated with the most important mean motion resonances (MMRs) in the Sun-Jupiter planar restricted three-body problem. We explicitly compute the stable and unstable manifolds of the unstable periodic orbits associated with the first order interior MMRs 2:1, 3:2, and the exterior MMR 2:3. We also compute short-time FLI maps showing the chaotic saddle structure created by the manifolds of several interior or exterior MMRs other than the 1:1 (co-orbital) resonance. Transits of particles from the exterior to the interior of Jupiter's orbit and vice versa are allowed for Tisserand parameter lesser than 3, and are shown to exist through a variety of heteroclinic channels. Besides the classical ones by Koon et al., we find heteroclinic connections between manifolds of short-period orbits around L3 and periodic orbits of interior or exterior first order MMRs, as well as direct connections between interior and exterior MMR manifolds not involving co-orbital periodic orbits. Through these manifolds and the corresponding FLI ridges, we explain the 'arches-of-chaos' in the asteroid orbital plane (a,e). Chaotic orbits shadowing heteroclinic trajectories exhibit resonance hopping, suggesting links to quasi-Hildas and Jupiter-family comets. Results are obtained in the circular RTBP but persist in the elliptic problem.

### [173] [Lindblad-Deformed Spectral Geometry: Heat-Kernel Asymptotics and Effective Spectral Dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00033)
*Soumadeep Maiti*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种Lindblad变形谱几何框架，通过有界耗散数据将标准谱三元组变形为Dirac算子D_gamma = D - igammaSigma，其中Sigma由Lindblad跳跃算子构造。该框架将正算子Q_gamma = D_gamma^* D_gamma识别为正确的谱几何可观测量，并分析了其热核渐近展开和热迹修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在将耗散动力学纳入谱几何框架，通过引入Lindblad变形将标准谱三元组扩展为包含耗散效应的几何结构。这种扩展允许在几何背景下研究量子开放系统的谱特性，为理解耗散对几何结构的影响提供数学框架。

Method: 方法基于Lindblad变形谱几何框架，通过构造变形Dirac算子D_gamma = D - igammaSigma，其中Sigma = (1/2) sum_k L_k^dagger L_k由Lindblad跳跃算子{L_k}构建。研究正算子Q_gamma = D_gamma^* D_gamma的热核渐近展开，分析标量变形L = sqrt(gamma) f情况下的热迹修正，并在S^2球面模型中进行具体计算。

Result: 对于光滑自同态值Lindblad数据，Q_gamma属于Laplace类型并允许标准热核渐近展开，具有耗散修正的偶Seeley-DeWitt系数。标量变形情况下，热迹K_gamma(sigma)的Duhamel一阶修正恒为零，首次非平凡耗散效应出现在gamma^4阶。在S^2球面模型中确定了显式变形算子并提取了W_2扇区的主导局部渐近贡献，定义了有效尺度依赖谱维度d_{s,eff}(sigma,gamma)。

Conclusion: 本文成功建立了Lindblad变形谱几何框架，证明了耗散效应在谱几何中的可观测性。标量变形情况下耗散效应延迟到gamma^4阶出现，为理解耗散对几何谱特性的影响提供了系统分析工具，特别是在S^2模型中的具体结果为该框架的应用提供了实例验证。

Abstract: We introduce a Lindblad-deformed spectral geometric framework in which bounded dissipative data deform a standard spectral triple through the Dirac operator D_gamma = D - igammaSigma, where Sigma = (1/2) sum_k L_k^dagger L_k is constructed from Lindblad jump operators {L_k}. The associated positive operator Q_gamma = D_gamma^* D_gamma = D^2 + gamma^2 Sigma^2 - i*gamma [D, Sigma] is identified as the correct spectral-geometric observable. For smooth endomorphism-valued Lindblad data, Q_gamma is of Laplace type and admits a standard heat-kernel asymptotic expansion with dissipation-modified even Seeley-DeWitt coefficients. For the scalar deformation L = sqrt(gamma) f with f in C^infty(M) real-valued, we prove that the first-order Duhamel correction to the heat trace K_gamma(sigma) = Tr(exp(-sigma Q_gamma)) vanishes identically, so that the first nontrivial dissipative effect appears at order gamma^4. We identify the exact Duhamel-level decomposition of the O(gamma^4) correction into a direct W_2 insertion and a quadratic W_1 x W_1 term. In the round S^2 model we determine the explicit deformed operator and extract the leading local asymptotic contribution of the W_2 sector. We define the effective scale-dependent spectral dimension d_{s,eff}(sigma,gamma) = -2 d/d(log sigma) log K_gamma(sigma) and identify its leading perturbative deformation.

</details>


### [174] [Zeno-Constrained Formation of Relativistic Mass Shells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00051)
*Ansgar Pernice*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过强连续监测下的量子线性玻尔兹曼方程扩展，在量子芝诺（Zeno）区域中推导出有效红外固定点，该固定点具有洛伦兹（Lorentz）签名，并产生类似质量壳的约束表面，从而在扩展量子玻尔兹曼框架内涌现出相对论性特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索开放量子系统在强连续监测下的不可逆动量空间动力学，特别关注在扩展的四维欧几里得动量空间中，如何从微观无固定签名的观测中涌现出有效的相对论结构。

Method: 采用扩展的量子线性玻尔兹曼方程（quantum linear Boltzmann equation），在量子芝诺（Zeno）区域中通过绝热消除快速自由度，利用舒尔补（Schur-complement）构造推导二阶修正，并在温和各向同性假设和适当校准条件下分析有效流。

Result: 研究发现有效流在红外区域趋近于一个固定点，该固定点由具有洛伦兹（Lorentz）签名的二次型表征，其零集定义了类似质量壳的约束表面，其等距群在有效层面匹配洛伦兹变换的动力学结构。

Conclusion: 在扩展量子玻尔兹曼框架内，通过量子芝诺（Zeno）投影动力学，可以从无固定签名的微观观测中涌现出相对论性特征，包括麦克斯韦-尤特纳（Maxwell-Juettner）型稳态分布，这些特征是该固定点在有效红外描述层面的结果。

Abstract: We study an extension of the quantum linear Boltzmann equation describing irreversible momentum-space dynamics of an open quantum system under strong continuous monitoring. The monitored observable is taken to be a quadratic form in an extended, purely Euclidean four-dimensional momentum space, without assuming any fixed signature at the microscopic level. In the resulting quantum Zeno regime, rapid suppression of off-constraint excursions allows for an adiabatic elimination of fast degrees of freedom. Using a Schur-complement construction, the induced second-order corrections give rise to an effective flow of the monitored quadratic form under temporal coarse graining. Under mild isotropy assumptions on the underlying momentum-mixing dynamics and an appropriate calibration condition, this flow approaches an infrared fixed point characterized by a quadratic form of Lorentzian signature. The corresponding null set defines a mass-shell-like constraint surface that governs the long-time Zeno-projected dynamics and whose isometry group matches the kinematic structure of Lorentz transformations at the effective level. Familiar relativistic features, including Maxwell-Juettner-type stationary distributions, arise at the level of the effective infrared description as consequences of this fixed point within the extended quantum Boltzmann framework.

</details>


### [175] [The time of arrival problem in the Page-Wootters formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00092)
*Niyusha Hosseini,Maximilian P. E. Lock*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过反转Page-Wootters框架，构建了量子粒子到达特定位置的时间分布，为时间到达问题提供了关系性描述，并揭示了该框架在条件概率解释中的复杂性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间到达问题（time-of-arrival problem）探讨量子粒子到达指定位置的概率分布，该问题凸显了量子理论中缺乏自伴时间可观测量的困境，并成为数十年争论的焦点。

Method: 研究采用反转Page-Wootters框架的方法，将时间视为关系量，通过询问"当粒子到达固定位置时时钟显示什么时间"来构建时间到达分布。

Result: 该方法得到的时间分布与时间到达问题的常见处理方法一致，表明后者可能具有关系性解释，同时揭示了Page-Wootters形式在条件概率解释中的复杂性。

Conclusion: 该研究不仅为时间到达问题提供了关系性描述，还将Page-Wootters形式应用于具体物理问题，深化了对量子时间概念的理解。

Abstract: The time-of-arrival problem asks for the probability distribution for when a quantum particle reaches a specified location. It has been the subject of decades of debate, exemplifying the lack of a self-adjoint time observable in quantum theory. In the Page-Wootters framework, time is a relational quantity, emerging from correlations between a system and a clock induced by a global Hamiltonian constraint. We construct a time-of-arrival distribution by inverting the Page-Wootters approach, asking what time a clock reads given that the particle arrives at some fixed position. The result coincides with a common approach to the time-of-arrival problem, suggesting a potential relational interpretation of the latter. In addition to providing a relational description of the time-of-arrival problem, this gives an application of the Page-Wootters formalism to a concrete physical problem, and reveals some complications with its canonical interpretation as a theory of conditional probabilities.

### [176] [Quantum walk on a random comb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00908)
*François David,Thordur Jonsson*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究随机梳状图上量子行走的动力学行为，特别关注无限齿结构对行走传播特性的影响，旨在理解此类系统中局域化现象与逃逸行为的相互作用。

Method: 通过分析图随机哈密顿量（random Hamiltonian）的谱和本征态特性，结合解析与数值方法，其中许多方法源自一维安德森局域化（Anderson localization）理论。

Result: 由于脊柱方向的局域化效应，量子行走无法沿脊柱方向传播至无穷远，但可沿梳齿方向逃逸至无穷远；从初始顶点出发，行走存在非零概率被困在有限区域内。

Conclusion: 随机梳状图上的连续时间量子行走表现出各向异性传播特性：脊柱方向因局域化而受限，梳齿方向则允许逃逸至无穷远，揭示了此类结构中局域化与逃逸行为的共存现象。

Abstract: We study continuous time quantum walk on a random comb graph with infinite teeth. Due to localization effects along the spine, the walk cannot go to infinity in the spine direction, while it can escape to infinity along the teeth of the comb. Starting from an initial vertex the walk has a nonzero probability to stay trapped in a finite region. These results are obtained by studying the spectrum and eigenstates of the random Hamiltonian for the graph and analysing its properties. We use both analytic and numerical methods many of which come from the theory of Anderson localization in one dimension.

### [177] [Quantum Gibbs Sampling in Infinite Dimensions: Generation, Mixing Times and Circuit Implementation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01192)
*Simon Becker,Cambyse Rouzé,Robert Salzmann*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个严格且可实现的无限维量子系统吉布斯采样框架，解决了无界哈密顿量带来的生成器定义、谱间隙缺失等基本障碍，建立了可实现性与收敛性之间的权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将耗散吉布斯采样器扩展到有限维之外面临基本障碍，包括生成器定义不明确、自然巴拿赫空间上谱间隙的缺失，以及可实现性与收敛保证之间的张力。这些挑战阻碍了无限维量子系统的有效吉布斯采样。

Method: 基于狄利克雷形式（Dirichlet forms）的抽象框架，在可分希尔伯特空间上构造KMS对称量子马尔可夫半群。该方法适用于可分希尔伯特空间上的有界算子代数，并利用自伴生成器的谱特性建立定量收敛结果。

Result: 建立了在迹距离下的定量收敛结果，包括快速热化（fast thermalization）机制。同时发现，对于某些哈密顿量，保证可实现性的生成器选择通常以失去相关演化的收敛性为代价，从而确立了可实现性与收敛性之间的强权衡关系。

Conclusion: 该框架适用于广泛模型，包括薛定谔算子（Schrödinger operators）、高斯系统（Gaussian systems）和玻色-哈伯德哈密顿量（Bose-Hubbard Hamiltonians），为连接严格无限维分析与算法吉布斯态制备提供了统一方法。

Abstract: We develop a rigorous and implementable framework for Gibbs sampling of infinite-dimensional quantum systems governed by unbounded Hamiltonians. Extending dissipative Gibbs samplers beyond finite dimensions raises fundamental obstacles, including ill-defined generators, the absence of spectral gaps on natural Banach spaces, and tensions between implementability and convergence guarantees. We overcome these issues by constructing KMS-symmetric quantum Markov semigroups on separable Hilbert spaces that are both well-posed and efficiently implementable on qubit hardware. Our generation theory is based on the abstract framework of Dirichlet forms, adapted here to the case of algebras of bounded operators over separable Hilbert spaces. Leveraging the spectral properties of our self-adjoint generators, we establish quantitative convergence results in trace distance, including regimes of fast thermalization. In contrast, we also identify Hamiltonians for which a naive choice of generators guaranteeing implementability generally comes at the cost of losing convergence of the associated evolutions, thereby establishing a strong trade-off between implementability and convergence. Our framework applies to a wide class of models, including Schrödinger operators, Gaussian systems, and Bose-Hubbard Hamiltonians, and provides a unified approach linking rigorous infinite-dimensional analysis with algorithmic Gibbs state preparation.

### [178] [Conditional channel entropy sets fundamental limits on thermodynamic quantum information processing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01217)
*Himanshu Badhani,Siddhartha Das*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在条件非热性（conditional athermality）资源理论框架下，量化了量子通道的热力学资源性与因果结构及量子关联生成能力之间的相互作用。研究揭示了条件通道熵（conditional channel entropy）与最优单次蒸馏/模拟速率之间的直接权衡关系，并建立了特定通道类的渐近可逆性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子通道的热力学资源性主要取决于其底层因果结构及产生量子关联的能力。本文旨在量化这种相互作用，特别是在存在作为记忆的边信道（side channel）的二分量子通道（bipartite quantum channels）背景下，建立条件非热性（conditional athermality）资源理论。

Method: 在条件非热性资源理论框架下，针对具有平凡输出哈密顿量（trivial output Hamiltonians）的通道，在条件吉布斯保持超通道（conditional Gibbs-preserving superchannels）约束下，表征了从给定通道蒸馏出恒等门（identity gate）的最优单次速率（optimal one-shot rates）以及使用恒等门模拟通道的成本。进一步建立了条件通道最小熵（conditional channel min-entropy）的等分性质（equipartition property）。

Result: 研究揭示了最优单次蒸馏/模拟速率与条件通道熵（conditional channel entropies）之间存在直接权衡关系，为量子过程中的信令（signaling）提供了操作意义。对于满足遥协变（tele-covariant）或从非条件输入到条件输出无信令（no-signaling）的通道类，建立了条件通道最小熵的等分性质，从而证明了这些通道的渐近可逆性（asymptotic reversibility）。遥协变通道的渐近条件非热性容量（asymptotic conditional athermality capacity）是其Choi态超密编码容量（superdense coding capacity）的一半。

Conclusion: 本文确立了条件通道熵作为量子过程的基本信息论概念，阐明了其在量子信息科学中更广泛应用的潜力。研究结果将通道的热力学资源性与信息论性质联系起来，为理解量子过程中的因果结构和关联提供了新视角。

Abstract: The thermodynamic resourcefulness of quantum channels primarily depends on their underlying causal structure and their ability to generate quantum correlations. We quantify this interplay within the resource theory of athermality for bipartite quantum channels in the presence of a side channel acting as memory, referred to as the resource theory of conditional athermality. For channels with trivial output Hamiltonians, we characterize the optimal one-shot rates for distilling the identity gate from a given channel, as well as the cost of simulating the channel using the identity gate, under conditional Gibbs-preserving superchannels. We show that these rates have a direct trade-off relation with the conditional channel entropies, attributing operational significance to signaling in quantum processes. Furthermore, we establish an equipartition property for the conditional channel min-entropy for classes of channels that are either tele-covariant or no-signaling from the non-conditioning input to the conditioning output. As a consequence, we demonstrate asymptotic reversibility of the resource theory for these channels. The asymptotic conditional athermality capacity of a tele-covariant channel is half the superdense coding capacity of its Choi state. Our work establishes the conditional channel entropy as a primitive information-theoretic concept for quantum processes, elucidating its potential for wider applications in quantum information science.

Method: 提出两种解决方案：在虚时间模拟厄米系统，或在实时模拟非厄米系统。为解决两种方法导致的非幺正量子演化问题，开发了结合块编码（block encoding）和哈达玛测试（Hadamard test）的量子算法。

One is to simulate Hermitian systems in imaginary time, the other is to simulate non-Hermitian systems in real time. We demonstrate that both approaches lead to the problem of non-unitary quantum evolution which can be solved by combining two quantum algorithms: block encoding and Hadamard test. The combined quantum algorithm does not require mid-circuit measurements or adjustment of the input parameters of the Hamiltonian, and can be easily implemented on quantum computers. Both the size and length of quantum circuits grow linearly with evolution time. Numerical tests on quantum simulators show that both approaches agree with exact solutions for a sufficiently long time before the signal is lost in statistical fluctuations. The results bode well for using non-Hermitian and imaginary-time simulations to circumvent oscillations inherent in real-time simulation of other quantum systems.

Here, we realize such memories using erbium-doped silicon waveguides, fabricated as part of a multi-wafer project by a nanophotonic foundry. The phase of the read-out light field is preserved with a visibility of $91.3(30)\ \%$. The efficiency of $1.89(28)\times 10^{-8}$ can be improved in future devices through resonator enhancement and higher dopant concentrations. With this, the demonstrated approach will pave the way towards applications in photonic quantum computing based on scalable silicon processing technology.

### [181] [Nonlinearity-Induced Thouless Pumping in Quasiperiodic Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00639)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用准周期晶格中的能隙孤子（gap solitons）作为研究对象，其中局域非线性自洽势（local nonlinear self-consistent potentials）导致晶格势重构。通过分析这种局域重构诱导的拓扑结构来研究孤子动力学。

Conclusion: 通过调控非线性强度或晶格标度，可以在拓扑泵浦、漂移和局域化之间实现可控切换。该工作揭示了复杂晶格势中非线性诱导拓扑行为的新机制。

Abstract: Nonlinear Thouless pumping has been established in periodic lattices; its counterpart in quasiperiodic lattices remains unexplored. Here, we show a nonlinear topological pumping of gap solitons in quasiperiodic lattices where the local nonlinear self-consistent potentials lead to a lattice potential reconstruction; as a result, an emergent topological structure induced by this local reconstruction governs the dynamics of the gap solitons. This enables solitons to adiabatically occupy a single topological band, realizing quasi-quantized Thouless pumping. In addition, the intrinsic lattice perturbations disrupt this band occupation, which drives solitons into a non-quantized drifting regime. However, even in this regime, we also find that the soliton transport is constrained by the topological properties of a critical rational approximant. Tuning nonlinearity or lattice scaling reveals a controllable switching among topological pumping, drifting, and localization. Our work uncovers a mechanism for nonlinearity-induced topological behavior in complex lattice potentials.

### [182] [Multi-Mode Quantum Annealing for Variational Autoencoders with General Boltzmann Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00919)
*Gilhan Kim,Daniel K. Park*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了玻尔兹曼机先验变分自编码器（BM-VAEs），通过量子退火（quantum annealing）在三种操作模式下训练基于能量的先验分布，实现了比高斯先验VAE更快的收敛和更低的重建损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变分自编码器（VAEs）的生成能力受限于潜在空间的先验分布选择。基于能量的先验（energy-based priors）能够超越因子化假设并捕捉潜在变量间的结构化交互，但大规模训练需要从难处理分布中进行准确高效的采样。

Method: 提出了玻尔兹曼机先验变分自编码器（BM-VAEs），在单个生成系统中使用三种量子退火操作模式：训练时使用非绝热量子退火（DQA）提供无偏玻尔兹曼样本进行梯度估计；无条件生成时使用较慢的量子退火（QA）在低能量最小值附近集中采样；条件生成时添加偏置场引导采样到能量景观的特定属性区域（c-QA）。

Result: 在D-Wave Advantage2处理器上使用多达2000个量子比特，在多个数据集上实现了稳定高效的训练，相比高斯先验VAE具有更快的收敛速度和更低的重建损失。学习到的玻尔兹曼先验支持直接从基于能量的潜在分布进行无条件生成，以及通过利用学习到的成对交互进行潜在偏置的条件生成。

Conclusion: BM-VAEs通过量子退火采样有效训练了基于能量的先验，扩展了VAEs的生成能力，实现了普通自编码器所缺乏的直接从能量分布生成的能力，并通过潜在偏置支持条件生成。

Abstract: Variational autoencoders (VAEs) learn compact latent representations of complex data, but their generative capacity is fundamentally constrained by the choice of prior distribution over the latent space. Energy-based priors offer a principled way to move beyond factorized assumptions and capture structured interactions among latent variables, yet training such priors at scale requires accurate and efficient sampling from intractable distributions. Here we present Boltzmann-machine--prior VAEs (BM-VAEs) trained using quantum annealing--based sampling in three distinct operational modes within a single generative system. During training, diabatic quantum annealing (DQA) provides unbiased Boltzmann samples for gradient estimation of the energy-based prior; for unconditional generation, slower quantum annealing (QA) concentrates samples near low-energy minima; for conditional generation, bias fields are added to direct sampling toward attribute-specific regions of the energy landscape (c-QA). Using up to 2000 qubits on a D-Wave Advantage2 processor, we demonstrate stable and efficient training across multiple datasets, with faster convergence and lower reconstruction loss than a Gaussian-prior VAE. The learned Boltzmann prior enables unconditional generation by sampling directly from the energy-based latent distribution, a capability that plain autoencoders lack, and conditional generation through latent biasing that leverages the learned pairwise interactions.

### [183] [Thermal Entanglement and Out-of-Equilibrium Thermodynamics in 1D Bose gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01157)
*Julia Mathé,Nicky Kai Hong Li,Pharnam Bakhshinezhad,Giuseppe Vitagliano*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了一维玻色气体在低能Bogoliubov区域中平衡与非平衡状态下的纠缠现象，基于协方差矩阵框架开发了最优纠缠见证方法，并分析了压缩演化过程中纠缠的产生与演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解一维量子玻色气体中纠缠如何出现和演化，特别是在低能Bogoliubov区域的高斯态设置下，为二次玻色模型中的纠缠分析提供统一的物理直观图像。

Method: 采用基于协方差矩阵的框架和相关纠缠单调量，在热态中确定最优纠缠见证；通过幺正压缩诱导非平衡动力学，研究从初始可分离热态产生纠缠的过程。

Result: 热态的最优纠缠见证具有简单模式解析结构：在正则模基中呈对角化，可表示为仅两个正则模不确定度的乘积。在完全绝热演化中，最优见证保持与热态相同的双模结构；快速压缩时见证结构变得更为复杂。

Conclusion: 该研究方法和结果为理解一维量子玻色气体中纠缠的出现和演化提供了统一且物理直观的图像，并确定了与二次玻色模型中纠缠分析及其在热力学循环中作用相关的最优见证结构。

Abstract: We investigate entanglement in and out of equilibrium in a one-dimensional Bose gas in its low-energy Bogoliubov regime. In this Gaussian setting, the state is fully characterized by its covariance matrix, which allows us to detect and quantify entanglement using a covariance-based framework and associated entanglement monotones. For thermal states, we determine the optimal entanglement witness arising from the covariance matrix criterion and show that it has a remarkably simple mode-resolved structure: it is diagonal in the normal-mode basis and admits a simple analytic form that can be expressed as a product of only two normal-mode uncertainties. We then study out-of-equilibrium dynamics induced by unitary compression and show that entanglement can be generated even from initially separable thermal states. When the evolution is fully adiabatic, the optimal witness retains the same two-mode structure as in the thermal case. Departing from this regime, i.e., performing increasingly rapid compression, the optimal witness becomes genuinely more intricate. Our methods and results provide a unified and physically intuitive picture of how entanglement emerges and evolves in 1D quantum Bose gases, and identify an optimal witness structure relevant more broadly to the analysis of entanglement in quadratic bosonic models and its role in thermodynamic cycles.

</details>


### [184] [Variational Dynamics of Open Quantum Spin Systems in Phase Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01165)
*Jacopo Tosca,Zejian Li,Francesco Carnazza,Cristiano Ciuti*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于自旋相空间表示和变分原理的开放量子自旋系统动力学模拟方法，该方法采用自旋相干态混合表示并允许负系数，能够准确捕获量子关联，在二维晶格上具有高效可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在模拟相互作用开放量子自旋系统的动力学时面临挑战，特别是对于大规模二维晶格系统。需要开发能够准确捕获量子关联且计算高效的新方法。

Method: 该方法基于自旋相空间表示（spin phase-space representation），采用变分方法（variational method）以Husimi-Q函数为目标。核心是使用基于多维自旋相干态混合（multi-dimensional mixture of spin-coherent states）的变分拟设（ansatz），并允许混合系数取负值以超越半经典描述。

Result: 该方法能够准确捕获横场量子伊辛模型（transverse-field quantum Ising model）的完整量子动力学和非平衡稳态，与精确对角化（exact diagonalization）结果高度一致。更重要的是，该方法能够高效扩展到大规模二维晶格系统。

Conclusion: 提出的变分方法为开放量子自旋系统的动力学模拟提供了准确且可扩展的解决方案，特别适用于其他方法难以处理的大规模二维晶格系统，为研究量子多体系统的非平衡行为提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We introduce a variational method for simulating the dynamics of interacting open quantum spin systems. The method is based on the spin phase-space representation and variationally targets the Husimi-$Q$ function with an ansatz based on a multi-dimensional mixture of spin-coherent states. Crucially, the mixture coefficients are allowed to take negative values, enabling the faithful capture of quantum correlations beyond semiclassical descriptions. The resulting equations of motion are derived from the Dirac-Frenkel variational principle and can be evaluated efficiently without resorting to Monte Carlo sampling by exploiting the analytical structure of the ansatz. As a first application, we demonstrate that this approach accurately captures both the full quantum dynamics and the non-equilibrium steady states of the transverse-field quantum Ising model, in excellent agreement with exact diagonalization. Furthermore, we show that the method scales efficiently to large two-dimensional lattices, a regime that remains challenging for other techniques.

</details>


### [185] [Learning and Generating Mixed States Prepared by Shallow Channel Circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01197)
*Fangjun Hu,Christian Kokail,Milan Kornjača,Pedro L. S. Lopes,Weiyuan Gong,Sheng-Tao Wang,Xun Gao,Stefan Ostermann*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究证明了在有限维晶格上，属于平凡相（trivial phase）的任意混合态可以从测量数据中高效学习。算法输出一个浅层局域信道电路来近似生成目标态，样本复杂度和运行时间在量子比特数上是多项式或拟多项式级别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于量子信息与计算复杂性中从测量数据学习量子态的核心问题，特别是受到混合态物质相（mixed state phases of matter）最新进展的推动。该工作专注于平凡相中的任意态，这些态具有浅层制备信道电路且保持局域可逆性。

Method: 方法基于证明平凡相混合态可以从测量访问中高效学习。给定未知平凡相混合态的副本，算法输出一个浅层局域信道电路（shallow local channel circuit），在迹距离（trace distance）下近似生成该态。学习过程不依赖原始制备电路，仅需其存在性假设。

Result: 结果表明，对于平凡相混合态，样本复杂度和运行时间在量子比特数上是多项式或拟多项式级别，前提是电路深度和门局域性（gate locality）为常数或对数多项式。该结果为基于浅层信道电路的量子生成模型提供了结构基础。

Conclusion: 该研究为基于浅层信道电路的量子生成模型建立了结构基础。在经典极限下，该框架还启发了仅需多项式训练和生成开销的经典扩散模型（classical diffusion models）高效算法，展示了量子学习理论对经典机器学习的影响。

Abstract: Learning quantum states from measurement data is a central problem in quantum information and computational complexity. In this work, we study the problem of learning to generate mixed states on a finite-dimensional lattice. Motivated by recent developments in mixed state phases of matter, we focus on arbitrary states in the trivial phase. A state belongs to the trivial phase if there exists a shallow preparation channel circuit under which local reversibility is preserved throughout the preparation. We prove that any mixed state in this class can be efficiently learned from measurement access alone. Specifically, given copies of an unknown trivial phase mixed state, our algorithm outputs a shallow local channel circuit that approximately generates this state in trace distance. The sample complexity and runtime are polynomial (or quasi-polynomial) in the number of qubits, assuming constant (or polylogarithmic) circuit depth and gate locality. Importantly, the learner is not given the original preparation circuit and relies only on its existence. Our results provide a structural foundation for quantum generative models based on shallow channel circuits. In the classical limit, our framework also inspires an efficient algorithm for classical diffusion models using only a polynomial overhead of training and generation.

</details>

### [186] [Stable algorithms cannot reliably find isolated perceptron solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00328)
*Shuyang Gong,Brice Huang,Shuangping Li,Mark Sellke*

Main category: cs.CC

TL;DR: 本文研究二元感知机（binary perceptron）模型中孤立解的算法可发现性问题，证明稳定算法无法可靠定位孤立解，成功概率上限为约0.84233。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二元感知机作为随机约束满足问题，存在一个显著特征：在任意正约束密度下，大部分解都是强孤立的（strongly isolated），即与其他解的海明距离（Hamming distance）为Ω(N)。然而，已知算法能在某些正约束密度下找到解，这引发了一个自然问题：孤立解是否能够被算法发现？

Method: 研究采用稳定性分析框架，考察在微小高斯重采样（tiny Gaussian resampling）下输出保持稳定的算法类别。证明方法不使用重叠间隙性质（overlap gap property），而是通过Pitt相关不等式（Pitt's correlation inequality）证明：在随机扰动后，靠近预存孤立解的解数量无法集中在1。

Result: 任何稳定算法可靠定位孤立解的成功概率上限为(3√17-9)/4+o_N(1)≤0.84233。此外，任何以1-o_N(1)概率找到解的稳定算法，找到孤立解的概率仅为o_N(1)。所考虑的稳定算法类别包括度数为D≤o(N/log N)的多项式算法。

Conclusion: 基于低度启发式（low-degree heuristic），定位强孤立解需要指数运行时间exp(Θ̃(N))。该结果揭示了算法发现孤立解的根本限制，为理解随机约束满足问题的算法复杂性提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study the binary perceptron, a random constraint satisfaction problem that asks to find a Boolean vector in the intersection of independently chosen random halfspaces. A striking feature of this model is that at every positive constraint density, it is expected that a $1-o_N(1)$ fraction of solutions are \emph{strongly isolated}, i.e. separated from all others by Hamming distance $Ω(N)$. At the same time, efficient algorithms are known to find solutions at certain positive constraint densities. This raises a natural question: can any isolated solution be algorithmically visible?
  We answer this in the negative: no algorithm whose output is stable under a tiny Gaussian resampling of the disorder can \emph{reliably} locate isolated solutions. We show that any stable algorithm has success probability at most $\frac{3\sqrt{17}-9}{4}+o_N(1)\leq 0.84233$. Furthermore, every stable algorithm that finds a solution with probability $1-o_N(1)$ finds an isolated solution with probability $o_N(1)$. The class of stable algorithms we consider includes degree-$D$ polynomials up to $D\leq o(N/\log N)$; under the low-degree heuristic \cite{hopkins2018statistical}, this suggests that locating strongly isolated solutions requires running time $\exp(\widetildeΘ(N))$.
  Our proof does not use the overlap gap property. Instead, we show via Pitt's correlation inequality that after a random perturbation of the disorder, the number of solutions located close to a pre-existing isolated solution cannot concentrate at $1$.

</details>

### [187] [The motion of tracer particles in turbulent superfluid $^4$He down to the zero-temperature limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00707)
*C. O. Goodwin,M. J. Doyle,J. A. Hay,I. Skachko,W. Guo,P. M. Walmsley,A. I. Golov*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 开发了一种用于超流氦-4流动可视化的聚合物颗粒注入系统，可观测颗粒在低温下的统计行为，包括与热激发和量子化涡旋线的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要开发一种能够在极低温（低至0.14 K）超流氦-4中可视化流动的系统，以研究颗粒与量子流体中热激发和量子化涡旋线的相互作用。

Method: 使用超声波换能器将直径1-6微米的荧光聚合物颗粒注入超流氦样品，通过激光片照明和荧光成像技术追踪颗粒轨迹，并开发了识别和量化结合在涡旋线上颗粒数量的方法。

Result: 观测到颗粒下降过程中平滑和随机轨迹的混合行为，测量了温度依赖的速度分布（呈现高斯分布和幂律尾部），发现小颗粒在近1 K温度下形成长寿命悬浮，与湍流涡旋缠结中的颗粒捕获相关。

Conclusion: 该系统成功实现了超流氦-4流动的可视化，揭示了颗粒与量子流体相互作用的复杂统计行为，并通过分析模型描述了结合在涡旋线上颗粒数量的时间动力学。

Abstract: An injection system for polymer particles, with diameters ranging from 1 to 6 $μ$m, has been developed for visualizing flows in superfluid $^4$He at temperatures down to 0.14 K. Using an ultrasound transducer, bursts of particles were launched into a sample of superfluid and allowed to descend under gravity. The particles were imaged using their fluorescence in the presence of a sheet of laser light. We report on the statistical behavior of particles during their descent, including descriptions of a mixture of smooth and erratic trajectories, indicative of the interactions with thermal excitations and quantized vortex lines. Temperature-dependent velocity distributions were measured and analyzed, yielding Gaussian distributions with power law tails persisting into the zero temperature limit. When sampled over increasing length scales, these distributions bifurcated into exponential for the smallest particles and bimodal Gaussian for the largest. We also report observations of long-lived suspensions of small particles at temperatures near 1 K, which appear to be associated with the trapping of large numbers of particles in a turbulent vortex tangle. A method was developed for identifying and quantifying the numbers of particles bound to vortex lines, allowing for a description of the temporal dynamics of their population by an analytical model.

</details>
